vana ākāraiḥ pradeśaiḥ upaśobhitam hima chattra mahā śṛṅgam prapāta śata nirjharam dṛṣṭvā eva tam cāru nitamba bhūmim mahā anubhāvaḥ sa tu madra nāthaḥ babhrāma tatra eva mudā sametaḥ sthānam tadā kiṃcid atha āsasāda Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca agamyam mānuṣaiḥ anyaiḥ daiva yogāt upāgataḥ airāvatī sarit śreṣṭhā yasmāt deśāt vinirgatā megha śyāmam ca tam deśam druma khaṇḍaiḥ anekaśas śālaiḥ tālaiḥ tamālaiḥ ca karṇikāraiḥ sa śāmalaiḥ nyagrodhaiḥ ca tathā aśvatthaiḥ śirīṣaiḥ śiṃśapa drumaiḥ śleṣmātakaiḥ āmalakaiḥ harītaka vibhītakaiḥ bhūrjaiḥ samuñjakaiḥ bāṇaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ saptacchada drumaiḥ devadāru mahāvṛkṣaiḥ tathā kāleyaka drumaiḥ mātāmra riṣṭaka akṣoṭaiḥ abdakaiḥ ca tathā arjunaiḥ hastikarṇaiḥ sumanasaiḥ kovidāraiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ prācīnāmalakaiḥ ca api dhanakaiḥ samarāṭakaiḥ kharjūraiḥ nārikelaiḥ ca priyāla āmrātaka iṅgudaiḥ tantumālaiḥ dhavaiḥ bhavyaiḥ kāśmīrī parṇibhiḥ tathā jātīphalaiḥ pūga phalaiḥ kaṭphala elā āvalī phalaiḥ mandāraiḥ kovidāraiḥ ca kiṃśukaiḥ kusuma aṃśukaiḥ rakta atiraṅga nāraṅgaiḥ hiṅgubhiḥ sa priyaṅgubhiḥ raktāśokaiḥ tathā aśokaiḥ ākallaiḥ avicārakaiḥ mucukundaiḥ tathā kundaiḥ āṭarūṣa parūṣakaiḥ kirātaiḥ kiṅkirātaiḥ ca ketakaiḥ śveta ketakaiḥ śobhāñjanaiḥ añjanaiḥ ca su kaliṅga nikoṭakaiḥ drumaśreṣṭhaiḥ tathā asanaiḥ pīta yūthikayā ca eva śveta yūthikayā tathā jātyā campaka jātyā ca tumbaraiḥ ca api atumbaraiḥ tathā supuṣpa āvaraṇaiḥ cavyakaiḥ kāmivallabhaiḥ puṣpa aṅkuraiḥ ca bakulaiḥ pāribhadra haridrakaiḥ dhārākadambaiḥ kuṭajaiḥ kadambaiḥ girikuṭajaiḥ ādityamustakaiḥ kumbhaiḥ kuṅkumaiḥ kāmavallabhaiḥ raktaiḥ pālī vanaiḥ śvetaiḥ dāḍimaiḥ campaka drumaiḥ bandhūkaiḥ ca subandhūkaiḥ kuñjakānām tu jātibhiḥ kusumaiḥ pāṭalābhiḥ ca mallikā karavīrakaiḥ bījapūraiḥ sa karpūraiḥ gurubhiḥ ca aguru drumaiḥ tathā guggula vṛkṣaiḥ ca hintāla dhavala ikṣubhiḥ tṛṇaśūnyaiḥ karavīraiḥ aśokaiḥ cakramardanaiḥ pīlubhiḥ dhātakībhiḥ ca ciribilvaiḥ samākulaiḥ tintiḍīkaiḥ tathā lodhraiḥ viḍaṅgaiḥ kṣīrikā drumaiḥ aśmantakaiḥ tathā kālaiḥ jambīraiḥ śvaitaka drumaiḥ karamardaiḥ kāsamardaiḥ ariṣṭaka variṣṭakaiḥ rudrākṣaiḥ drākṣa sambhūtaiḥ sapta āhvaiḥ putrajīvakaiḥ kaṅkolakaiḥ lavaṅgaiḥ ca tvagdrumaiḥ pārijātakaiḥ pratānaiḥ pippalīnām ca nāgavalyaḥ ca bhāgaśas mṛdvīkā maṇḍapaiḥ mukhyaiḥ atimuktaka maṇḍapaiḥ trapuṣaiḥ nartikānām ca pratānaiḥ sa phalaiḥ śubhaiḥ kūṣmāṇḍānām pratānaiḥ ca alābūnām tathā kvacid cirbhiṭasya pratānaiḥ ca paṭolī kāravellakaiḥ karkoṭakī vitānaiḥ ca vārtākaiḥ bṛhatī phalaiḥ kaṇṭakaiḥ mūlakaiḥ mūla śākaiḥ tu vividhaiḥ tathā kahlāraiḥ ca vidāryā ca rurūṭaiḥ svādukaṇṭakaiḥ sa bhāṇḍīra vidūsāra rājajambūka vālukaiḥ kākolī kṣīrakākolī chattrayā ca ati chatrayā kāsamardī saha āsadbhiḥ sa kandala sa kāṇḍakaiḥ tathā kṣīraka śākena kālaśākena ca api atha śimbī dhānyaiḥ tathā dhānyaiḥ sarvaiḥ niravaśeṣataḥ auṣadhībhiḥ vicitrābhiḥ dīpyamānābhiḥ eva ca āyuṣyābhiḥ yaśasyābhiḥ balyābhiḥ ca narādhipa saubhāgya jananībhiḥ ca kutsnābhiḥ ca api anekaśas tatra veṇu latābhiḥ ca tathā kīcaka veṇubhiḥ kāśaiḥ śaśāṅka kāśaiḥ ca śara gulmaiḥ tathā eva ca tathā marakata prakhyaiḥ pradeśaiḥ śādvala anvitaiḥ irā puṃṣpa samāyuktaiḥ kuṅkamasya ca bhāgaśas tagara ativiṣā māṃsī granthikaiḥ tu surā gadaiḥ suvarṇa puṣpaiḥ ca tathā bhūmi puṣpaiḥ tathā aparaiḥ jambīrakaiḥ bhūstṛṇakaiḥ sa rasaiḥ sa śukaiḥ tathā śaṅgavera ajamodābhiḥ kuberaka priyālakaiḥ jala jaiḥ ca tathā vaṇaiḥ nānā varṇaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ udaya āditya saṃkāśaiḥ sūrya candra nibhaiḥ tathā tapanīya savarṇaiḥ ca atasī puṣpa saṃnibhaiḥ śūkapattra nibhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ sthala pattraiḥ ca bhāgaśas pañca varṇaiḥ samākīrṇaiḥ bahu varṇaiḥ tathā eva ca draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭyā hita mudaiḥ kumudaiḥ candra saṃnibhaiḥ tathā vahniśikhā ākāraiḥ gaja vaktra utpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ śṛṅgāṭaka mṛṇālaiḥ ca rājata utpalaiḥ jala jaiḥ sthala jaiḥ mūlaiḥ phalaiḥ puṣpaiḥ viśeṣataḥ madra īśvaraḥ sa dadṛśe tapasā hi atiyogataḥ dadṛśe ca tathā tatra nānā rūpān patatriṇaḥ mayūrān śatapattrān ca kalaviṅkān ca kokilān tathā kādambakān haṃsān koyaṣṭīn khañjarīṭakān kurarān kālakūṭān ca khaṭvāṅgān lubdhakān tathā gokṣveḍakān tathā kumbhān dhārtarāṣṭrān śukān bakān ghātukān cakravākān ca kaṭukān ṭiṭṭibhān bhaṭān pārāvatān ca kamalān sārikāḥ jīvajīvakān tāmracūḍān svarṇacūḍān kukkuṭān kāṣṭhakukkuṭān kapiñjalān kalaviṅkān tathā kuṅkumacūḍakān bhṛṅgarājān sīrapādān bhūliṅgān ḍiṇḍimān navān mañjulītaka dātyūhān bhāradvājān tathā caṣān etān ca anyān ca su bahūn pakṣi saṃghān manoharān śvāpadān vividha ākārān mṛgān ca eva mahāmṛgān vyāghrān kesariṇaḥ siṃhān dvīpinaḥ śarabhān vṛkān ṛkṣān tarakṣūn ca bahūn golāṅgūlān sa vānarān śaśalomān sa kādambān mārjārān vāyu veginaḥ mūṣakān nakulān kāvān siṃhān druma manoharān tathā mattān ca mātaṃgān mahiṣān gavayān vṛṣān camarān sṛmarān ca eva tathā gaurakharān api urabhrān ca tathā meṣān sāraṅgān atha kūkurān nīlān ca eva mahā nālān karālān mṛgamātṛkān krauñca ākāraka śambarān karālān kṛtamālān ca kālapucchān ca toraṇān daṃṣṭrān khaḍgān varāhān ca turaṃgān khara gardabhān etān adviṣṭān madra īśaḥ viruddhān ca parasparam aviruddhān vane dṛṣṭvā vismayam paramam yayau tat ca āśrama padam puṇyam babhūva atreḥ purā nṛpam kravyādāḥ prāṇinaḥ tatra sarve kṣīra phala aśanāḥ nirmitāḥ tatra ca atyartham atriṇā su mahātmanā śailā nitamba deśeṣu nyavasat ca svayam nṛpaḥ payaḥ kṣaranti te divyam amṛta svādu kaṇṭakam kvacid rājan mahiṣyaḥ ca kvacid ājāḥ ca sarvaśas śilāḥ kṣīreṇa sampūrṇāḥ dadhnā ca anyatra vā bahis saṃpaśyan paramām prītim avāpa vasudhādhipaḥ sarāṃsi tatra divyāni nadyaḥ ca vimala udakāḥ praṇālikāni ca uṣṇāni śītalāni ca bhāgaśas tatra asti rājan śikharam parvata indrasya pāṇḍuram hima pātam ghanāḥ yatra kurvanti sahitāḥ sadā tatra asti ca aparam śṛṅgam yatra toya ghanāḥ ghanāḥ nityam eva abhivarṣanti śilābhiḥ śikharam varam tat āśramam manohāri yatra kāma dharā dharā sura mukhya upayogi tvāt śākhinām saphalāḥ phalāḥ vānaraiḥ krīḍamānaiḥ ca deśāt deśāt narādhipa hima puñjāḥ kṛtāḥ tatra candra bimba sama prabhāḥ śaila vāṭaiḥ parivṛtam agamyam manujaiḥ sadā pūrva ārādhita bhāvaḥ asau mahā rājaḥ purūravāḥ tad āśrama padam prāptaḥ devadeva prasādataḥ tat āśramam śrama śamanam manoharam manoharaiḥ kusuma śataiḥ alaṃkṛtam kṛtam svayam ruciram atha atriṇā śubham śubha āvaham ca hi dadṛśe sa madra rāj Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca tatra yau tau mahā śṛṅgau mahā varṇau mahā himau nitya atapta śilā jātam sadā abhra parivarjitam tasya adhastāt vṛkṣa gaṇe diśām bhāge ca paścime jātī latā parikṣiptam vivaram cāru darśanam dṛṣṭvā eva kautuka āviṣṭaḥ tam viveśa mahīpatiḥ tamasā ca ati nibiḍam nalva mātram su saṃkaṭam tathā api divasa ākāram prakāśam tat aharniśam krośa adhika parīmāṇam sarasā ca virājitam nānā māṇikya kusumaiḥ suprabha ābharaṇa ujjvalaiḥ karṇikāḥ ca tathā teṣām jātarūpasya pārthiva nānā ratnaiḥ upacitāḥ jalajānām samāśrayaḥ kapardikānām śuktīnām śaṅkhānām ca mahīpate makarāṇām ca matsyānām caṇḍānām kacchapaiḥ saha tatra marakata khaṇḍāni vajrāṇām ca sahasraśas padmarāga indranīlāni mahānīlāni pārthiva puṣparāgāṇi sarvāṇi tathā karkoṭakāni ca tutthakasya tu khaṇḍāni tathā śeṣasya bhāgaśas sūrya indukāntayaḥ ca eva nīlaḥ varṇa antimaḥ ca yaḥ sura uraga valakṣāṇām sphaṭikasya tathā eva ca vaiḍūrya saugandhikayoḥ tathā rāja maṇeḥ nṛpa muktāphalāni muktānām tārā vigraha dhāriṇām sukha uṣṇam ca eva tat toyam snānāt śīta vināśanam vaiḍūryasya śilā madhye sarasaḥ tasya śobhanā pramāṇena tathā sā ca dve ca rājan dhanuḥ śate caturasrā tathā ramyā tapasā nirmitā atriṇā tathā puṣkariṇī ramyā tasmin rājan śilā tale su śīta amala pānīyā jalajaiḥ ca virājitā ākāśa pratimā rājan catur asrā manoharā na kṣiṇoti yathā kaṇṭham kukṣim na āpūrayati api tṛptim vidhatte paramām śarīre ca mahat sukham madhye tu tasyāḥ prāsādam nirmitam tapasā atriṇā śaśāṅka raśmeḥ saṃkāśam prāsādam rājatam hitam ramya vaiḍūrya sopānam vidruma āmalasārakam vajra aṃśu jālaiḥ sphuritam ramyam dṛṣṭi manoramam bhogi bhoga āvalī suptaḥ sarva alaṃkāra bhūṣitaḥ phaṇīndra saṃniviṣṭaḥ aṅghriḥ dvitīyaḥ ca tathā anagha lakṣa yudh saṅga gataḥ aṅghriḥ tu śeṣa bhoga praśāyinaḥ phaṇi indra bhoga saṃnyasta bāhuḥ keyūra bhūṣaṇaḥ aṅgulī pṛṣṭha vinyasta deva śīrṣa dharam bhujam kiṃcid ākuñcitam ca eva nābhi deśa kara sthitam tṛtīyam tu bhujam tasya caturtham tu tathā śṛṇu ātta saṃtāna kusumam ghrāṇa deśa anusarpiṇam lakṣmyā saṃvāhyamāna aṅghriḥ padma pattra nibhaiḥ karaiḥ saṃtāna mālā mukuṭam hāra keyūra bhūṣitam bhūṣitam ca tathā devam aṅgadaiḥ aṅgulīyakaiḥ ajñāta vastu caritam pratiṣṭhitam atha atriṇā siddha anupūjyam satatam saṃtāna kusuma arcitam śobhita uttama pārśvam tam devam utpala śīrṣakam jānubhyām śirasā ca eva gatvā bhūmim yathāvidhi nāmnām sahasreṇa tadā tuṣṭāva madhusūdanam pradakṣiṇam atho cakre sa tu utthāya punar punar ramyam āyatanam dṛṣṭvā tatra uvāsa āśrame punar bilāt bahis guhām kāṃcid āśritya su manoharām nānāvidhaiḥ tathā puṣpaiḥ phala mūlaiḥ sa gorasaiḥ nityam triṣavaṇa snāyī vahni pūjā parāyaṇaḥ deva vāpī jalaiḥ kurvan satatam prāṇadhāraṇam sarva āhāra parityāgam kṛtvā tu manuja īśvaraḥ an āstṛta guhā śāyī kālam nayati pārthivaḥ tyakta āhāra kriyaḥ ca eva kevalam toyataḥ nṛpaḥ na tasya glānim āyāti śarīram ca tat adbhutam Purāṇa krīḍā vihāram gandharvaiḥ paśyan apsarasām saha kṛtvā puṣpa uccayam bhūri granthayitvā tathā srajaḥ puṣpa uccaya prasaktānām krīḍantīnām yathāsukham ceṣṭāḥ nānāvidha ākārāḥ paśyan api na paśyati kācid puṣpa uccaye saktā latā jālena veṣṭitā sakhī janena saṃtyaktā kāntena abhisamujjhitā kācid kamala gandha ābhā niḥśvāsa pavana āhṛtaiḥ makaranda sabhā ākrānta nayanā kācid aṅganā kānta niḥśvāsa vātena nīrajaska kṛta īkṣaṇā kācid uccīya puṣpāṇi dadau kāntasya bhāminī kānta saṃgrathitaiḥ puṣpaiḥ rarāja kṛta śekharā kṛtakṛtyam iva ātmānam mene manmatha vardhinī astu asmin gahane kuñje viśiṣṭa kusumā latā kācid evam rahaḥ nītā ramaṇena riraṃsunā kānta saṃnāmita latā kusumāni vicinvatī sarvābhyaḥ kācid ātmānam mene sarva guṇa adhikam kāścid paśyati bhūpālam nalinīṣu pṛthak pṛthak krīḍamānāḥ tu gandharvaiḥ deva rāmāḥ manoramāḥ kācid ātāḍayat kāntam udakena śuci smitā tāḍyamānā atha kāntena prītim kācid upāyayau kāntam ca tāḍayāmāsa jāta khedā vara aṅganā adṛśyata varārohā śvāsa nṛtyat payodharā kānta ambu tāḍana ākṛṣṭa keśa pāśa nibandhanā sva cakṣuḥ sadṛśaiḥ puṣpaiḥ saṃchanne nalinī vane channā kācid cirāt prāptā kāntena anviṣya yatnataḥ snātā śīta apadeśena kācid prāha aṅganā bhṛśam ramaṇa āliṅganam cakre manaḥ abhilaṣitam ciram jala ārdra vasanam sūkṣmam aṅga līnam śuci smitā kaṇṭha mālya guṇaiḥ kācid kāntena kṛṣyatā ambhasi kācid bhugnā sakhī datta jānu deśe nakha kṣatā saṃbhrāntā kānta śaraṇam magnā kācid gatā ciram kācid pṛṣṭha kṛtā ādityā keśa nistoya kāriṇī śilā tala gatā bhartrā dṛṣṭā kāma ārta cakṣuṣā kṛtta mālyam vilulitam saṃkrānta kuca kuṅkumam pūjyamānam ca dadṛśe devadevam janārdanam kvacid ca dadṛśe rājā latā gṛha gatāḥ striyaḥ maṇḍayantīḥ sva gātrāṇi kānta saṃnyasta mānasāḥ kācid ādarśana karā vyagrā dūtī mukha udgatam śṛṇvatī kānta vacanam adhikā tu tathā babhau kācid sa tvaritā dūtyā bhūṣaṇānām viparyayam kurvāṇā nā eva bubudhe manmatha āviṣṭa cetanā kācid pibantī dadṛśe maireyam nīla śādvale pāyayāmāsa ramaṇam svayam kācid vara aṅganā kācid papau varārohā kānta pāṇi samarpitam tathā viditvā mugdha tvāt babhūva vrīḍitā bhṛśam kācid kānta arpitam subhrūḥ kānta pīta avaśeṣitam āpāna goṣṭhīṣu tathā tāsām sa nara puṃgavaḥ śuśrāva vividham gītam tantrī svara vimiśritam rājan sadā upanṛtyanti nānā vādya puraḥsarāḥ āvasan saṃyutāḥ kāntaiḥ para ṛddhi racitām guhām nānā gandha anvita latām nānā gandha sugandhinīm nānā vicitra śayanām kusuma utkara maṇḍitām evam apsarasām paśyan krīḍitāni sa parvate tapaḥ tepe mahā rājan keśava arpita mānasaḥ tam ūcuḥ nṛpatim gatvā gandharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ vayam hi te pradāsyāmaḥ manasaḥ kāṅkṣitān varān tān ādāya gṛham gaccha tiṣṭha iha yadi vā punar rājā uvāca varam vitarata adya eva prasādam madhusūdanāt evam astu iti athā uktaḥ taiḥ sa tu rājā purūravāḥ tatra uvāsa sukhī māsam pūjayānaḥ janārdanam priyaḥ eva sadā eva āsīt gandharva apsarasām nṛpaḥ tutoṣa sa janaḥ rājñaḥ tasya a laulyena karmaṇā toya aśanaḥ tatra hi uvāsa māsam yāvat sita antaḥ nṛpa phālgunasya phālguna amala pakṣa ante rājā svapne purūravāḥ rātryām asyām vyatītāyām atriṇā tvam sameṣyasi svapnam evam sa rājarṣiḥ dṛṣṭvā deva indra vikramaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ yathākāmam pūjayitvā janārdanam dadarśa atrim munim rājā pratyakṣam tapasām nidhim tatas śuśrāva vacanam devatānām samīritam evam etat mahīpāla na atra kāryā vicāraṇā evam prasādam samprāpya devadevāt janārdanāt kṛta deva arcanaḥ rājā tathā huta hutāśanaḥ sarvān kāmān avāptaḥ asau vara dānena keśavāt Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca nānā ratna mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ kalpadruma samanvitaiḥ madhye himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe kailāsaḥ nāma parvataḥ kailāsa pāda sambhūtam puṇyam śīta jalam śubham tasmāt pravahate divyā nadī mandākinī śubhā yakṣa senāpatiḥ krūraḥ guhyakaiḥ parivāritaḥ puṇyā mandākinī nāma nadī hi acchodakā śubhā kailāsa dakṣiṇe prācyām śivam sarva oṣadhim girim manaḥśilā mayam divyam suvelam parvatam prati lohitaḥ hemaśṛṅgaḥ tu giriḥ sūrya prabhaḥ mahān divya araṇyam viśokam ca tasya tīre mahat vanam kailāsāt paścima udīcyām kakudmān auṣadhī giriḥ tasmāt prabhavate puṇyā sarayūḥ loka pāvanī yasyāḥ tīre vanam divyam vaibhrājam nāma viśrutam kailāsāt paścimām āśām divyaḥ sarva oṣadhi giriḥ varuṇaḥ parvata śreṣṭhaḥ rukma dhātu vibhūṣitaḥ śātakaumbha mayaiḥ divyaiḥ śilā jālaiḥ samācitaḥ śata saṅkhyaiḥ tāpanīyaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ divam iva ullikhan śṛṅgavān su mahā divyaḥ durgaḥ śailaḥ mahā citaḥ tasya pādāt prabhavati śailodam nāma tat saraḥ tasmāt prabhavate puṇyā nadī śailodakā śubhā sā tayoḥ madhye praviṣṭā paścima udadhim gauram tu parvata śreṣṭham haritāla mayam prati hiraṇyaśṛṅgaḥ su mahā d-ivya oṣadhi mayaḥ giriḥ tasya pāde mahat divyam saraḥ kāñcana vālukam ramyam bindusaraḥ nāma yatra rājā bhagīrathaḥ gaṅgā arthe sa tu rājarṣiḥ uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ divam yāsyantu me pūrve gaṅgā toya āpluta asthikāḥ soma pādāt prasūtā sā saptadhā pravibhajyate yūpāḥ maṇi mayāḥ tatra vimānāḥ ca hiraṇmayāḥ tatra iṣṭvā kratubhiḥ siddhaḥ śakraḥ sura gaṇaiḥ saha divyaḥ chāyāpathaḥ tatra nakṣatrāṇām tu maṇḍalam dṛśyate bhāsurā rātrau devī tripathagā tu sā antarikṣam divam ca eva bhāvayitvā bhuvam gatā bhava uttamāṅge patitā saṃruddhā yoga māyayā tatas tasyāḥ niruddhāyāḥ bhavena sahasā ruṣā jñātvā tasyāḥ hi abhiprāyam krūram devyāḥ cikīrṣitam bhittvā viśāmi pātālam srotasā gṛhya śaṃkaram atha avalepam tam jñātvā tasyāḥ kruddhaḥ tu śaṃkaraḥ tirobhāvayitum buddhiḥ āsīt aṅgeṣu tām nadīm etasmin eva kāle tu dṛṣṭvā rājānam agratas dhamanī saṃtatam kṣīṇam kṣudhā vyākulita indriyam brahmaṇaḥ vacanam śrutvā yat uktam dhārayan nadīm tatas visarjayāmāsa saṃruddhām svena tejasā nadīm bhagīrathasya arthe tapasā ugreṇa toṣitaḥ tatas visarjayāmāsa sapta srotāṃsi gaṅgayā trīṇi prācīm abhimukham pratīcīm trīṇi atha eva tu nalinī hlādinī ca eva pāvanī ca eva prācya gā sītā cakṣuḥ ca sindhuḥ ca tisraḥ tāḥ vai pratīcya gāḥ saptamī tu anugā tāsām dakṣiṇena bhagīratham tasmāt bhāgīrathī sā vai praviṣṭā dakṣiṇa udadhim prasūtāḥ sapta nadyaḥ tu śubhāḥ bindusarā udbhavāḥ tān deśān plāvayanti sma mleccha prāyān ca sarvaśas sa śailān kukurān raudhrān barbarān yavanān khasān pulikān ca kulatthān ca aṅga lokyān varān ca yān kṛtvā dvidhā himavantam praviṣṭāḥ dakṣiṇa udadhim atha vīra marūn ca eva kālikān ca eva śūlikān tukarān barbara ākārān pahlavān pāradān śakān etān janapadān cakṣuḥ plāvayitvā udadhim gatā daradoḥ jaguḍān ca eva gāndhārān aurasān kuhūn śunāmukhān ca ūrda marūn sindhuḥ etān niṣevate gandharvān kinnarān yakṣān rakṣaḥ vidyādhara uragān kalāpa grāmakān ca eva tathā kimpuruṣān narān kirātān ca pulindān ca kurūn vai bhāratān api pāñcālān kauśikān matsyān māgadha aṅgān tathā eva ca brahma uttarān ca vaṅgān ca tāmraliptān tathā eva ca etān janapadān āryān gaṅgā bhāvayate śubhā tatas pratihatāḥ vindhye praviṣṭāḥ dakṣiṇa udadhim tatas tu hlādinī puṇyā prācīna abhimukhī yayau plāvayanti upakān ca eva niṣādān api sarvaśas dhīvarān ṛṣikān ca eva tathā nali mukhān api kekarān eka karṇān ca kirātān api ca eva hi kālañjarān vikarṇān ca kuśikān svargabhaumakān sā maṇḍale samudrasya tīre bhūtvā tu sarvaśas tatas tu nalinī ca api prācīm eva diśam yayau tathā khara pathān deśān vetra śaṅku pathān api indradvīpa samīpe tu praviṣṭāḥ lavaṇa udadhim tatas tu pāvanī prāyāt prācīm āśām javena tu tomarān plāvayatī ca haṃsa mārgān samūhakān pūrvān deśān ca sevantī bhittvā sā bahudhā girim karṇa prāvaraṇān prāpya gatā sa aśva mukhān api siktvā parvata merum sā gatvā vidyādharān api śaimi maṇḍala koṣṭham tu sā praviṣṭā mahat saraḥ tāsām nadī upanadyaḥ anyāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tīre vaṃśaukasārāyāḥ surabhiḥ nāma tat vanam hiraṇya śṛṅgaḥ vasati vidvān kauberakaḥ vaśī yajñāt apetaḥ su mahān amita ojāḥ su vikramaḥ tatra agastyaiḥ parivṛtāḥ vidvabhiḥ dbrahmarākṣasaiḥ kubera anucarāḥ hi ete catvāraḥ tad samāśritāḥ paraspareṇa dviguṇāḥ dharmataḥ kāmataḥ arthataḥ hemakūṭasya pṛṣṭhe tu sarpāṇām tat saraḥ smṛtam jambūḥ ca eva nadī puṇyā yasyām jāmbūnadam smṛtam payodaḥ tu hradaḥ nīlaḥ sa śubhraḥ puṇḍarīkavān puṇḍarīkāt payaḥ dāt ca tasmāt dve samprasūyatām mṛgyā ca mṛgakāntā ca tasmāt dve hradāḥ kuruṣu vikhyātāḥ padma mīna kula ākulāḥ nāmnā te vai jayāḥ nāma dvādaśa udadhi saṃnibhāḥ tebhyaḥ śāntī ca madhvī ca dve nadyau samprasūyatām kimpuruṣa ādyāni yāni aṣṭau teṣu devaḥ na varṣati viniviṣṭāḥ pratidiśam nimagnāḥ lavaṇa ambudhim candrakāntaḥ tathā droṇaḥ su mahān ca śiloccayaḥ udgāyatā udīcyām tu avagāḍhāḥ mahā udadhim pratīcīm āyatāḥ te vai pratiṣṭhāḥ te mahā udadhim jīmūtaḥ drāvaṇaḥ ca eva mainākaḥ candraparvataḥ āyatāḥ te mahā śailāḥ samudram dakṣiṇam prati iti ete parvata āviṣṭāḥ catvāraḥ lavaṇa udadhim chidyamāneṣu pakṣeṣu purā indrasya vai bhayāt teṣām tu dṛśyate candre śukle kṛṣṇe samāplutiḥ te bhāratasya varṣasya bhedāḥ yena prakīrtitāḥ uttarottaram eteṣām varṣam udricyate guṇaiḥ ārogya āyuḥ pramāṇābhyām dharmataḥ kāmataḥ arthataḥ samanvitāni bhūtāni teṣu varṣeṣu bhāgaśas vasanti nānā jātīni teṣu sarveṣu tāni vai iti etat dhārayat viśvam pṛthvī jagat idam sthitā Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca śākadvīpasya vakṣyāmi yathāvat iha niścayam kathyamānam nibodha tvam śākam dvīpam dvijottamāḥ vistārāt triguṇaḥ ca api pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ tena āvṛtaḥ samudraḥ ayam dvīpena lavaṇa udadhiḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cirāt ca mriyate janaḥ tatra api parvatāḥ śubhrāḥ sapta eva maṇi bhūṣitāḥ śākadvīpa ādiṣu tu eṣu sapta sapta nagāḥ triṣu ṛju āyatāḥ pratidiśam niviṣṭāḥ varṣaparvatāḥ ratnākara ādi nāmānaḥ sānumantaḥ mahā citāḥ sama uditāḥ pratidiśam dvīpa vistāra mānataḥ ubhayatra avagāḍhau ca lavaṇa kṣīra sāgarau śākadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi sapta divyān mahā acalān prāc āyataḥ sa sauvarṇaḥ udayaḥ nāma parvataḥ tasya apareṇa su mahān jaladhāraḥ mahā giriḥ tasya apareṇa su mahān śyāmaḥ nāma mahā giriḥ yatra śyāma tvam āpannāḥ prajāḥ pūrvam imāḥ kila śabda mṛtyuḥ purā tasmin dundubhiḥ tāḍitaḥ suraiḥ ratna mālā antara mayaḥ śālmalaḥ ca antarāla kṛt tasya apareṇa rajataḥ mahān astaḥ giriḥ smṛtaḥ saṃbhṛtam ca hṛtam ca eva mātuḥ arthe garutmatā tasya apare ca āmbikeyaḥ sumanāḥ ca eva sa smṛtaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ varāheṇa tasmin śaile niṣūditaḥ āmbikeyāt paraḥ ramyaḥ sarva oṣadhi niṣevitaḥ vibhrājaḥ tu samākhyātaḥ sphāṭikaḥ tu mahān giriḥ teṣām varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi parvatānām dvijottamāḥ śṛṇudhvam nāmataḥ tāni yathāvat anupūrvaśas dvi nāmāni eva varṣāṇi yathā eva girayaḥ tathā nāmnā gatabhayam nāma varṣam tat prathamam smṛtam tat eva śaiśiram nāma varṣam tat parikīrtitam śyāma parvata varṣam tat anīcakam iti smṛtam tat eva asitam iti uktam varṣam somaka saṃjñitam āmbikeyasya mainākam kṣemakam ca eva tat kṛtam śākaḥ nāma mahā vṛkṣaḥ prajāḥ tasya mahā anugāḥ eteṣu deva gandharvāḥ siddhāḥ ca saha cāraṇaiḥ viharanti ramante ca dṛśyamānāḥ ca taiḥ saha tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cāturvarṇya samanvitāḥ dvi nāmnā ca eva tāḥ sarvāḥ gaṅgāḥ saptavidhāḥ smṛtāḥ prathamā sukumārī iti gaṅgā śiva jalā śubhā munitaptā ca nāmnā eṣā nadī samparikīrtitā sukumārī tapaḥsiddhā dvitīyā nāmataḥ satī nandā ca pāvanī ca eva tṛtīyā parikīrtitā śibikā ca caturthī syāt dvividhā ca punar smṛtā ikṣuḥ ca pañcamī jñeyā tathā eva ca punar kuhūḥ veṇukā ca amṛtā ca eva ṣaṣṭhī samparikīrtitā sukṛtā ca gabhastī ca saptamī parikīrtitā etāḥ sapta mahābhāgāḥ prativarṣam śiva udakāḥ bhāvayanti janam sarvam śākadvīpa nivāsinam abhigacchanti tāḥ ca anyāḥ nadāḥ nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca bahu udaka parisrāvāḥ yatas varṣati vāsavaḥ tāsām tu nāmadheyāni parimāṇam tathā eva ca na śakyam parisaṃkhyātum puṇyāḥ tāḥ sarit uttamāḥ tāḥ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭāḥ nadīḥ janapadāḥ tu te ete śānta bhayāḥ proktāḥ pramodāḥ ye ca vai śivāḥ ānandāḥ ca sukhāḥ ca eva kṣemakāḥ ca navaiḥ saha varṇa āśrama ācāra yutāḥ deśāḥ te sapta viśrutāḥ ārogyāḥ balinaḥ ca eva sarve maraṇa varjitāḥ śākadvīpa ādiṣu jñeyam pañcasu eteṣu sarvaśas deśasya tu vicāreṇa kālaḥ svābhāvikaḥ smṛtaḥ na teṣu saṃkaraḥ kaścid varṇa āśrama kṛtaḥ kvacid dharmasya ca avyabhīcārāt ekānta sukhinaḥ prajāḥ na teṣu māyā lobhaḥ vai īrṣyā asūyā bhayam kutas kālaḥ nā eva ca teṣu asti na daṇḍaḥ na ca dāṇḍikaḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ tu su mahān dvīpaḥ vai kuśa saṃjñakaḥ nadī jalaiḥ parivṛtaḥ parvataḥ ca abhra saṃnibhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpa phala upetaiḥ sarvatas dhana dhānyavān nityam puṣpa phala upetaḥ sarva ratna samāvṛtaḥ āvṛtaḥ paśubhiḥ sarvaiḥ grāmya āraṇyaiḥ ca sarvaśas ānupūrvyāt samāsena kuśadvīpam nibodhata atha tṛtīyam vakṣyāmi kuśadvīpam ca kṛtsnaśas kuśadvīpena kṣīrodaḥ sarvatas parivāritaḥ śākadvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇena samanvitaḥ tatra api parvatāḥ sapta vijñeyāḥ ratna yonayaḥ ratna ākarāḥ tathā nadyaḥ teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu dvi nāmānaḥ ca te sarve śākadvīpe yathā tathā prathamaḥ sūrya saṃkāśaḥ kumudaḥ nāma parvataḥ sarva dhātu mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ śilā jāla samanvitaiḥ haritāla mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ dvīpam āvṛtya sarvaśas balāhakaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu jāti añjana mayaḥ giriḥ dyutimān nāmataḥ proktaḥ saḥ eva ca mahīdharaḥ viśalya karaṇī ca eva mṛtasaṃjīvanī tathā puṣpavān nāma saḥ eva uktaḥ parvataḥ su mahā citaḥ kaṅkaḥ tu pañcamaḥ teṣām parvataḥ nāma sāravān kuśeśayaḥ iti proktaḥ punar sa pṛthivīdharaḥ mandaraḥ sa eva vijñeyaḥ sarva dhātu mayaḥ śubhaḥ mandaḥ iti eṣa yaḥ dhātuḥ apām arthe prakāśakaḥ apām vidāraṇāt ca eva mandaraḥ sa nigadyate tatra ratnāni anekāni svayam rakṣati vāsavaḥ teṣām antara viṣkambhaḥ dviguṇaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ iti ete parvatāḥ sapta kuśadvīpe prabhāṣitāḥ teṣām varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi sapta eva tu vibhāgaśaḥ kumudasya smṛtaḥ śvetaḥ unnataḥ ca iva sa smṛtaḥ unnatasya tu vijñeyam varṣam lohita saṃjñakam balāhakasya jīmūtaḥ svairatha ākāram iti api droṇasya harikam nāma lavaṇam ca punar smṛtam mahiṣam mahiṣasya api punar ca api prabhākaram etāni api viśiṣṭāni sapta sapta pṛthak pṛthak varṣāṇi parvatāḥ ca eva nadīḥ teṣu nibodhata tatra api nadyaḥ sapta eva prativarṣam hi tāḥ smṛtāḥ dvi nāmavatyaḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāḥ puṇya jalāḥ smṛtāḥ dhūtapāpā nadī nāma yoniḥ ca eva punar smṛtā sītā dvitīyā vijñeyā sā ca eva hi niśā smṛtā pavitrā tṛtīyā vijñeyā vitṛṣṇā api ca yā punar caturthī hlādinī iti uktā candrabhā iti ca smṛtā puṇḍrā ṣaṣṭhī tu vijñeyā punar ca eva vibhāvarī mahatī saptamī proktā punar ca eṣā dhṛtiḥ smṛtā anyāḥ tābhyaḥ api saṃjātāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas iti eṣa saṃniveśaḥ vaḥ kuśadvīpasya varṇitaḥ śākadvīpena vistāraḥ proktaḥ tasya sanātanaḥ kuśadvīpaḥ samudreṇa ghṛtamaṇḍa udakena ca sarvatas su mahān dvīpaḥ candra vat pariveṣṭitaḥ vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca eva kṣīrodāt dviguṇaḥ mataḥ tatas param pravakṣyāmi krauñcadvīpam yathā tathā ghṛta udakaḥ samudraḥ vai krauñca dvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ cakranemi pramāṇena vṛtaḥ vṛttena sarvaśas tasmin dvīpe nagāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ devanaḥ giriḥ ucyate krauñcāt pare pāvanakaḥ pāvanāt andhakārakaḥ andhakārāt pare ca api devāvṛt nāma parvataḥ devāvṛtaḥ pareṇa api puṇḍarīkaḥ mahān giriḥ varṣāṇi tasya vakṣyāmi nāmataḥ tu nibodhata manonugāt pare ca uṣṇāḥ tṛtīyaḥ api saḥ ucyate uṣṇāt pare pāvanakaḥ pāvanāt andhakārakaḥ andhakāraka deśāt tu munideśaḥ tathā paraḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃkīrṇaḥ gaura prāyaḥ śuciḥ janaḥ śrutāḥ tatra eva nadyaḥ tu prativarṣam gatāḥ śubhāḥ gaurī kumudvatī ca eva saṃdhyā rātriḥ manojavā khyātī ca puṇḍarīkā ca gaṅgā saptavidhā smṛtā tāsām sahasraśas ca anyāḥ nadyaḥ pārśva samīpa gāḥ abhigacchanti tāḥ nadyaḥ bahulāḥ ca bahu udakāḥ teṣām nisargaḥ deśānām ānupūrvyeṇa sarvaśas sargaḥ yaḥ ca prajānām tu saṃhāraḥ yaḥ ca teṣu vai atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi śālmalasya nibodhata śālmalaḥ dviguṇaḥ dvīpaḥ krauñcadvīpasya vistarāt tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cirāt ca mriyate janaḥ prathamaḥ sūrya saṃkāśaḥ sumanāḥ nāma parvataḥ tṛtīyaḥ ca eva sauvarṇaḥ bhṛṅga pattra nibhaḥ giriḥ sumanāḥ kuśalaḥ deśaḥ sukha udarkaḥ sukha udayaḥ rohitaḥ yaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu rohiṇaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ tatra ratnāni anekāni svayam rakṣati vāsavaḥ na tatra meghāḥ varṣanti śīta uṣṇam ca na tadvidham varṇa āśramāṇām vārttā vā triṣu dvīpeṣu vidyate na grahaḥ na ca candraḥ asti īrṣyā asūyā bhayam tathā bhojanam ṣaṣ rasam tatra teṣām svayam upasthitam triṃśat varṣa sahasrāṇi mānasīm siddhim āsthitāḥ śālmala anteṣu vijñeyam dvīpeṣu triṣu sarvatas vyākhyātaḥ śālmala antānām dvīpānām tu vidhiḥ śubhaḥ Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca gomedakam pravakṣyāmi ṣaṣṭham dvīpam tapodhanāḥ prathamaḥ sumanāḥ nāma jāti añjana mayaḥ giriḥ śātakaumbha mayaḥ śrīmān vijñeyaḥ su mahā citaḥ ṣaṣṭhena tu samudreṇa surodāt dviguṇena ca saumanam prathamam varṣam dhātakīkhaṇḍam ucyate gomedam yat smṛtam varṣam nāmnā sarvasukham tu tat pūrveṇa tasya dvīpasya sumanāḥ parvataḥ sthitaḥ prāc paścima āyataiḥ pādaiḥ āsamudrāt iti sthitaḥ etaiḥ parvata pādaiḥ tu sa deśaḥ vai dvidhā kṛtaḥ dakṣiṇa ardham tu dvīpasya dhātakīkhaṇḍam ucyate samudra ikṣu rasam ca eva gomedāt dviguṇam hi saḥ āvṛtya tiṣṭhati dvīpaḥ puṣkaraḥ puṣkaraiḥ vṛtaḥ puṣkareṇa vṛtaḥ śrīmān citrasānu mahā giriḥ kūṭaiḥ citraiḥ maṇi mayaiḥ śilā jāla samudbhavaiḥ parimaṇḍala sahasrāṇi vistīrṇaḥ saptaviṃśatiḥ ūrdhvam sa vai caturviṃśat yojanānām mahā balaḥ dvīpa ardhasya parikṣiptaḥ paścime mānasaḥ giriḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi sārdham pañcāśat ucchritaḥ tasya putraḥ mahāvītaḥ paścima ardhasya rakṣitā pūrva ardhe parvatasya api dvidhā deśaḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ svādu udakena udadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca eva gomedāt dviguṇena tu triṃśat varṣa sahasrāṇi teṣu jīvanti mānavāḥ ārogyam sukha bāhulyam mānasīm siddhim āsthitāḥ sukham āyuḥ ca rūpam ca triṣu dvīpeṣu sarvaśas adhama uttamau na teṣu āstām tulyāḥ te vīrya rūpataḥ satya anṛte na teṣu āstām dharma adharmau tathā eva ca varṇa āśramāṇām vārttā ca pāśupālyam vaṇij kṛṣiḥ trayī vidyā daṇḍanītiḥ śuśrūṣā daṇḍaḥ eva ca na tatra varṣam nadyaḥ vā śīta uṣṇam ca na vidyate tulya uttarakurūṇām tu kālaḥ tatra tu sarvadā sargaḥ tu dhātakīkhaṇḍe mahāvīte tathā eva ca evam dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ tu sapta saptabhiḥ āvṛtāḥ evam dvīpa samudrāṇām vṛddhiḥ jñeyā parasparam apām ca eva samudrekāt samudraḥ iti saṃjñitaḥ ṛṣat vasantyaḥ varṣeṣu prajāḥ yatra caturvidhāḥ āpūryamāṇaḥ hi udadhiḥ ātmanā eva abhipūryate tatas vai kṣīyamāṇe tu sva ātmani eva hi apām kṣayaḥ udayāt payasām yogāt āpaḥ yathā svayam udaye astamaye ca indoḥ pakṣayoḥ śukla kṛṣṇayoḥ kṣaya vṛddhī samudrasya śaśi vṛddhi kṣaye tathā daśa uttarāṇi pañca āhuḥ aṅgulānām śatāni ca apām vṛddhiḥ kṣayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ samudrāṇām tu parvasu dvis āpa tvāt smṛtaḥ dvīpaḥ dadhanāt ca udadhiḥ smṛtaḥ nigīrṇa tvāt ca girayaḥ parva bandhāt ca parvatāḥ śākadvīpe tu vai śākaḥ parvataḥ tena ca ucyate śālmaliḥ śālmala dvīpe pūjyate sa mahā drumaḥ tasmin sa vasati brahmā sādhyaiḥ sārdham prajāpatiḥ dvīpeṣu teṣu sarveṣu prajānām kramaśas tu vai ārogya āyuḥ pramāṇābhyām dviguṇam dviguṇam tatas dvīpeṣu teṣu sarveṣu yathoktam varṣakeṣu ca ṣaṣ rasam tat mahā vīryam tatra te bhuñjate janāḥ pareṇa puṣkarasya atha āvṛtya avasthitaḥ mahān svādu udakasya paritas śailaḥ tu parimaṇḍalaḥ prakāśaḥ ca aprakāśaḥ ca lokālokaḥ saḥ ucyate loka vistāra mātram tu pṛthivī ardham tu bāhyatas bhūmeḥ daśaguṇāḥ ca apaḥ samantāt pālayanti gām adbhyaḥ daśaguṇaḥ ca agniḥ sarvatas dhārayati apaḥ agneḥ daśaguṇaḥ vāyuḥ dhārayan jyotiḥ āsthitaḥ tiryak ca maṇḍalaḥ vāyuḥ bhūtāni āveṣṭya dhārayan daśa adhikam tathā ākāśam vāyoḥ bhūtāni adhārayat bhūtāditaḥ daśaguṇam mahat bhūtāni adhārayat ādhāra ādheya bhāvena vikārāḥ te vikāriṇām paraspara adhikāḥ ca eva praviṣṭāḥ ca parasparam yasmāt praviṣṭāḥ te anyonyam tasmāt te sthiratām gatāḥ āsan te hi aviśeṣāḥ ca viśeṣāḥ anya veśanāt tathā hi āloke ākāśe paricchinnāni sarvaśas pātre mahati pātrāṇi yathā hi antargatāni ca tathā hi āloke ākāśe bhedāḥ tu antargata āgatāḥ kṛtāni etāni tattvāni anyonyasya adhikāni ca jantūnām iha saṃskāraḥ bhūteṣu antargateṣu vai tasmāt parimitāḥ bhedāḥ smṛtāḥ kārya ātmakāḥ tu vai te kāraṇa ātmakāḥ ca eva syuḥ bhedāḥ mahat ādayaḥ iti evam saṃniveśaḥ ayam pṛthvī ākrāntaḥ tu bhāgaśas sapta dvīpa samudrāṇām yāthātathyena vai mayā vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca eva prasaṃkhyānena ca eva hi viśva rūpam pradhānasya parimāṇa ekadeśinaḥ etāvat saṃniveśaḥ tu mayā samyak prakāśitaḥ etāvat eva śrotavyam saṃniveśasya pārthiva Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca sapta dvīpa samudrāṇām dvīpānām bhāti vistaraḥ paryāsa parimāṇam ca candra ādityau prakāśataḥ paryāsa pārimāṇyāt tu budhaiḥ tulyam divaḥ smṛtam trīn lokān prati sāmānyāt sūryaḥ yāti avilambataḥ acirāt tu prakāśena avanāt tu raviḥ smṛtaḥ bhūyas bhūyas pravakṣyāmi pramāṇam candra sūryayoḥ vistārāt triguṇaḥ ca api pariṇāhaḥ atra maṇḍale viṣkambhāt maṇḍalāt ca eva bhāskarāt dviguṇaḥ śaśī atas pṛthivyāḥ vakṣyāmi pramāṇam yojanaiḥ punar sapta dvīpa samudrāyāḥ vistāraḥ maṇḍalasya tu iti etat iha saṃkhyātam purāṇe parimāṇataḥ tat vakṣyāmi prasaṃkhyāya sāmpratam ca abhimānibhiḥ śatārdha koṭi vistārā pṛthivī kṛtsnaśas smṛtā tasyāḥ ca ardha pramāṇam ca meroḥ ca eva uttarottaram meroḥ madhye pratidiśam koṭiḥ ekā tu sā smṛtā tathā śata sahasrāṇām ekonanavatim punar pañcāśat ca sahasrāṇi pṛthivī ardhasya vistaraḥ tisraḥ koṭyaḥ tu vistārāt saṃkhyātāḥ tu caturdiśam tathā śata sahasrāṇām ekonāśītiḥ ucyate sapta dvīpa samudrāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ sa tu vistaraḥ vistāram triguṇam ca eva pṛthivī antara maṇḍalam gaṇitam yojanānām tu koṭyaḥ tu ekādaśa smṛtāḥ tathā śata sahasrāṇām saptatriṃśa adhikāḥ tu tāḥ tārakā saṃniveśasya divi yāvat tu maṇḍalam paryāpta saṃniveśasya bhūmeḥ tāvat tu maṇḍalam paryāsa parimāṇam ca bhūmeḥ tulyam divaḥ smṛtam meroḥ prācyām diśāyām tu mānasa uttara mūrdhani vastu eka sārā māhendrī puṇyā hema pariṣkṛtā dakṣiṇena punar meroḥ mānasasya tu pṛṣṭhatas suṣā nāma purī ramyā varuṇasya api dhīmataḥ mānasottara pṛṣṭhe tu lokapālāḥ caturdiśam sthitāḥ dharma vyavasthā artham loka saṃrakṣaṇāya ca lokapāla upariṣṭāt tu sarvatas dakṣiṇāyane dakṣiṇa upakrame sūryaḥ kṣipta iṣuḥ iva sarpati jyotiṣām cakram ādāya satatam parigacchati madhya gaḥ ca amarāvatyām yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ suṣāyām ardharātraḥ tu vibhāvaryāḥ astam eti ca suṣāyām atha vāruṇyām uttiṣṭhan sa tu dṛśyate suṣāyām atha vāruṇyām madhyāhne tu raviḥ yadā vibhāvaryām soma puryām uttiṣṭhati vibhāvasuḥ ardha rātram saṃyamane vāruṇyām astam eti ca bhraman vai bhramamāṇāni ṛkṣāṇi carate raviḥ evam caturṣu pārśveṣu dakṣiṇa anteṣu sarpati udaya astamaye vā asau uttiṣṭhati punar punar pūrvāhṇe ca aparāhṇe ca dvau dvau devālayau tu saḥ udaya astamayābhyām ca smṛte pūrva apare tu vai yādṛś purastāt tapati yādṛś pṛṣṭhe tu pārśvayoḥ yatra udayaḥ tu dṛśyeta teṣām saḥ udayaḥ smṛtaḥ praṇāśam gacchate yatra teṣām astaḥ saḥ ucyate vidūra bhāvāt arkasya bhūmeḥ eṣā gatasya ca śrayante raśmayaḥ yasmāt tena rātrau na dṛśyate ūrdhvam śata sahasra aṃśuḥ sthitaḥ tatra pradṛśyate yojanānām sahasrasya imām saṃkhyām nibodhata pūrṇam śata sahasrāṇām ekatriṃśat ca sā smṛtā pañcāśat ca sahasrāṇi tathā anyāni adhikāni ca mauhūrtikī gatiḥ hi eṣā sūryasya tu vidhīyate etena krama yogeṇa yadā kāṣṭhām tu dakṣiṇām parigacchati sūryaḥ asau māsam kāṣṭhām udak dināt sarvatas dakṣiṇasyām tu kāṣṭhāyām tat nibodhata nava koṭyaḥ prasaṃkhyātāḥ yojanaiḥ parimaṇḍalam tathā śata sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśat ca pañca ca ahorātrāt pataṃgasya gatiḥ eṣā vidhīyate dakṣiṇā diś nivṛttaḥ asau viṣuva sthaḥ yadā raviḥ tisraḥ koṭyaḥ tu sampūrṇāḥ viṣuvasya api maṇḍalam tathā śata sahasrāṇi viṃśati eka adhikāni tu śrāvaṇe ca uttarām kāṣṭhām citrabhānuḥ yadā bhavet uttarāyāḥ pramāṇam tu kāṣṭhāyāḥ maṇḍalasya tu vaiśvānaram dakṣiṇatas nirdiṣṭam iha tattvataḥ nāgavīthī uttarā vīthī hi ajavīthiḥ tu dakṣiṇā ubhe āṣāḍha mūlam tu ajavīthī ādayaḥ trayaḥ abhijit pūrvatas svātim nāgavīthī uttarāḥ trayaḥ aśvinī kṛttikā yāmyā nāgavīthyaḥ trayaḥ smṛtāḥ rohiṇī ārdrā mṛgaśiraḥ nāgavīthiḥ iti smṛtā puṣya āśleṣā punarvasvoḥ vīthī ca airāvatī smṛtā pūrva uttara proṣṭhapadau go vīthī revatī smṛtā śravaṇam ca dhaniṣṭhā ca vāruṇam ca jaradgavam hastaścitrā tathā svātī hi ajavīthiḥ iti smṛtā jyeṣṭhā viśākhā maitram ca mṛgavīthī tathā ucyate mūlam pūrva uttara āṣāḍhe vīthī vaiśvānarī bhavet smṛtāḥ tisraḥ tu vīthyaḥ tāḥ mārge vai dakṣiṇe punar kāṣṭhayoḥ antaram ca etat vakṣyate yojanaiḥ punar etat śata sahasrāṇām ekatriṃśat tu vai smṛtam śatāni trīṇi ca anyāni trayastriṃśat tathā eva ca kāṣṭhayoḥ antaram hi etat yojanānām prakīrtitam kāṣṭhayoḥ lekhayoḥ ca eva ayane dakṣiṇa uttare sahasreṇa atiriktā ca tatas anyā pañcaviṃśatiḥ lekhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ ca eva bāhya abhyantarayoḥ caran abhyantaram sa paryeti maṇḍalāni uttarāyaṇe bāhyatas dakṣiṇena eva satatam sūrya maṇḍalam caran asau udīcyām ca hi aśītyā maṇḍalān śatam pramāṇam maṇḍalasya api yojanānām nibodhata yojanānām sahasrāṇi daśa ca aṣṭau tathā smṛtam adhikāni aṣṭapañcāśat yojanāni tu vai punar ahar tu carate nābheḥ sūryaḥ vai maṇḍalam kramāt dakṣiṇe cakra vat sūryaḥ tathā śīghram nivartate tasmāt prakṛṣṭām bhūmim tu kālena alpena gacchati sūryaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ śīghram muhūrtaiḥ dakṣiṇāyane trayodaśa ardham ṛkṣāṇām madhye carati maṇḍalam muhūrtaiḥ tāni ṛkṣāṇi naktam aṣṭādaśaiḥ caran tasmāt dīrgheṇa kālena bhūmim saḥ alpām prasarpati sūryaḥ aṣṭādaśabhiḥ ahnaḥ muhūrtaiḥ udagāyane trayodaśānām madhye tu ṛkṣāṇām carate raviḥ muhūrtaiḥ tāni ṛkṣāṇi rātrau dvādaśabhiḥ caran muhūrtaiḥ triṃśatā tāvat ahorātram bhuvaḥ bhraman ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ madhye bhramate maṇḍalāni tu dakṣiṇa prakrame vā api divā śīghram vidhīyate gatiḥ sūryasya vai naktam mandā ca api vidhīyate evam gati viśeṣeṇa vibhajan rātri ahāni tu ajavīthyām dakṣiṇāyām lokālokasya ca uttaram loka saṃtānataḥ hi eṣa vaiśvānara pathāt bahis vyuṣṭiḥ yāvat prabhā saurī puṣkarāt sampravartate pārśvebhyaḥ bāhyatas tāvat lokālokaḥ ca parvataḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi daśa ūrdhvam ca ucchritaḥ giriḥ prakāśaḥ ca aprakāśaḥ ca parvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ nakṣatra candra sūryāḥ ca grahāḥ tārā gaṇaiḥ saha tasmāt saṃdhyā iti tām āhuḥ uṣā vyuṣṭaiḥ yathā antaram uṣāḥ rātriḥ smṛtā vipraiḥ vyuṣṭiḥ ca api ahar smṛtam hrāsaḥ vṛddhiḥ ahar bhāgaiḥ divasānām yathā tu vai saṃdhyā muhūrta mātrāyām hrāsa vṛddhī tu te ṛte prātar smṛtaḥ tatas kālaḥ bhāgān ca āhuḥ ca pañca ca tasmāt prātar gatāt kālāt muhūrtāḥ saṃgavaḥ trayaḥ tasmāt madhyaṃdināt kālāt aparāhṇaḥ iti smṛtaḥ trayaḥ eva muhūrtāḥ tu kālaḥ eṣa smṛtaḥ budhaiḥ aparāhṇa vyatītāt ca kālaḥ sāyam saḥ ucyate daśa pañca muhūrta ahnaḥ muhūrtāḥ trayaḥ eva ca daśa pañca muhūrtam vai ahar tu viṣuve smṛtam āloka antar smṛtaḥ lokaḥ lokāt ca ālokaḥ ucyate catvāraḥ te mahātmānaḥ tiṣṭhanti ābhūtasaṃplavam sudhāmā ca eva vairājaḥ kardamaḥ ca prajāpatiḥ hiraṇyaromā parjanyaḥ ketumān rājasaḥ ca saḥ nirdvaṃdvāḥ nirabhīmānāḥ nistandrāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ lokapālāḥ sthitāḥ tu ete lokāloke caturdiśam uttaram yat agastyasya śṛṅgam deva ṛṣi sevitam pitṛyānaḥ smṛtaḥ panthāḥ vaiśvānara pathāt bahis tatra āsate prajā kāmāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ye agnihotriṇaḥ lokasya saṃtāna karāḥ pitṛyāne pathi sthitāḥ bhūta ārambha kṛtam karma āśiṣaḥ ca viśām pate prārabhante loka kāmāḥ teṣām panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ saṃtapta tapasā ca eva maryādābhiḥ śrutena ca jāyamānāḥ tu pūrve vai paścimānām gṛheṣu te paścimāḥ ca eva pūrveṣām jāyante nidhaneṣu iha evam āvartamānāḥ te vartanti ābhūtasaṃplavam aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇām gṛhamedhinām savituḥ dakṣiṇam mārgam āśritya abhūtasaṃplavam kriyāvatām prasaṃkhyā eṣā ye śmaśānāni bhejire loka saṃvyavahāra artham bhūta ārambha kṛtena ca iti etaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhāḥ śmaśānāni iha bhejire prajā oṣaṇiḥ saptarṣayaḥ dvāpareṣu iha jajñire aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi teṣām api ūrdhvaretasām īrṣyā dveṣa nivṛttyā ca bhūta ārambha vivarjanāt tatas anya kāma saṃyoga śabda ādeḥ doṣa darśanāt iti etaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ śuddhaiḥ te amṛta tvam hi bhejire ābhūtasamplava sthānām amṛta tvam vibhāvyate bhrūṇahatyā aśvamedha ādi pāpa puṇya nibhaiḥ param etat viṣṇu padam divyam tṛtīyam vyomni bhāsvaram yatra gatvā na śocanti tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam dharme dhruvasya tiṣṭhanti ye tu lokasya kāṅkṣiṇaḥ Purāṇa evam śrutvā kathām divyām abruvan laumaharṣaṇim sūryācandramasoḥ cāram grahāṇām ca eva sarvaśas ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ bhramanti katham etāni jyotīṃṣi ravi maṇḍale a vyūhena eva sarvāṇi tathā ca asaṃkareṇa vā sūtaḥ uvāca pratyakṣam api dṛśyam tat saṃmohayati vai prajāḥ yaḥ asau caturdaśa ṛkṣeṣu śiśumāraḥ vyavasthitaḥ teṣām bhedaḥ ca yogaḥ ca tathā kālasya niścayaḥ jīmūtāḥ nāma te meghāḥ yat ebhyaḥ jīva sambhavaḥ dvitīyaḥ āvahan vāyuḥ meghāḥ te tu abhisaṃśritāḥ vṛṣṭi sargaḥ tathā teṣām dhārā sāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ puṣkarāvartakāḥ nāma ye meghāḥ pakṣa sambhavāḥ śakreṇa pakṣāḥ chinnāḥ vai parvatānām mahā ojasā kāmagānām samṛddhānām bhūtānām nāśam icchatām puṣkarāḥ nāma te pakṣāḥ bṛhantaḥ toya dhāriṇaḥ puṣkarāvartakāḥ nāma kāraṇena iha śabditāḥ nānā rūpa dharāḥ ca eva mahā ghora svarāḥ ca te kalpānta vṛṣṭi kartāraḥ kalpānta agneḥ niyāmakāḥ vāyu ādhārāḥ vahante vai sa amṛtāḥ kalpa sādhakāḥ yāni asya aṇḍasya bhinnasya prākṛtāni abhavan tadā tāni eva aṇḍa kapālāni sarve meghāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām āpyāyanam dhūmaḥ sarveṣām aviśeṣatas teṣām śreṣṭhaḥ ca parjanyaḥ catvāraḥ ca eva diggajāḥ gajānām parvatānām ca meghānām bhogibhiḥ saha kulam ekam dvidhā bhūtam yoniḥ ekā jalam smṛtam tuṣāra varṣam varṣanti vṛddhāḥ hi anna vivṛddhaye ṣaṣṭhaḥ parivahaḥ nāma vāyuḥ teṣām parāyaṇaḥ yau asau bibharti bhagavān gaṅgām ākāśa gocarām divya amṛta jalām puṇyām tripathām iti viśrutām tasyāḥ vispanditam toyam diggajāḥ pṛthubhiḥ karaiḥ śīkarān sampramuñcanti nīhāraḥ iti sa smṛtaḥ dakṣiṇena giriḥ yaḥ asau hemakūṭaḥ iti smṛtaḥ puṇḍram nāma samākhyātam samyak vṛṣṭi vivṛddhaye himavantam atikramya vṛṣṭi śeṣam tatas param ibha āsye ca tatas paścāt idam bhūta vivṛddhaye varṣa dvayam samākhyātam samyak vṛṣṭi vivṛddhaye sūryaḥ eva tu vṛṣṭīnām sraṣṭā samupadiśyate varṣam gharmam himam rātrim saṃdhye ca eva dinam tathā śubha aśubha phalāni iha dhruvāt sarvam pravartate dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhitāḥ ca apaḥ sūryaḥ vai gṛhya tiṣṭhati sarva bhūta śarīreṣu tu āpaḥ hi anuśritāḥ ca yāḥ dahyamāneṣu teṣu eva jaṅgama sthāvareṣu ca dhūma bhūtāḥ tu tāḥ hi āpaḥ niṣkrāmanti iha sarvaśas tena ca abhrāṇi jāyante sthānam abhra mayam smṛtam tatas tu ṛtu vaśāt kāle parivartan divākaraḥ niyacchati āpaḥ meghebhyaḥ śuklāḥ śuklaiḥ tu raśmibhiḥ abhra sthāḥ prapatanti āpaḥ vāyunā samudīritāḥ tatas varṣati ṣaṣ māsān sarva bhūta vivṛddhaye vāyubhiḥ stanitam ca eva vidyutaḥ tu agni jāḥ smṛtāḥ sraṣṭā asau vṛṣṭi sargasya dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhitaḥ raviḥ dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhitaḥ vāyuḥ vṛṣṭim saṃharate punar grahat nivṛttyā sūryāt tu carate ṛkṣa maṇḍalam cārasya ante viśati arkam dhruveṇa samadhiṣṭhitam atas sūrya rathasya api saṃniveśam pracakṣate sthitena tu eka cakreṇa pañca areṇa tri nābhinā hiraṇmayena aṇunā vai aṣṭa cakra eka neminā cakreṇa bhāsvatā sūryaḥ syandanena prasarpiṇā dviguṇā ca rathopasthāt īṣā daṇḍaḥ pramāṇataḥ sa tasya brahmaṇā sṛṣṭaḥ rathaḥ hi artha vaśena tu vāruṇasya rathasya iha lakṣaṇaiḥ sadṛśaḥ ca saḥ atha aṅgāni tu sūryasya pratyaṅgāni rathasya ca arāḥ saṃvatsarāḥ tasya nemyaḥ ṣaṣ ṛtavaḥ smṛtāḥ akṣa koṭyoḥ yugāni asya ārtavāhāḥ kalāḥ smṛtāḥ tasya kāṣṭhā smṛtā ghoṇā danta paṅktiḥ kṣaṇāḥ tu vai nimeṣaḥ ca anukarṣaḥ asya īṣā ca asya kalā smṛtā yuga akṣa koṭī te tasya artha kāmau ubhau smṛtau sapta aśvarūpāḥ chandāṃsi vahante vāyu raṃhasā paṅktiḥ ca bṛhatī ca eva uṣṇih eva tu saptamam yuga akṣa koṭī te tasya dakṣiṇe syandanasya tu yuga akṣa koṭī te tasya vāta ūrmī syandanasya tu bhramataḥ tasya raśmī te maṇḍale tu uttarāyaṇe vardhete dakṣiṇeṣu atra bhramataḥ maṇḍalāni tu ākṛṣyete yadā te tu dhruveṇa samadhiṣṭhite aśīti maṇḍala śatam kāṣṭhayoḥ ubhayoḥ caran tathā eva bāhyatas sūryaḥ bhramate maṇḍalāni tu Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca dhātā aryamā pulastyaḥ ca pulahaḥ ca prajāpatī uragau vāsukiḥ ca eva saṃkīrṇaḥ ca eva tau ubhau kṛtasthalā apsarāḥ ca eva yā ca sā puñjikasthalā rakṣaḥ hetiḥ prahetiḥ ca yātudhānau ubhau ṛtau ṛṣī atriḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca nāgau takṣa karambhakau menakā sahajanyī ca hāhā hūhūḥ ca gāyakau puruṣādaḥ vadhaḥ ca eva yātudhānau tu tau smṛtau ete vasanti vai sūrye māsayoḥ śuci śukrayoḥ tatas sūrye punar ca anyāḥ nivasanti sma devatāḥ indraḥ ca eva vivasvān ca aṅgirāḥ bhṛguḥ eva ca elāpattraḥ tathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālaḥ ca pannagaḥ viśvāvasu suṣeṇau ca prātar ca eva rathaḥ ca hi māsau dvau devatāḥ sūrye vasanti ca śarad ṛtau parjanyaḥ ca eva pūṣā ca bharadvājaḥ sa gautamaḥ viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca ubhe te puṇya lakṣaṇe nāgaḥ ca airāvataḥ ca eva viśrutaḥ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ senajit ca suṣeṇaḥ ca senānīḥ grāmaṇīḥ tathā cāraḥ vātaḥ ca dvau etau yātudhānau ubhau smṛtau aṃśaḥ bhagaḥ ca dvau etau kaśyapaḥ ca kratuḥ ca tau bhujaṃgaḥ ca mahāpadmaḥ sarpaḥ karkoṭakaḥ tathā citrasenaḥ ca gandharvaḥ pūrṇāyuḥ ca eva gāyanau apsarāḥ pūrvacittiḥ ca gandharvā hi urvaśī ca yā tārkṣyaḥ ca ariṣṭanemiḥ ca senānīḥ grāmaṇīḥ ca tau tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ jamadagniḥ viśvāmitraḥ tathā eva ca kādraveyau tathā nāgau kambala aśvatarau ubhau gandharvau dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ca sūryavarcāḥ ca tau ubhau tilottamā apsarāḥ ca eva devī rambhā manoramā grāmaṇīḥ ṛtajit ca eva satyajit ca mahā balaḥ sthāna abhimāninaḥ hi ete gaṇāḥ dvādaśa saptakāḥ vidyā grāmaṇinaḥ yakṣāḥ kurvantyā abhīṣu saṃgraham sarpāḥ sarpanti vai sūrye yātudhāna anuyānti ca eteṣām eva devānām yathāvīryam yathā tapaḥ yathāyogam yathādharmam yathātattvam yathābalam bhūtānām aśubham sarvam vyapohati sva tejasā duritam śubha cārāṇām vyapohanti kvacid kvacid sthāna abhimāninām hi etat sthānam manvantareṣu vai atīta anāgatānām ca vartante sāmpratam ca ye grīṣme hime ca varṣāsu muñcamānāḥ yathākramam gacchati asau anudinam parivṛtya raśmīn devān pitṝn ca manujān ca su tarpayan vai śukle ca kṛṣṇe tad ahar krameṇa kāla kṣaye ca eva surāḥ pibanti māsena tat ca amṛtam asya mṛṣṭam su vṛṣṭaye raśmiṣu rakṣitam tu sarve amṛtam tat pitaraḥ pibanti devāḥ ca saumyāḥ ca tathā eva kāvyāḥ vṛṣṭyā abhivṛṣṭābhiḥ atha auṣadhībhiḥ martyāḥ atha annena kṣudham jayanti tṛptiḥ ca tena ardha māsam surāṇām māsam sudhābhiḥ svadhayā pitṝṇām annena jīvanti aniśam manuṣyāḥ sūryaḥ śritam tat hi bibharti gobhiḥ iti eṣaḥ eka cakreṇa sūryaḥ tūrṇam prasarpati kāma rūpaiḥ sakṛt yuktaiḥ kāmagaiḥ taiḥ manojavaiḥ bāhyatas anantaram ca eva maṇḍalam divasa kramāt āvṛtaḥ vālakhilyaiḥ ca bhramate rātri ahāni tu sevyate gīta nṛtyaiḥ ca gandharva apsarasām gaṇaiḥ pataṃgaiḥ patagaiḥ aśvaiḥ bhrāmyamāṇaḥ divaspatiḥ vīthi āśrayāṇi carati nakṣatrāṇi tathā śaśī hrāsa vṛddhī tathā eva asya raśmayaḥ sūrya vat smṛtāḥ tri cakra ubhayatas aśvaḥ ca vijñeyaḥ śaśinaḥ rathaḥ apām garbha samutpannaḥ rathaḥ sa aśvaḥ sa sārathiḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ rathe tasmin śvetaḥ cakṣuḥśravāḥ ca vai aśvāḥ tam eka varṇāḥ te vahante śaṅkha varcasaḥ ajaḥ ca tripathaḥ ca eva vṛṣaḥ vājī naraḥ hayaḥ aṃśumān saptadhātuḥ ca haṃsaḥ vyomamṛgaḥ tathā devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ somaḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha gacchati āpūryate paraḥ bhāgaḥ somasya tu ahar kramāt tatas pīta kṣayam somam raviḥ pītam pañcadaśa aham ca raśminā ekena bhāskaraḥ āpūrayan dadau tena bhāgam bhāgam ahar kramāt tasmāt hrasanti vai kṛṣṇe śukle hi āpyāyayanti ca iti evam sūrya vīryeṇa candrasya āpyāyate tanuḥ paurṇamāsyām pradṛśyeta śuklaḥ sampūrṇa maṇḍalaḥ evam āpyāyate somaḥ śuklapakṣeṣu ahar kramāt saṃbhṛtam tu ardha māsena amṛtam sūrya tejasā bhakṣa artham āgatam somam paurṇamāsyām upāsate eka rātram surāḥ sārdham pitṛbhiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ ca vai somasya kṛṣṇa pakṣa ādau bhāskara abhimukhasya vai prakṣīyate pare hi ātmā pīyamāna kalā kramāt trayaḥ ca triṃśatā sārdham trayastriṃśat śatāni tu trayastriṃśat sahasrāṇi devāḥ somam pibanti vai iti evam pīyamānasya kṛṣṇe vardhanti tāḥ kalāḥ kṣīyante ca tāḥ śuklāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ hi āpyāyayanti ca evam dina kramāt pīte devaiḥ ca api niśākare pītvā ardha māsam gacchanti amāvāsyām surāḥ ca te pitaraḥ ca upatiṣṭhanti amāvāsyām niśākaram tatas pañcadaśe bhāge kiṃcid śeṣe niśākare pibanti dvi kalam kālam śiṣṭāḥ tāḥ tu kalāḥ tu yāḥ viniḥsṛṣṭam tu amāvāsyām gabhastibhyaḥ tadā amṛtam saumyāḥ barhiṣadaḥ ca eva agniṣvāttāḥ ca ye smṛtāḥ kāvyāḥ ca eva tu ye proktāḥ pitaraḥ sarve eva te saṃvatsarāḥ ca ye kāvyāḥ pañca abdāḥ vai dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ saumyāḥ su tapasaḥ jñeyāḥ saumyāḥ barhiṣadaḥ tathā agniṣvāttāḥ trayaḥ ca eva pitṛ sarga sthitāḥ dvijāḥ pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānāyām pañcadaśyām tu vai kalām yāvat ca kṣīyate tasmāt bhāgaḥ pañcadaśaḥ tu saḥ amāvāsyām tathā tasya antarā pūryate paraḥ vṛddhi kṣayau vai pakṣa ādau ṣoḍaśyām śaśinaḥ mṛtau evam sūrya nimitte te kṣaya vṛddhī niśākare Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca tārā grahāṇām vakṣyāmi svarbhānoḥ tu ratham punar yuktaḥ hayaiḥ piśaṅgaḥ tu daśabhiḥ vāta raṃhasaiḥ śvetaḥ piśaṅgaḥ sāraṅgaḥ nīlaḥ śyāmaḥ vilohitaḥ śvetaḥ ca haritaḥ ca eva pṛṣataḥ vṛṣṇiḥ eva ca tatas bhauma rathaḥ ca api aṣṭa aṅgaḥ kāñcanaḥ smṛtaḥ atas ca āṅgirasaḥ vidvān deva ācāryaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ yuktena aṣṭābhiḥ aśvaiḥ ca dhvajaiḥ agni samudbhavaiḥ yuktena aṣṭābhiḥ aśvaiḥ ca sa dhvajaiḥ agni saṃnibhaiḥ tatas śanaiścaraḥ api aśvaiḥ sabalaiḥ vāta raṃhasaiḥ kārṣṇāyasam samāruhya syandanam yāti asau śaniḥ svarbhānoḥ tu yathā aṣṭa aśvāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ vai vāta raṃhasaḥ ratham tamaḥ mayam tasya vahanti sma su daṃśitāḥ tatas ketumataḥ tu aśvāḥ aṣṭau te vāta raṃhasaḥ palāla dhūma varṇa ābhāḥ kṣāma dehāḥ su dāruṇāḥ ete vāhāḥ grahāṇām vai mayā proktāḥ rathaiḥ saha ete vai bhrāmyamāṇāḥ te yathāyogam vahanti vai vāya yābhiḥ adṛśyābhiḥ prabaddhāḥ vāta raśmibhiḥ yāvat tam anuparyeti dhruvam ca jyotiṣām gaṇaḥ tathā deva gṛhāṇi syuḥ uhyante vāta raṃhasā yāvatyaḥ ca eva tārāḥ syuḥ tāvantaḥ asya marīcayaḥ tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vāta baddhāni sarvaśas eṣa tārā mayaḥ proktaḥ śiśumāre dhruvaḥ divi yat ahnā kurute pāpam tam dṛṣṭvā niśi muñcati śiśumāra śarīra sthāḥ yāvatyaḥ tārakāḥ tu tāḥ varṣāṇi dṛṣṭvā jīveta tāvat eva adhikāni tu śiśumāra ākṛtim jñātvā pravibhāgena sarvaśas uttānapādaḥ tasya atha vijñeyaḥ sottaraḥ hanuḥ yajñaḥ adharaḥ tu vijñeyaḥ dharmaḥ mūrdhānam āśritaḥ hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ sādhyāḥ aśvinau pūrva pādayoḥ varuṇaḥ ca aryamā ca eva paścime tasya sakthinī śiśne saṃvatsaraḥ jñeyaḥ mitraḥ ca apānam āśritaḥ nakṣatra candra sūryāḥ ca grahāḥ tārā gaṇaiḥ saha tad mukha abhimukhāḥ sarve cakra bhūtāḥ divi sthitāḥ dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhitāḥ ca eva dhruvam eva pradakṣiṇam pariyānti suraśreṣṭham meḍhī bhūtam dhruvam divi āgnīdhra kāśyapānām tu teṣām sa paramaḥ dhruvaḥ jyotiṣām cakram ādāya ākarṣan tam adhomukhaḥ Purāṇa ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ yat etat bhavatā proktam śrutam sarvam aśeṣatas katham deva gṛhāṇi syuḥ punar jyotīṃṣi varṇaya sūtaḥ uvāca yathā deva gṛhāṇi syuḥ sūryācandramasoḥ tathā agneḥ vyuṣṭau rajanyām vai brahmaṇā avyakta yoninā avyākṛtam idam tu āsīt naiśena tamasā vṛtam catur bhūta avaśiṣṭe asmin brahmaṇā samadhiṣṭhite jñātvā agnim kalpa kāla ādau apaḥ pṛthvīm ca saṃśritā sa saṃbhṛtya prakāśa artham tridhā tulyaḥ abhavat punar yaḥ ca asau tapate sūrye śuciḥ agniḥ ca sa smṛtaḥ kāṣṭha indhanaḥ tu nirmathyaḥ saḥ adbhiḥ śāmyati pāvakaḥ arciṣmān pacanaḥ agniḥ tu niṣprabhaḥ saumya lakṣaṇaḥ yaḥ ca asau maṇḍale śukle nirūṣmā na prakāśate prabhā saurī tu pādena astam yāti divākare agnim āviśate rātrau tasmāt agniḥ prakāśate udite tu punar sūrye ūṣmā agneḥ tu samāviśat pādena tejasaḥ ca agneḥ tasmāt saṃtapate divā prākāśyam ca tathā auṣṇyam ca saurya āgneye tu tejasī paraspara anupraveśāt āpyāyete divāniśam uttiṣṭhati punar sūrye rātriḥ āviśate hi apaḥ tasmāt tāmrāḥ bhavanti āpaḥ divā rātri praveśanāt tasmāt naktam punar śuklāḥ hi āpaḥ bhāsurāḥ yaḥ ca asau tapate sūryaḥ saḥ apaḥ pibati raśmibhiḥ ādatte sa tu nāḍīnām sahasreṇa samantataḥ tasya raśmi sahasreṇa śīta varṣa uṣṇa niḥsravaḥ tāsām catuḥśatam nāḍyaḥ varṣante citra mūrtayaḥ candanāḥ ca eva medhyāḥ ca ketanāḥ cetanāḥ tathā amṛtāḥ jīvanāḥ sarvāḥ raśmayaḥ vṛṣṭi sarjanāḥ hima udbhavāḥ ca te anyonyam raśmayaḥ triṃśataḥ smṛtāḥ candra tārā grahaiḥ sarvaiḥ pītāḥ bhānoḥ gabhastayaḥ etāḥ madhyāḥ tathā anyāḥ ca hlādinyaḥ hima sarjanāḥ śuklāḥ ca kakubhaḥ ca eva gāvaḥ viśvasṛtaḥ ca yāḥ śuklāḥ tāḥ nāmataḥ sarvāḥ triṃśataḥ gharma sarjanāḥ saṃbibhrati hi tāḥ sarvāḥ manuṣyān devatāḥ pitṝn manuṣyān oṣadhībhiḥ ca svadhayā ca pitṝn api varṣāsu ca śaradi evam caturbhiḥ saṃpravarṣati oṣadhīṣu balam dhatte sudhām ca svadhayā punar bhidyate ṛtum āsādya sahasram bahudhā punar iti evam maṇḍalam śuklam bhāsvaram loka saṃjñitam nakṣatra graha somānām pratiṣṭhā yoniḥ eva ca candra ṛkṣa grahāḥ sarve vijñeyāḥ sūrya sambhavāḥ suṣumnā sūrya raśmiḥ yā kṣīṇam śaśinam edhate dakṣiṇe viśvakarmā tu raśmiḥ āpyāyayat budham viśvāvasuḥ ca yaḥ paścāt śukra yoniḥ ca sa smṛtaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ tu raśmiḥ yoniḥ sa hi bṛhaspateḥ śanaiścaram punar ca api raśmiḥ āpyāyate surāj na kṣīyate yatas tāni tasmāt nakṣatra tā smṛtā kṣetrāṇi etāni vai sūryam āpatanti gabhastibhiḥ kṣetrāṇi teṣām ādatte sūryaḥ nakṣatra tā tatas asmāt lokāt amum lokam tīrṇānām sukṛta ātmanām tāraṇāt tārakāḥ hi etāḥ śukla tvāt ca eva śuklikāḥ divyānām pārthivānām ca vaṃśānām ca eva sarvaśas sravaṇāt tejasaḥ ca eva tena asau savitā smṛtaḥ vasanti karma devāḥ tu sthānāni etāni sarvaśas manvantareṣu sarveṣu ṛṣi sūrya graha ādayaḥ tāni deva gṛhāṇi syuḥ sthāna ākhyāni bhavanti hi śaukram śukraḥ aviśat sthānam ṣoḍaśa aram prabhāsvaram bṛhaspatiḥ bṛhat tvam ca lohitam ca api lohitaḥ śanaiścaraḥ aviśat sthānam evam śānaiścaram tathā nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvāṇi nākṣatrāṇi āviśanti ca jyotīṃṣi sukṛtām ete jñeyāḥ deva gṛhāḥ tu vai sthānāni etāni tiṣṭhanti yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam abhimānena tiṣṭhanti tāni devāḥ punar punar atītāḥ tu saha atītaiḥ bhāvyāḥ bhāvyaiḥ suraiḥ saha vartante vartamānaiḥ ca suraiḥ sārdham tu sthāninaḥ sūryaḥ devaḥ vivasvān ca aṣṭamaḥ tu aditeḥ sutaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ bṛhat tejāḥ deva ācāryaḥ aṅgiraḥ sutaḥ śanaiścaraḥ virūpaḥ ca saṃjñā putraḥ vivasvataḥ agniḥ vikeśyām jajñe tu yuvā asau lohitādhipaḥ nakṣatra nāmnyaḥ kṣetreṣu dākṣāyaṇyaḥ sutāḥ smṛtāḥ svarbhānuḥ siṃhikāputraḥ bhūta saṃsādhanaḥ asuraḥ candra arka graha nakṣatreṣu abhimānī prakīrtitaḥ sthānāni etāni ca uktāni sthāninyaḥ ca eva devatāḥ śuklam agni samam divyam sahasrāṃśoḥ vivasvataḥ sahasrāṃśu tviṣaḥ sthānam ammayam taijasam tathā āśā sthānam manojñasya ravi raśmi gṛhe sthitam śukraḥ ṣoḍaśa raśmiḥ tu yaḥ tu devaḥ hi apaḥ mayaḥ bṛhat dvādaśa raśmīkam haridrā ābham tu vedhasaḥ aṣṭa raśmi śaneḥ tat tu kṛṣṇam vṛddham ayasmayam svarbhānoḥ tu āyasam sthānam bhūtasaṃtāpana ālayam sukṛtām āśrayāḥ tārāḥ raśmayaḥ tu hiraṇmayāḥ tāraṇāt tārakāḥ hi etāḥ śukla tvāt ca eva tārakāḥ nava yojana sāhasraḥ viṣkambhaḥ savituḥ smṛtaḥ maṇḍalam triguṇam ca asya vistāraḥ bhāskarasya tu dviguṇaḥ sūrya vistārāt vistāraḥ śaśinaḥ smṛtaḥ triguṇam maṇḍalam ca asya vaipulyāt śaśinaḥ smṛtam sarva upari nisṛṣṭāni maṇḍalāni tu tārakāḥ yojana ardha pramāṇāni tābhyaḥ anyāni tu uddhūtya pārthivīm chāyām nirmitām maṇḍala ākṛtim brahmaṇā nirmitam sthānam tṛtīyam tu tamaḥ mayam candrataḥ ṣoḍaśaḥ bhāgaḥ bhārgavasya vidhīyate viṣkambhāt maṇḍalāt ca eva yojanānām tu sa smṛtaḥ bhārgavāt pāda hīnaḥ ca vijñeyaḥ vai bṛhaspatiḥ bṛhaspateḥ pāda hīnau ketu vakrau ubhau smṛtau vistāra maṇḍalābhyām tu pāda hīnaḥ tayoḥ budhaḥ tārā nakṣatra rūpāṇi vapuṣmanti iha yāni vai budhena sama rūpāṇi vistārāt maṇḍalāt tu vai tārā nakṣatra rūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparam śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve ca ekam eva ca sarva upari nisṛṣṭāni maṇḍalāni tu tārakāḥ upariṣṭāt tu ye teṣām grahāḥ ye krūra sāttvikāḥ sauraḥ ca aṅgirasaḥ vakraḥ vijñeyāḥ manda cāriṇaḥ tebhyaḥ adhastāt tu catvāraḥ punar ca anye mahāgrahāḥ somaḥ sūryaḥ budhaḥ ca eva bhārgavaḥ ca iti śīghragāḥ yāvanti ca eva ṛkṣāṇi koṭyaḥ tāvanti tārakāḥ sarveṣām tu grahāṇām vai sūryaḥ adhastāt prasarpati vistīrṇam maṇḍalam kṛtvā tasya ūrdhvam carate śaśī nakṣatra maṇḍalam ca api somāt ūrdhvam prasarpati vakraḥ tu bhārgavāt ūrdhvam vakrāt ūrdhvam bṛhaspatiḥ tasmāt śanaiścaraḥ ca ūrdhvam devācārya upari sthitaḥ śanaiścarāt tathā ca ūrdhvam jñeyam saptarṣi maṇḍalam dviguṇeṣu sahasreṣu yojanānām śateṣu ca graha antaram atha ekaikam ūrdhvam nakṣatra maṇḍalāt tārāgraha antarāṇi syuḥ upari upari adhiṣṭhitam candra arka graha nakṣatrāḥ nīca ucca gṛham āśritāḥ asaṃkareṇa vijñeyaḥ teṣām yogaḥ tu vai budhaiḥ iti evam saṃniveśaḥ vai pṛthivyāḥ jyotiṣām ca yaḥ dvīpānām udadhīnām ca parvatānām tathā eva ca varṣāṇām ca nadīnām ca ye ca teṣu vasanti vai iti eṣaḥ arka vaśena eva saṃniveśaḥ tu jyotiṣām āvartaḥ sāntaraḥ madhye saṃkṣiptaḥ ca dhruvāt tu sa sarvatas teṣu vistīrṇaḥ vṛtta ākāraḥ iva ucchritaḥ loka saṃvyavahāra artham īśvareṇa vinirmitaḥ vaiśvarūpam pradhānasya pariṇāhaḥ asya yaḥ smṛtaḥ teṣām śakyam na saṃkhyātum yāthātathyena kenacid gatāgatam manuṣyeṇa jyotiṣām māṃsa cakṣuṣā Purāṇa ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ katham jagāma bhagavān purāri tvam maheśvaraḥ pṛcchāmaḥ tvām vayam sarve bahu mānāt punar punar devena eka iṣuṇā dagdham tathā naḥ vada mānada sūtaḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam tripuram devaḥ yathā dāritavān bhavaḥ mayaḥ nāma mahā māyaḥ māyānām janakaḥ asuraḥ nirjitaḥ sa tu saṃgrāme tatāpa paramam tapaḥ vidyunmālī ca balavān tāraka ākhyaḥ ca vīryavān lokāḥ iva yathā mūrtāḥ trayaḥ trayaḥ iva agnayaḥ hemante jalaśayyāsu grīṣme pañcatape tathā varṣāsu ca tathā ākāśe kṣapayantaḥ tanūḥ priyāḥ phala mūlāni puṣpāṇi ca jalāni ca anyadā ācarita āhārāḥ paṅkena ācita valkalāḥ magnāḥ śaivāla paṅkeṣu vimala avimaleṣu ca nirmāṃsāḥ ca tatas jātāḥ kṛśāḥ dhamani saṃtatāḥ teṣām tapaḥ prabhāvena prabhāva vidhutam yathā teṣām agre jagat bandhuḥ prādurbhūtaḥ pitāmahaḥ tatas sāhasa kartāraḥ prāhuḥ te sahasā āgatam svakam pitāmaham daityāḥ tam vai tuṣṭuvuḥ eva ca atha tān dānavān brahmā tapasā tapana prabhān uvāca harṣa pūrṇa akṣaḥ harṣa pūrṇa mukhaḥ tadā vriyatām īpsitam yat ca sa abhilāṣam tat ucyatām deva daityāḥ purā devaiḥ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye nirjitāḥ tāḍitāḥ ca eva hatāḥ ca api āyudhaiḥ api śaraṇam nā eva jānīmaḥ śarma vā śaraṇa arthinaḥ tasmin ca tripure durge mad kṛte kṛtinām vara bhūmyānām jala jānām ca śāpānām muni tejasām deva praharaṇānām ca devānām ca prajāpateḥ viśvakarmā iti iva uktaḥ sa tadā viśvakarmaṇā uvāca prahasan vākyam mayam daitya gaṇa adhipam tasmāt durga vidhānam hi kṣaṇāt api vidhīyatām pitāmaha vacaḥ śrutvā tadā evam dānavaḥ mayaḥ prāñjaliḥ punar api āha brahmāṇam padmasambhavam samam sa saṃyuge hanyāt avadhyam śeṣatas bhavet evam astu iti ca api uktvā mayam devaḥ pitāmahaḥ vara dānāt virejuḥ te tapasā ca mahā balāḥ devaiḥ tathā vidhātavyam mayā mati vicāraṇam kāryaḥ teṣām ca viṣkambhaḥ ca ekaika śata yojanam puṣya yogeṇa nirmāṇam purāṇam ca bhaviṣyati puṣya yogeṇa yuktāni yaḥ tāni āsādayiṣyati purāṇi eka prahāreṇa śatāni nihaniṣyati rājatasya upariṣṭāt tu sauvarṇam bhavitā puram dvāraiḥ mahā mandara meru kalpaiḥ prākāra śṛṅgaiḥ suvirājamānam Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca cakāra tripuram durgam manaḥ saṃcāra cāritam iha ca aṭṭālaka dvāram iha ca aṭṭāla gopuram sa vaṭāni taḍāgāni hi atra vāpyaḥ sarāṃsi ca ārāmāḥ ca sabhāḥ ca atra udyānāni atra vā tathā mayena tat puram sṛṣṭam tripuram tu iti naḥ śrutam kārṣṇāyasa mayam yat tu mayena vihitam puram yat tu pūrṇa indu saṃkāśam rājatam nirmitam puram meru parvata saṃkāśam mayasya api puram mahat puṣya saṃyoga mātreṇa kālena sa mayaḥ purā kṛtavān tripuram daityaḥ trinetraḥ puṣpakam yathā yena yena mayaḥ yāti prakurvāṇaḥ puram purāt praśastāḥ tatra tatra eva vāruṇyām ālayāḥ svayam rukma rūpya āyasānām ca śataśas atha sahasraśas ratna ācitāni śobhante purāṇi amara vidviṣām prāsāda śata juṣṭāni kūṭāgāra utkaṭāni ca sarveṣām kāmagāni syuḥ sarva loka atigāni ca citraśālā viśālāni catuḥśāla uttamāni ca sapta aṣṭa daśa bhaumāni satkṛtāni mayena ca bahu dhvaja patākāni sragdāma alaṃkṛtāni ca kiṅkiṇī jāla śabdāni gandhavanti mahānti ca yajña dhūma andhakārāṇi saṃpūrṇa kalaśāni ca gagana āvaraṇa ābhāni haṃsa paṅkti nibhāni ca paṅktīkṛtāni rājante gṛhāṇi tripure pure mallikā jāti puṣpa ādyaiḥ gandha dhūpa adhivāsitaiḥ hema rājata loha ādya maṇi ratna añjana aṅkitāḥ prākārāḥ tripure tasmin giri prākāra saṃnibhāḥ ekaikasmin pure tasmin gopurāṇām śatam śatam sa patākā dhvajavatām dṛśyante giri śṛṅga vat nūpura ārāva ramyāṇi tripure tad purāṇi api svarga atirikta śrīkāṇi tatra kanyā purāṇi ca ārāmaiḥ ca vihāraiḥ ca taḍāga vaṭa catvaraiḥ parikhā śata gambhīrāḥ kṛtāḥ māyā nivāraṇaiḥ niśamya tad durga vidhānam uttamam kṛtam mayena adbhuta vīrya karmaṇā diteḥ sutāḥ daivata rāja vairiṇaḥ sahasraśas prāpuḥ ananta vikramāḥ babhūva pūrṇam tripuram tathā purā yathā ambaram bhūri jalaiḥ jala pradaiḥ Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca tat durgam durga tām prāpa baddha vairaiḥ sura asuraiḥ sa kalatrāḥ sa putrāḥ ca śastravantaḥ antaka upamāḥ mayā ādiṣṭāni viviśuḥ gṛhāṇi hṛṣitāḥ ca te siṃhāḥ vanam iva aneke makarāḥ iva sāgaram roṣaiḥ ca eva ati pāruṣyaiḥ śarīram iva saṃhataiḥ tripuram saṃkulam jātam daitya koṭi śata ākulam sutalāt api niṣpatya pātālāt dānava ālayāt yaḥ yam prārthayate kāmam samprāptaḥ tripura āśrayāt sa candreṣu pradoṣeṣu sa ambujeṣu saraḥsu ca ārāmeṣu sa cūteṣu tapodhana vaneṣu ca su aṅgāḥ candana digdha aṅgām mātaṃgāḥ sa madāḥ iva mṛṣṭa ābharaṇa vastrāḥ ca mṛṣṭa sraj anulepanāḥ priyābhiḥ priya krāmābhiḥ hāva bhāva prasūtibhiḥ nārībhiḥ satatam remuḥ muditāḥ ca eva dānavāḥ mayena nirmite sthāne modamānāḥ mahā asurāḥ teṣām tripura yuktānām tripure tridaśa ariṇām vrajati sma sukham kālaḥ svarga sthānām yathā tathā śuśrūṣante pitṝn putrāḥ patnyaḥ ca api patīn tathā vimukta kalahāḥ ca api prītayaḥ pracurāḥ abhavan na adharmaḥ tripura sthānām bādhate vīryavān api puṇyāha śabdān ucceruḥ āśīrvādān ca veda gān sva nūpura rava unmiśrān veṇu vīṇā ravān api hāsaḥ ca vara nārīṇām citta vyākula kārakaḥ tripure dānava indrāṇām ramatām śrūyate sadā teṣām arcayatām devān brāhmaṇān ca namasyatām dharma artha kāma mantrāṇām mahān kālaḥ abhyavartata atha alakṣmīḥ asūyā ca tṛṣ bubhukṣe tathā eva ca saṃdhyā kālam praviṣṭāḥ te tripuram ca bhaya āvahāḥ samadhyāsuḥ samam ghorāḥ śarīrāṇi yathā āmayāḥ svapne bhaya āvahāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ āviśantaḥ tu dānavān udite ca sahasrāṃśau śubha bhāsa ākare ravau mayaḥ sabhām āviveśa bhāskarābhyām iva ambudaḥ meru kūṭa nibhe ramye āsane svarṇa maṇḍite āsīnāḥ kāñcana gireḥ śṛṅge toyamucaḥ yathā pārśvayoḥ tāraka ākhyaḥ ca vidyunmālī ca dānavaḥ tatas surārayaḥ sarve aśeṣa kopāḥ raṇa ajire upaviṣṭāḥ dṛḍham viddhāḥ dānavāḥ deva śatravaḥ teṣu āsīneṣu sarveṣu sukha āsana gateṣu ca mayaḥ māyā vijanakaḥ iti uvāca sa dānavān khecarāḥ khecara ārāvāḥ bho bho dākṣāyaṇīsutāḥ niśāmayadhvam svapnaḥ ayam mayā dṛṣṭaḥ bhaya āvahaḥ kopa anala ādīpta mukhāḥ praviṣṭāḥ tripura ardinaḥ praviśya ruṣitāḥ te ca purāṇi atula vikramāḥ praviṣṭāḥ sma śarīrāṇi bhūtvā bahu śarīriṇaḥ sa gṛham saha yuṣmābhiḥ sāgara ambhasi majjitam ulūkam rucirā nārī nagna ārūḍhā kharam tathā īdṛśī pramadā dṛṣṭā mayā ca ati bhaya āvahā eṣaḥ īdṛśakaḥ svapnaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vai diti nandanāḥ dṛṣṭaḥ katham hi kaṣṭāya asurāṇām bhaviṣyati kāmam ca īrṣyām ca kopam ca asūyām saṃvihāya ca śāntayaḥ ca prayujyantām pūjyatām ca maheśvaraḥ bhaviṣyāṇi ca dṛśyante yatas naḥ tripure asurāḥ śrutvā dākṣāyaṇī putrāḥ iti evam maya bhāṣitam krodha īrṣyā avasthayā yuktāḥ dṛśyante ca vināśa gāḥ vināśam upapaśyantaḥ hi alakṣmyā vyāpita asurāḥ tatra eva dṛṣṭvā te anyonyam sa krodha āpūrita īkṣaṇāḥ atha daiva paridhvastāḥ dānavāḥ tripura ālayāḥ hitvā satyam ca dharmam ca akāryāṇi upacakramuḥ dviṣanti brāhmaṇān puṇyān na ca arcanti hi devatāḥ uccais gurūn prabhāṣante na abhibhāṣanti pūjitāḥ akasmāt sa aśru nayanāḥ jāyante ca samutsukāḥ bhakṣayanti ca śerantaḥ ucchiṣṭāḥ saṃvṛtāḥ tathā mūtram kṛtvā upaspṛśanti ca a kṛtvā pāda dhāvanam saṃviśanti ca śayyāsu śauca ācāra vivarjitāḥ saṃkucanti bhayāt ca eva mārjārāṇām yathā ākhukaḥ bhāryām gatvā na śudhyanti rahaḥ vṛttiṣu nistrapāḥ purā su śīlāḥ bhūtvā ca duḥśīla tvam upāgatāḥ devān tapodhanān ca eva bādhante tripura ālayāḥ mayena vāryamāṇāḥ api te vināśam upasthitāḥ vipriyāṇi eva viprāṇām kurvāṇāḥ kalaha eṣiṇaḥ aśokam ca varāśokam sarvartukam atha api ca svargam ca devatā vāsam pūrvadeva vaśa anugāḥ jagat babhūva amararāja duṣṭaiḥ abhidrutam sasyam iva ali vṛndaiḥ Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca aśīleṣu praduṣṭeṣu dānaveṣu durātmasu lokeṣu utsādyamāneṣu tapodhana vaneṣu ca siṃhanāde vyomagānām teṣu bhīteṣu jantuṣu ādityāḥ vasavaḥ sādhyāḥ pitaraḥ marutām gaṇāḥ bhītāḥ śaraṇam ājagmuḥ brahmāṇām prapitāmaham te tam svarṇa utpala āsīnam brahmāṇam samupāgatāḥ nemuḥ ūcuḥ ca sahitāḥ pañcāsyam caturānanam vara guptāḥ tava eva iha dānavāḥ tripura ālayāḥ bādhante asmān yathā preṣyān anuśādhi tatas anagha megha āgame yathā haṃsāḥ mṛgāḥ siṃha bhayāt iva dānavānām bhayāt tadvat bhramāmaḥ hi pitāmaha putrāṇām nāmadheyāni kalatrāṇām tathā eva ca dānavaiḥ bhrāmyamāṇānām vismṛtāni tatas anagha deva veśma prabhaṅgāḥ ca āśrama bhraṃśanāni ca dharṣaṇā anena nirdevam nirmanuṣya āśramam jagat iti evam tridaśaiḥ uktaḥ padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ pratyāha tridaśān sa indrān indu tulya ānanaḥ prabhuḥ tasya antaḥ eṣa samprāptaḥ yaḥ purā uktaḥ mayā surāḥ tat ca teṣām adhiṣṭhānam tripuram tridaśa ṛṣabhāḥ eka iṣu pāta mokṣeṇa hantavyam na iṣu vṛṣṭibhiḥ bhavatām ca na paśyāmi kam api atra sura ṛṣabhāḥ tripuram na alpa vīryeṇa śakyam hantum śareṇa tu ekam muktvā mahādevam maheśānam prajāpatim yācāmaḥ sahitāḥ devam tripuram sa haniṣyati kṛtaḥ purāṇām viṣkambhaḥ yojamānām śatam śatam puṣya yogeṇa yuktāni tāni ca eka kṣaṇena tu pitāmahaḥ ca taiḥ sārdham bhava saṃsadam āgataḥ tam bhavam bhūta bhavya īśam giriśam śūlapāṇinam paśyanti ca umayā sārdham nandinā ca mahātmanā agni varṇam ajam devam agni kuṇḍa nibha īkṣaṇam astuvan gopatim śambhum vara dam pārvatīpatim devāḥ ūcuḥ mahādevāya bhīmāya tryambakāya ca śāntaye īśānāya bhaya ghnāya namaḥ tu andhaka ghātine nīlagrīvāya bhīmāya vedhase vedhasā stute nityam nīlaśikhaṇḍāya śūline divya śāyine vṛṣadhvajāya muṇḍāya jaṭine brahmacāriṇe tapyamānāya salile brahmaṇyāya ajitāya ca viśva ātmane viśva sṛje viśvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhate abhigamyāya kāmyāya stutyāya arcyāya sarvadā Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca prajāpatim uvāca idam devānām kva bhayam mahat tāvat eva prayacchāmi na asti adeyam mayā hi vaḥ yuṣmākam nitarām śam vai kartāham vibudha ṛṣabhāḥ vidviṣṭāḥ vaḥ mama dviṣṭāḥ kaṣṭāḥ kaṣṭa parākramāḥ teṣām abhāvaḥ saṃpādyaḥ yuṣmākam bhavaḥ eva ca evam uktāḥ tu devena premṇā sa brahmakāḥ surāḥ rudram āhuḥ mahābhāgam bhāga arhāḥ sarve eva te asuraiḥ vadhyamānāḥ sma vayam tvām śaraṇam gatāḥ tripuram yena tat durgam kṛtam pāṇḍura gopuram tat āśritya puram durgam dānavāḥ vara nirbhayāḥ bādhante asmān mahādeva preṣyam asvāminam yathā udyānāni ca bhagnāni nandana ādīni yāni ca varāḥ ca apsarasaḥ sarvāḥ rambhā ādyāḥ danujaiḥ hṛtāḥ indrasya vāhyāḥ ca gajāḥ kumuda añjana vāmanāḥ airāvata ādyāḥ apahṛtāḥ devatānām maheśvara jātāḥ ca dānavānām te ratha yogyāḥ turaṃgamāḥ ye rathāḥ ye gajāḥ ca eva yāḥ striyaḥ vasu yat ca naḥ tat naḥ vyapahṛtam daityaiḥ saṃśayaḥ jīvite punar uvāca devān deveśaḥ vara daḥ vṛṣavāhanaḥ digvāsasā tathā uktāḥ te sapitāmahakāḥ surāḥ adhiṣṭhānam śiraḥ meroḥ akṣaḥ mandaraḥ eva ca cakruḥ candram ca sūryam ca cakre kāñcana rājate kṛṣṇapakṣam śuklapakṣam pakṣa dvayam api īśvarāḥ ādi dvayam pakṣa yantram yantram etāḥ ca devatāḥ kambala aśvatarābhyām ca nāgābhyām sama veṣṭitam bhārgavaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ ca eva budhaḥ aṅgārakaḥ eva ca śanaiścaraḥ tathā ca atra sarve te deva sattamāḥ varūtham gaganam cakruḥ cāru rūpam rathasya te kṛtam dvijihva nayanam triveṇum śātakaumbhikam maṇi muktā indranīlaiḥ ca vṛtam hi aṣṭa mukhaiḥ suraiḥ gaṅgā sindhuḥ śatadruḥ ca candrabhāgā irāvatī vitastā ca vipāśā ca yamunā gaṇḍakī tathā etāḥ sarit varāḥ sarvāḥ veṇu saṃjñā kṛtā rathe dhṛtarāṣṭrāḥ ca ye nāgāḥ te ca veśyā ātmakāḥ kṛtāḥ vāsukeḥ kula jāḥ ye ca ye ca raivata vaṃśa jāḥ te sarpāḥ darpa sampūrṇāḥ cāpa tūṇeṣu anūna gāḥ avatasthuḥ śarāḥ bhūtvā nānā jāti śubha ānanāḥ tṛṣā bubhukṣā sarva ugrā mṛtyuḥ sarva śamaḥ tathā brahma vadhyā ca go vadhyā bāla vadhyā prajā bhayāḥ gadā bhūtvā śaktayaḥ ca tadā deva rathe abhyayus yugam kṛta yugam ca atra cāturhotra prayojakāḥ catur varṇāḥ sa līlāḥ ca babhūvuḥ svarṇa kuṇḍalāḥ tat yugam yuga saṃkāśam ratha śīrṣe pratiṣṭhitam dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa nāgena baddham balavatā mahat ṛgvedaḥ sāmavedaḥ ca yajurvedaḥ tathā paraḥ anna dāna purogāṇi yāni dānāni kānicid tāni āsan vājinām teṣām bhūṣaṇāni sahasraśas nāgāḥ babhūvuḥ eva ete hayānām vāla bandhanāḥ oṃkāra prabhavāḥ tāḥ vā mantra yajña kratu kriyāḥ upadravāḥ pratīkārāḥ paśubandha iṣṭayaḥ tathā yajña upavāhāni etāni tasmin loka rathe śubhe maṇi muktā pravālaiḥ tu bhūṣitāni sahasraśas pratodaḥ oṃkāraḥ eva āsīt tad agram ca vaṣaṭkṛtam sinīvālī kuhuḥ rākā tathā ca anumatiḥ śubhā yoktrāṇi āsan turaṃgāṇām apasarpaṇa vigrahāḥ kṛṣṇāni atha ca pītāni śveta māñjiṣṭhakāni ca avadātāḥ patākāḥ tu babhūvuḥ pavana īritāḥ ṛtubhiḥ ca kṛtaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ dhanuḥ saṃvatsaraḥ abhavat ajarā jyā abhavat ca api sā ambikā dhanuṣaḥ dṛḍhā tasmāt umā kālarātriḥ dhanuṣaḥ jyā ajarā bhavat tejasaḥ samavāyaḥ atha ca iṣoḥ tejaḥ tasmin ca vīrya vṛddhi artham vāsukiḥ nāga pārthivaḥ tejaḥ saṃvasana artham vai mumoca ativiṣaḥ viṣam kṛtvā devāḥ ratham ca api divyam divya prabhāvataḥ idam āpad paritrāṇam devān sa indra purogamān praśasya devān sādhu iti ratham paśyati śaṃkaraḥ muhur dṛṣṭvā ratham sādhu sādhu iti uktvā muhur muhur yādṛśaḥ ayam rathaḥ kḷptaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ mama sattamāḥ īdṛśaḥ ratha sampattyā yantā śīghram vidhīyatām avāpuḥ mahatīm cintām katham kāryam iti bruvan muktvā cakra āyudham devam saḥ api asya iṣum samāśritaḥ dhuri yuktāḥ iva ukṣāṇaḥ ghaṭantaḥ iva parvataiḥ aham sārathiḥ iti uktvā jagrāha aśvān tatas agrajaḥ tatas devaiḥ sa gandharvaiḥ siṃha nādaḥ mahān kṛtaḥ pratoda hastam samprekṣya brahmāṇam sūta tām gatam sadṛśaḥ sūtaḥ iti uktvā ca āruroha ratham haraḥ ārohati ratham deve hi aśvāḥ hara bhara āturāḥ jānubhiḥ patitāḥ bhūmau rajaḥ grāsaḥ ca grāsitaḥ devaḥ dṛṣṭvā atha vedān tān bhayāt ujjahāra pitṝn ārtān suputraḥ iva duḥkhitān jaya śabdaḥ ca devānām saṃbabhūva arṇava upamaḥ tat oṃkāra mayam gṛhya pratodam vara daḥ prabhuḥ grasamānāḥ iva ākāśam muṣṇantaḥ iva medinīm mukhebhyaḥ sasṛjuḥ śvāsān ucchvasantaḥ iva uragāḥ vrajanti te aśvāḥ javanāḥ kṣaya kāle iva anilāḥ śeṣaḥ ca bhagavān nāgaḥ anantaḥ ananta karaḥ ariṇām śara hastaḥ ratham pāti śayanam brahmaṇaḥ tadā yamaḥ tūrṇam samāsthāya mahiṣam ca ati dāruṇam draviṇādhipatiḥ vyālam surāṇām adhipaḥ dvipam mayūram śata candram ca kūjantam kiṃnaram yathā nandīśvaraḥ ca bhagavān śūlam ādāya dīptimān pṛṣṭhatas ca api pārśvābhyām lokasya kṣaya kṛt yathā pramathāḥ ca agni varṇa ābhāḥ sa agni jvālāḥ iva acalāḥ anujagmuḥ ratham śārvam nakrāḥ iva mahā arṇavam bhṛguḥ bharadvāja vasiṣṭha gautamāḥ kratuḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ tapodhanāḥ marīciḥ atriḥ bhagavān atha aṅgirāḥ parāśara agastya mukhāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ haram ajitam ajam pratuṣṭuvuḥ vacana viśeṣaiḥ vicitra bhūṣaṇaiḥ Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca īśvara svara ghoṣeṇa nardamāne mahā vṛṣe raṇa aṅgaṇāt samutpatya devarṣiḥ nāradaḥ prabhuḥ kāntyā candra upamaḥ tūrṇam tripuram puram āgataḥ nāradaḥ ca atra bhagavān prādurbhūtaḥ tapodhanaḥ āgatam jalada ābhāsam sametāḥ sarva dānavāḥ uttasthuḥ nāradam dṛṣṭvā abhivādana vādinaḥ tam arghyeṇa ca pādyena madhuparkeṇa ca īśvarāḥ nāradam pūjayāmāsuḥ brahmāṇam iva vāsavaḥ teṣām sa pūjām pūjā arhaḥ pratigṛhya tapodhanaḥ nāradaḥ sukham āsīnaḥ kāñcane parama āsane yathārham dānavaiḥ sārdham āsīnaḥ dānava adhipaḥ āsīnam nāradam prekṣya mayaḥ tu atha mahā asuraḥ abravīt vacanam tuṣṭaḥ hṛṣṭa roma ānana īkṣaṇaḥ dṛśyante bhaya dāḥ svapnāḥ bhajyante ca dhvajāḥ param aṭṭālakāḥ ca nṛtyante sa patākāḥ sa gopurāḥ hiṃsa hiṃsa iti śrūyante giraḥ ca bhaya dāḥ pure na aham bibhemi devānām sa indrāṇām api nārada muktvā ekam vara dam sthāṇum bhakta abhaya karam haram anāgatam atītam ca bhavān jānāti tattvataḥ nāradaḥ uvāca śṛṇu dānava tattvena bhavanti autpātikāḥ yathā saḥ iṣṭa prāpakaḥ dharmaḥ ācāryaiḥ upadiśyate itaraḥ ca aniṣṭa phalaḥ ācāryaiḥ na upadiśyate utpathāt mārgam āgacchet mārgāt ca iva vimārga tām apakāriṣu devānām kuruṣe tvam sahāya tām tat etāni evamādīni utpāta āveditāni ca vaināśikāni dṛśyante dānavānām tathā eva ca eṣa rudraḥ samāsthāya mahā loka mayam ratham āyāti tripuram hantum maya tvām asurān api dānavānām punar devaḥ deveśa padam āgataḥ śūra saṃmatam iti evam dānavān āha dānavaḥ śūrāḥ stha jāta putrāḥ stha kṛtakṛtyāḥ stha dānavāḥ jitvā vayam bhaviṣyāmaḥ sarve amara sabhā sadaḥ devān ca sa indrakān hatvā lokān bhokṣyāmahe asurāḥ aṭṭālakeṣu ca tathā tiṣṭhadhvam śastra pāṇayaḥ daṃśitāḥ yuddha sajjāḥ ca tiṣṭhadhvam prodyata āyudhāḥ purāṇi trīṇi ca etāni yathā sthāneṣu dānavāḥ tiṣṭhadhvam laṅghanīyāni bhaviṣyanti purāṇi ca namaḥ gatāḥ tathā śūrāḥ devatāḥ viditāḥ hi vaḥ tāḥ prayatnena vāryāḥ ca vidāryāḥ ca eva sāyakaiḥ iti danu tanayān mayaḥ tathā uktvā sura gaṇa vāraṇa vāraṇe vacāṃsi yuvati jana viṣaṇṇa mānasam tat tripura puram sahasā viveśa rājā tad abhimatam adāt tatas śaśāṅkī sa ca kila nirbhayaḥ eva dānavaḥ abhūt Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca ilāvṛtam iti khyātam tat varṣam vistṛta āyatam devānām janma bhūmiḥ yā triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā vivāhāḥ kratavaḥ ca eva jātakarma ādikāḥ kriyāḥ devānām yatra vṛttāni kanyā dānāni yāni ca reme nityam bhavaḥ yatra sahāyaiḥ pārṣadaiḥ gaṇaiḥ madhu piṅgala netraḥ tu candra avayava bhūṣaṇaḥ devānām adhipam prāha gaṇapān ca maheśvaraḥ vāsava etat arīṇām te tripuram paridṛśyate vimānaiḥ ca patākābhiḥ dhvajaiḥ ca samalaṃkṛtam idam vṛttam idam khyātam vahni vat bhṛśa tāpanam ete janāḥ giri prakhyāḥ sa kuṇḍala kirīṭinaḥ prākāra gopura aṭṭeṣu kakṣa ante dānavāḥ sthitāḥ ime ca toyada ābhāsāḥ danujāḥ vikṛta ānanāḥ nirgacchanti puras daityāḥ sa āyudhāḥ vijaya eṣiṇaḥ sa tvam sura śataiḥ sārdham sa sahāyaḥ vara āyudhaḥ puras purasya randhra arthī sthāsyāmi vijayāya vaḥ prakrānta ratha bhīmaiḥ taiḥ sa devaiḥ pārṣadām gaṇaiḥ tena nādena tripurāt dānavāḥ yuddha lālasāḥ utpatya dudruvuḥ celuḥ sa āyudhāḥ khe gaṇeśvarān anye payodhara ārāvāḥ payodhara samāḥ babhuḥ sa siṃhanādam vāditram vādayāmāsuḥ uddhatāḥ devānām siṃha nādaḥ ca sarva tūrya ravaḥ mahān candra udayāt samudbhūtaḥ paurṇamāsaḥ iva arṇavaḥ aṭṭālakān samāruhya kecid calita vādinaḥ svarṇa mālā dharāḥ śūrāḥ prabhā sitakara ambarāḥ itas ca itas ca dhāvantaḥ kecid udbhūta vāsasaḥ kim etat iti papracchuḥ anyonyam gṛham āśritāḥ jñāsyase anantareṇa iti kālaḥ vistārataḥ mahān saḥ api asau pṛthvī sāram ca siṃhaḥ ca ratham āsthitaḥ tiṣṭhate tripuram pīḍya deham vyādhiḥ iva ucchritaḥ ehi āyudham ādāya kva me pṛcchā bhaviṣyati iti te anyonyam āviddhāḥ uttara uttara bhāṣiṇaḥ āsādya pṛcchanti tadā dānavāḥ tripura ālayāḥ tāraka ākhya pure daityāḥ tāraka ākhya puraḥsarāḥ nirgatāḥ kupitāḥ tūrṇam bilāt iva mahā uragāḥ niruddhāḥ gaja rājānaḥ yathā kesari yūthapaiḥ darpitānām tatas ca eṣām darpitānām iva agnīnām rūpāṇi jajvaluḥ teṣām agnīnām iva dhamyatām tatas bṛhanti cāpāni bhīma nādāni sarvaśas nikṛṣya jaghnuḥ anyonyam iṣubhiḥ prāṇa bhojanaiḥ mārjāra mṛga bhīma āsyān pārṣadān vikṛta ānanān dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā ahasan uccais dānavāḥ rūpa sampadā bāhubhiḥ parigha ākāraiḥ kṛṣyatām dhanuṣām śarāḥ viviśuḥ taḍāgāni iva pakṣiṇaḥ mṛtāḥ stha kva nu yāsyadhvam haniṣyāmaḥ nivartatām iti evam paruṣāṇi uktvā dānavāḥ pārṣada ṛṣabhān bibhiduḥ sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ sūrya pādāḥ iva ambudān pramathāḥ api siṃha akṣāḥ siṃha vikrānta vikramāḥ khaṇḍa śaila śilā vṛkṣaiḥ bibhiduḥ daitya dānavān vikṛṣṭa cāpāḥ daitya indrāḥ sṛjanti śara durdinam iṣubhiḥ tāḍyamānāḥ te bhūyas bhūyas gaṇeśvarāḥ cakruḥ te deha niryāsam svarṇa dhātum iva acalāḥ tathā vṛkṣa śilā vajra śūla paṭṭi paraśvadhaiḥ cūrṇyante abhihatāḥ daityāḥ kācāḥ ṭaṅka hatāḥ iva candra udayāt samudbhūtaḥ paurṇamāsaḥ iva arṇavaḥ jayati indraḥ ca rudraḥ ca iti eva ca gaṇeśvarāḥ vāritāḥ dāritāḥ bāṇaiḥ yodhāḥ tasmin bala arṇave karaiḥ chinnaiḥ śirobhiḥ ca dhvajaiḥ chattraiḥ ca pāṇḍuraiḥ yuddha bhūmiḥ bhayavatī māṃsa śoṇita pūritā dṛḍha āhatāḥ patan pūrvam dānavāḥ pramathāḥ tathā siddhāḥ ca apsarasaḥ ca eva cāraṇāḥ ca nabhaḥ gatāḥ dṛḍha prahāra hṛṣitāḥ sādhu sādhu iti cukruśuḥ nadantaḥ megha śabdena śarabhāḥ iva roṣitāḥ tāraka ākhya pure tasmin surāḥ śūrāḥ samantataḥ sa śastrāḥ nipatanti sma sa pakṣāḥ iva bhūdharāḥ yodhayanti tri bhāgeṇa tripure tu gaṇeśvarāḥ ādāya parigham ghoram tāḍayāmāsa nandinam sa nandī dānava indreṇa parigheṇa dṛḍha āhataḥ bhramate madhunā vyaktaḥ purā nārāyaṇaḥ yathā nandīśvare gate tatra gaṇapāḥ khyāta vikramāḥ ghaṇṭākarṇaḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ mahākālaḥ ca pārṣadāḥ tatas ca sāyakaiḥ sarvān gaṇapān gaṇapa ākṛtīn bhūyas bhūyas sa vivyādha gaṇeśvara mahattamān saṃjñām prāpya tatas saḥ api vidyunmālinam ādravat papāta vakṣasi tadā vajram daityasya bhīṣaṇam papāta vajra abhihataḥ śakreṇa adriḥ iva āhataḥ cukruśuḥ dānavāḥ prekṣya dudruvuḥ ca gaṇādhipāḥ duḥkha āmarṣita roṣāḥ te vidyunmālini pātite druma śaila mahā vṛṣṭim payodāḥ sasṛjuḥ yathā te pīḍyamānāḥ gurubhiḥ giribhiḥ ca gaṇeśvarāḥ tatas asura varaḥ śrīmān tāraka ākhyaḥ pratāpavān girīṇām vai tulya rūpa dharaḥ babhau bhinna uttamāṅgāḥ gaṇapāḥ bhinna pāda aṅkita ānanāḥ virejuḥ bhujagāḥ mantraiḥ vāryamāṇāḥ yathā tathā mayena māyā vīryeṇa vadhyamānāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ bhramanti bahu śabdālāḥ pañjare śakunāḥ iva tayā asura varaḥ śrīmān tāraka ākhyaḥ pratāpavān dadāha ca balam sarvam śuṣka indhanam iva analaḥ tāraka ākhyena vāryante śara varṣaiḥ tadā gaṇāḥ mayena māyā nihatāḥ tāraka ākhyena ca iṣubhiḥ gaṇeśāḥ vidhurāḥ jātāḥ jīrṇa mūlāḥ yathā drumāḥ bhūyas saṃpatate ca agniḥ grahān grāhān bhujaṃgamān giri indrān ca harīn vyāghrān vṛkṣān sṛmara varṇakān śarabhān aṣṭapādān ca apaḥ pavanam eva ca te tāraka ākhyena mayena māyayā saṃmuhyamānāḥ vivaśāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ na aśaknuvan te manasā api ceṣṭitum yathā indriyārthāḥ muninā abhisaṃyatāḥ mahā jala agni ādi sa kuñjara uragaiḥ hari indra vyāghra ṛkṣa tarakṣu rākṣasaiḥ vibādhyamānāḥ tamasā vimohitāḥ samudra madhyeṣu iva gādha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ saṃmardyamāneṣu gaṇeśvareṣu saṃnardamāneṣu suretareṣu tatas surāṇām pravarā abhirakṣitum ripoḥ balam saṃviviśuḥ saha āyudhāḥ yamaḥ gadā astraḥ varuṇaḥ ca bhāskaraḥ tathā kumāraḥ amara koṭi saṃyutaḥ svayam ca śakraḥ sita nāga vāhanaḥ kulīśa pāṇiḥ sura loka puṃgavaḥ sa ca uḍunāthaḥ sa sutaḥ divākaraḥ sa sa antakaḥ tryakṣa patiḥ mahā dyutiḥ ete ripūṇām prabala abhirakṣitam tadā balam saṃviviśuḥ mada uddhatāḥ yathā vanam darpita kuñjara adhipāḥ yathā nabhaḥ sa ambudharam divākaraḥ kṛta prahāra ātura dīna dānavam tatas tu abhajyanta balam hi pārṣadāḥ svar jyotiṣām jyotiḥ iva ūṣmavān hariḥ yathā tamaḥ ghorataram narāṇām yathā sadā eva niśākaraḥ saṃcita śārvaram tamaḥ diś lokapālaiḥ gaṇanāyakaiḥ ca kṛtaḥ mahān siṃha ravaḥ muhūrtam saṃkhye vibhagnāḥ vikarāḥ vipādāḥ chinna uttamāṅgāḥ śara pūrita aṅgāḥ devetarāḥ deva varaiḥ vibhinnāḥ sīdanti paṅkeṣu yathā gaja indrāḥ vajreṇa bhīmena ca vajrapāṇiḥ śaktyā ca śaktyā ca mayūraketuḥ daṇḍena ca ugreṇa ca dharmarājaḥ pāśena ca ugreṇa ca vāri goptā śūlena kālena ca yakṣa rājaḥ vīryeṇa tejasvi tayā sukeśaḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ te sura saṃnikāśāḥ pūrṇa āhutī sikta śikhi prakāśāḥ śareṇa bhittvā sa hi tārakāsutam sa tāraka ākhya asuram ābabhāṣe kṛtvā prahāram praviśāmi vīram puram hi daitya indra balena yuktaḥ viśrāmam ūrjaskaram api avāpya punar kariṣyāmi raṇam prapannaiḥ vayam hi śastra kṣata vikṣata aṅgāḥ viśīrṇa śastra dhvaja varma vāhāḥ jaya eṣiṇaḥ te jaya kāśinaḥ ca gaṇeśvarāḥ loka vara adhipāḥ ca mayasya śrutvā divi tāraka ākhyaḥ vacaḥ abhikāṅkṣan kṣataja upama akṣaḥ viveśa tūrṇam tripuram diteḥ sutaiḥ sutaiḥ adityāḥ yudhi vṛddha harṣaiḥ tatas sa śaṅkha ānaka bheri bhīmam sa siṃhanādam hara sainyam ābabhau maya anugam ghora gabhīra gahvaram yathā siṃha nāditam Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca mayaḥ prahāram kṛtvā tu māyāvī dānava ṛṣabhaḥ viveśa tūrṇam tripuram abhram nīlam iva ambaram sa dīrgham uṣṇam niḥśvasya dānavān vīkṣya madhya gān dadhyau loka kṣaye prāpte kālam kālaḥ iva aparaḥ sa ca api nidhanam prāptaḥ vidyunmālī mahā yaśāḥ tasya api eṣaḥ anayaḥ prāptaḥ na durgam kāraṇam kvacid kāle kruddhe katham kālāt trāṇam naḥ adya bhaviṣyati laṅghane kaḥ samarthaḥ syāt ṛte devam maheśvaram svāmī ca eṣām tu devānām durjayaḥ sa maheśvaraḥ tat adya darśayiṣyāmi yāvat vīrāḥ samantataḥ vāpīm amṛta toyena pūrṇām srakṣye vara oṣadhīḥ jīviṣyanti tadā daityāḥ saṃjīvana vara auṣadhaiḥ iti saṃcintya balavān mayaḥ māyāvinām varaḥ māyayā sasṛje vāpīm rambhām iva pitāmahaḥ dvi yojana āyatām dīrghām pūrṇa yojana vistṛtām āroha saṃkramavatīm citra rūpām kathām iva indoḥ kiraṇa kalpena mṛṣṭena amṛta gandhinā pūrṇām parama toyena guṇa pūrṇām iva aṅganām utpalaiḥ kumudaiḥ padmaiḥ vṛtām kādambakaiḥ tathā candra bhāskara varṇa ābhaiḥ bhīmaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ vṛtām kāma eṣibhiḥ iva ākīrṇām jīvānām araṇīm iva tām vāpīm sṛjya sa mayaḥ gaṅgām iva maheśvaraḥ tasyām prakṣālayāmāsa vidyunmālinam āditas sa vāpyām majjitaḥ daityaḥ deva śatruḥ mahā balaḥ mayasya ca añjalim kṛtvā tāraka ākhyaḥ abhivāditaḥ vidyunmālī iti vacanam mayam utthāya ca abravīt yudhyāmaḥ arīn viniṣpīḍya dayā deheṣu kā hi naḥ taiḥ vā vinihatāḥ yuddhe bhaviṣyāmaḥ yama aśanāḥ tam pariṣvajya sa ārdra akṣaḥ idam āha mahā asuraḥ mahā amṛta mayī vāpī hi eṣā māyābhiḥ īśvara sṛṣṭā dānava daityānām hatānām jīva vardhinī diṣṭyā tvām daitya paśyāmi yama lokāt iha āgatam dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā ca tām vāpīm māyayā maya nirmitām hṛṣṭa ānana akṣāḥ daitya indrāḥ idam vacanam abruvan dānavāḥ yudhyata idānīm pramathaiḥ saha nirbhayāḥ mayena nirmitā vāpī hatān saṃjīvayiṣyati tatas kṣubdha ambudhi nibhā bherī sā tu bhayaṃkarī vādyamānā nanāda uccais rauravī sā punar punar śrutvā bherī ravam ghoram megha ārambhita saṃnibham nyapatan asurāḥ tūrṇam tripurāt yuddha lālasāḥ loha rājata sauvarṇaiḥ kaṭakaiḥ maṇi rājitaiḥ āmuktaiḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ hāraiḥ mukuṭaiḥ api ca utkaṭaiḥ dhūmāyitāḥ hi aviramāḥ jvalantaḥ iva pāvakāḥ āyudhāni samādāya kāśinaḥ dṛḍha vikramāḥ nṛtyamānāḥ iva naṭāḥ garjantaḥ iva toyadāḥ kara ucchrayāḥ iva gajāḥ siṃhāḥ iva ca nirbhayāḥ hradāḥ iva ca gambhīrāḥ sūryāḥ iva pratāpitāḥ pramathāḥ api sa utsāhāḥ garuḍa utpāta pātinaḥ yuyutsavaḥ abhidhāvanti dānavān dānava arayaḥ nandīśvareṇa pramathāḥ tāraka ākhyena dānavāḥ cakruḥ saṃhatya saṃgrāmam codyamānāḥ balena ca te asibhiḥ candra saṃkāśaiḥ śūlaiḥ ca anala piṅgalaiḥ śarāṇām sṛjyamānānām asīnām ca nipātyatām rūpāṇi āsan mahā ulkānām patantīnām iva ambarāt śaktibhiḥ bhinna hṛdayāḥ nirdayāḥ iva pātitāḥ nirayeṣu iva nirmagnāḥ kūjante pramatha asurāḥ hema kuṇḍala yuktāni kirīṭa utkaṭavanti ca śirāṃsi urvyām patanti sma giri kūṭāḥ iva atyaye paraśvadhaiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ ca khaḍgaiḥ ca parighaiḥ tathā chinnāḥ kari vara ākārāḥ nipetuḥ te dharā tale garjanti sahasā hṛṣṭāḥ pramathāḥ bhīma garjanāḥ iti ca uccārayan vācam vāraṇāḥ raṇa dhūrgatāḥ parighaiḥ āhatāḥ kecid dānavaiḥ śaṃkara anugāḥ vamante rudhiram vaktraiḥ svarṇa dhātum iva acalāḥ pramathaiḥ api nārācaiḥ asurāḥ sura śatravaḥ drumaiḥ ca giri śṛṅgaiḥ ca gāḍham eva āhave hatāḥ sūditān atha tān daityān anye dānava puṃgavāḥ utkṣipya cikṣipuḥ vāpyām maya dānava coditāḥ te ca api bhāsvaraiḥ dehaiḥ svarga loke iva amarāḥ uttasthuḥ vāpīm āsādya sat rūpa ābharaṇa ambarāḥ atha eke dānavāḥ prāpya vāpī prakṣepaṇāt asūn āsphoṭya siṃhanādam ca kṛtvā adhāvan tathā asurāḥ dānavāḥ pramathān etān prasarpata kim āsatha evam śrutvā śaṅkukarṇaḥ vacaḥ agra graha saṃnibhaḥ sūditāḥ sūditāḥ deva pramathaiḥ asurāḥ hi amī uttiṣṭhanti punar bhīmāḥ sasyāḥ iva jala ukṣitāḥ asmin kila pure vāpī pūrṇa amṛta rasa ambhasā nihatāḥ nihatāḥ yatra kṣiptāḥ jīvanti dānavāḥ iti vijñāpayat devam śaṅkukarṇaḥ maheśvaram abhavan dānava bale utpātāḥ vai su dāruṇāḥ tāraka ākhyaḥ su bhīma akṣaḥ dārita āsyaḥ hariḥ yathā dānavāḥ niḥsṛtāḥ dṛṣṭvā devadeva rathe suram bhūkampaḥ ca abhavat tatra śatāṅgaḥ bhū gataḥ abhavat dṛṣṭvā kṣobham agāt rudraḥ svayambhūḥ ca pitāmahaḥ tābhyām deva variṣṭhābhyām anvitaḥ sa ratha uttamaḥ anāyatanam āsādya sīdate guṇavān iva ujjahāra mahā prāṇaḥ ratham trailokya rūpiṇam tadā śarāt viniṣpatya pīta vāsāḥ janārdanaḥ vṛṣa rūpam mahat kṛtvā ratham jagrāha durdharam sa viṣāṇābhyām trailokyam ratham eva mahā rathaḥ abhyadravat tadā devam brahmāṇam hatavān ca saḥ sa tāraka ākhya abhihataḥ pratodam nyasya kūbare tāraka ākhyasya pūjā artham kṛtaḥ jaladhara upamaḥ ratha caraṇa karaḥ atha mahā mṛdhe vṛṣabha vapuḥ vṛṣabha indra pūjitaḥ sa jala jalada rājitām samastām kumuda vara utpala phulla paṅkaja āḍhyām vāpīm pītvā asura indrāṇām pīta vāsāḥ janārdanaḥ nardamānaḥ mahā bāhuḥ praviveśa śaram tatas tatas asurāḥ bhīma gaṇeśvaraiḥ hatāḥ prahāra saṃvardhita śoṇita āpagāḥ parāṅmukhāḥ bhīma mukhaiḥ kṛtāḥ raṇe yathā naya abhyudyata tatparaiḥ naraiḥ puram parāvṛtya nu te śara arditāḥ yathā śarīram pavana udaye gatāḥ gaṇeśvara abhyudyata darpa kāśinaḥ mahā indra nandīśvara ṣaṇmukhāḥ yudhi Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca śīrṇa daṃṣṭrāḥ yathā nāgāḥ bhagna śṛṅgāḥ yathā vṛṣāḥ yathā vipakṣāḥ śakunāḥ nadyaḥ kṣīṇa udakāḥ yathā mṛta prāyāḥ tathā daityāḥ daivataiḥ vikṛta ānanāḥ atha tān mlāna manasaḥ tadā tāmarasa ānanaḥ uvāca daityaḥ daityānām parama adhipatiḥ mayaḥ kṛtvā yuddhāni ghorāṇi pramathaiḥ saha sa amaraiḥ yūyam yat prathamam daityāḥ paścāt ca bala pīḍitāḥ praviṣṭāḥ nagaram trāsāt pramathaiḥ bhṛśa marditāḥ yatra nāma mahābhāgāḥ praviśanti gireḥ vanam babhūvuḥ niṣprabhāḥ daityāḥ grahāḥ indu udaye yathā vāpī pālāḥ tatas abhyetya nabhaḥ kāle iva ambudāḥ mayam āhuḥ yama prakhyam sāñjali pragrahāḥ sthitāḥ yā sā amṛta rasā gūḍhā vāpī vai nirmitā tvayā samākula utpala vanā samīna ākula
