sarve vigata mṛtyavaḥ upāsanti mahātmānam sarve divya paricchadāḥ vimānaiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ bhrājamānaiḥ iva agnibhiḥ mahā indra vapuṣaḥ sarve vicitra aṅgada bāhavaḥ bhūṣita aṅgāḥ diteḥ putrāḥ tam upāsanta sarvaśas tasyām sabhāyām divyāyām asurāḥ parvata upamāḥ hiraṇya vapuṣaḥ sarve divākara sama prabhāḥ na śrutam na eva dṛṣṭam hi hiraṇyakaśipoḥ yathā sa dadarśa mṛgādhipaḥ sabhāyām sura cita ratna gavākṣa śobhitāyām kanaka vimala hāra bhūṣita aṅgam dititanayam sa mṛgādhipaḥ dadarśa Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca tatas dṛṣṭvā mahātmānam kālacakram iva āgatam hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ prahlādaḥ nāma vīryavān divyena cakṣuṣā siṃham apaśyat devam āgatam te dṛṣṭvā rukma śaila ābham apūrvām tanum āśritam vismitāḥ dānavāḥ sarve hiraṇyakaśipuḥ ca saḥ prahlādaḥ uvāca mahā bāho mahā rāja daityānām ādi saṃbhava na śrutam na ca no dṛṣṭam nārasiṃham idam vapuḥ daitya anta karaṇam ghoram manaḥ mama asya devāḥ śarīra sthāḥ sāgarāḥ saritaḥ ca yāḥ himavān pāriyātraḥ ca ye ca anye kulaparvatāḥ dhanadaḥ varuṇaḥ ca eva yamaḥ śakraḥ śacīpatiḥ marutaḥ deva gandharvāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ nāgāḥ yakṣāḥ piśācāḥ ca rākṣasāḥ bhīma vikramāḥ sthāvarāṇi ca sarvāṇi jaṅgamāni tathā eva ca bhavān ca sahitaḥ asmābhiḥ sarvaiḥ daitya gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ vimāna śata saṃkīrṇā tathā eva bhavataḥ sabhā sarvam tribhuvanam rājan loka dharmāḥ ca śāśvatāḥ prajāpatiḥ ca atra manuḥ mahātmā grahāḥ ca yogāḥ ca mahīruhāḥ ca utpāta kālaḥ ca dhṛtiḥ matiḥ ca ratiḥ ca satyam ca tapaḥ damaḥ ca sanatkumāraḥ ca mahā anubhāvaḥ viśve ca devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca sarve prahlādasya vacaḥ śrutvā hiraṇyakaśipuḥ prabhuḥ uvāca dānavān sarvān gaṇān ca sa gaṇa adhipaḥ mṛgendraḥ gṛhyatām eṣa apūrvām tanum āsthitaḥ yadi vā saṃśayaḥ kaścid vadhyatām vanagocaraḥ te dānava gaṇā sarve mṛgendram bhīma vikramam parikṣipantaḥ muditāḥ trāsayāmāsuḥ ojasā siṃha nādam vimucya atha narasiṃhaḥ mahā balaḥ babhañja tām sabhām divyām vyādita āsyaḥ iva antakaḥ sabhāyām bhajyamānāyām hiraṇyakaśipuḥ svayam cikṣepa astrāṇi siṃhasya roṣāt vyākula locanaḥ sarva astrāṇām atha jyeṣṭham daṇḍa mantram su dāruṇam kālacakram tathā aghoram viṣṇucakram tathā param vicitrām aśanīm ca eva śuṣka ārdram ca aśani dvayam raudram tathā ugram śūlam ca kaṅkālam musalam tathā mohanam śoṣaṇam ca eva saṃtāpana vilāpanam tathā apratihatām śaktim krauñcam astram tathā eva ca astram brahmaśiraḥ ca eva soma astram śiśiram tathā kampanam śātanam ca eva tvāṣṭram ca eva su bhairavam saṃvartanam mohanam ca tathā māyā dharam param prasvāpanam pramathanam vāruṇam ca astram uttamam astram pāśupatam ca eva yasya apratihatā gatiḥ nārāyaṇa astram aindram ca sārpam astram tathā adbhutam paiśācam astram ajitam śoṣa dam śāmanam tathā etāni astrāṇi divyāni hiraṇyakaśipuḥ tadā astraiḥ prajvalitaiḥ siṃham āvṛṇot asura uttamaḥ sa hi amarṣa anila udbhūtaḥ daityānām sainya sāgaraḥ kṣaṇena plāvayāmāsa mainākam iva sāgaraḥ prāsaiḥ pāśaiḥ ca khaḍgaiḥ ca gadābhiḥ musalaiḥ tathā śataghnībhiḥ ca dīptābhiḥ daṇḍaiḥ api su dāruṇaiḥ te dānavāḥ pāśa gṛhīta hastāḥ mahā indra tulya aśani vajra vegāḥ samantataḥ abhyudyata bāhu kāyāḥ sthitāḥ tri śīrṣāḥ iva nāgapāśāḥ suvarṇa mālā ākula bhūṣita aṅgāḥ pīta aṃśuka ābhoga vibhāvita aṅgāḥ muktā āvalī dāma sanātha kakṣāḥ haṃsāḥ iva ābhānti viśāla pakṣāḥ teṣām tu vāyu pratimā ojasām vai keyūra maulī valaya utkaṭānām tāni uttamāṅgāni abhitas vibhānti prabhāta sūrya aṃśu sama prabhāṇi giriḥ yathā saṃtata varṣibhiḥ ghanaiḥ kṛta andhakāra antara kaṃdaraḥ drumaiḥ na akampata ājau bhagavān pratāpa sthitaḥ prakṛtyā himavān iva acalaḥ saṃtrāsitāḥ tena nṛsiṃha rūpiṇā diteḥ sutāḥ pāvaka tulya tejasā bhayāt viceluḥ pavana uddhuta aṅgāḥ yathā ūrmayaḥ sāgara vāri saṃbhavāḥ Purāṇa sūtaḥ uvāca kharāḥ khara mukhāḥ ca eva makara āśīviṣa ānanāḥ īhāmṛga mukhāḥ ca anye varāha mukha saṃsthitāḥ bāla sūrya mukhāḥ ca anye dhūmaketu mukhāḥ tathā haṃsa kukkuṭa vaktrāḥ ca vyādita āsyāḥ bhaya āvahāḥ siṃha āsyāḥ lelihānāḥ ca kāka gṛdhra mukhāḥ tathā dvi jihvakāḥ vakra śīrṣāḥ tathā ulkāmukha saṃsthitāḥ mahā grāha mukhāḥ ca anye dānavāḥ bala darpitāḥ śaila saṃvarṣmaṇaḥ tasya śarīre śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ evam bhūyas aparān ghorān asṛjan dānava īśvarāḥ te dānava śarāḥ ghorāḥ dānava indra samīritāḥ tatas cakrāṇi divyāni daityāḥ krodha samanvitāḥ mṛgendrāya asṛjan āśu jvalitāni samantataḥ tāni sarvāṇi cakrāṇi mṛgendreṇa mahātmanā grastāni udīrṇāni tadā pāvaka arciḥ samāni vai tāni cakrāṇi vadane viśamānāni bhānti vai hiraṇyakaśipuḥ daityaḥ bhūyas prāsṛjat ūrjitām śaktim prajvalitām ghorām dhauta śastra taḍit prabhām tām āpatantīm samprekṣya mṛgendraḥ śaktim ujjvalām huṃkāreṇa eva raudreṇa babhañja bhagavān tadā rarāja bhagnā sā śaktiḥ mṛgendreṇa mahī tale nārāca paṅktiḥ siṃhasya prāptā reje avidūrataḥ nīlotpala palāśānām mālā iva ujjvala darśanā tat sainyam utsāritavān tṛṇa agrāṇi iva mārutaḥ tatas aśma varṣam daitya indrāḥ vyamṛjanta nabhaḥ gatāḥ naga mātraiḥ śilā khaṇḍaiḥ giri śṛṅgaiḥ mahā prabhaiḥ diśaḥ daśa vikīrṇāḥ vai khadyota prakarāḥ iva tadā aśma oghaiḥ daitya gaṇāḥ punar siṃham ariṃdamam chādayāṃcakrire meghāḥ dhārābhiḥ iva parvatam dhārābhiḥ akṣa mātrābhiḥ prādurāsīt samantataḥ nabhasaḥ pracyutāḥ dhārāḥ tigma vegāḥ samantataḥ āvṛtya sarvatas vyoma diśaḥ ca tathā dhārāḥ divi ca sarvatra vasudhāyām ca sarvaśas na spṛśanti ca tāḥ devam nipatantyaḥ aniśam bhuvi bāhyatas vavṛṣuḥ varṣam na upariṣṭāt ca vavṛṣuḥ saḥ asṛjat dānavaḥ māyām agni vāyu samīritām mahā indraḥ toyadaiḥ sārdham sahasrākṣaḥ mahā dyutiḥ mahatā toya varṣeṇa śamayāmāsa pāvakam tasyām pratihatāyām tu māyāyām yudhi dānavaḥ asṛjat ghora saṃkāśam tamaḥ tīvram samantataḥ tamasā saṃvṛte loke daityeṣu ātta āyudheṣu ca tri śikhām bhrukuṭīm ca asya dadṛśuḥ dānavāḥ raṇe lalāṭa sthām triśūla aṅkām gaṅgām tripathagām iva tatas sarvāsu māyāsu hatāsu diti nandanāḥ hiraṇyakaśipum daityam vivarṇāḥ śaraṇam yayuḥ parāvahaḥ saṃvahaḥ ca mahā bala parākramāḥ tathā parivahaḥ śrīmān utpāta bhaya śaṃsinaḥ iti evam kṣubhitāḥ sapta marutaḥ gaganecarāḥ ayogataḥ ca api acarat mārgam niśi niśācaraḥ sagrahaḥ saha nakṣatraiḥ ākāpatiḥ ariṃdamaḥ vivarṇa tām ca bhagavān gataḥ divi divākaraḥ kṛṣṇam kabandham ca tathā lakṣyate su mahat divi amuñcat ca arciṣām vṛndam bhūmi vṛttiḥ vibhāvasuḥ gagana sthaḥ ca bhagavān abhīkṣṇam paridṛśyate sapta dhūmra nibhāḥ ghorāḥ sūryāḥ divi samutthitāḥ somasya gagana sthasya grahāḥ tiṣṭhanti śṛṅga gāḥ vāme tu dakṣiṇe ca eva sthitau śukra bṛhaspatī śanaiścaraḥ lohitāṅgaḥ jvalana aṅga sama dyutiḥ śṛṅgāṇi śanakais ghorāḥ yuga anta āvartinaḥ grahāḥ carācara vināśāya rohiṇīm na abhyanandata gṛhītaḥ rāhuṇā candraḥ ulkābhiḥ abhihanyate devānām api yaḥ devaḥ saḥ api avarṣata śoṇitam apatan gaganāt ulkāḥ vidyut rūpāḥ mahā svanāḥ latāḥ ca saphalāḥ sarvāḥ ye ca āhuḥ daityanāśanam phalaiḥ phalāni ajāyanta puṣpaiḥ puṣpam tathā eva ca āraṇyaiḥ saha saṃsṛṣṭāḥ grāmyāḥ ca mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ nadyaḥ ca pratikūlāni vahanti kaluṣa udakāḥ na prakāśanti ca diśaḥ rakta reṇu samākulāḥ vānaspatyaḥ na pūjyante pūjana arhāḥ kathaṃcana yadā ca sarva bhūtānām chāyā na parivartate aparāhṇa gate sūrye lokānām yuga saṃkṣaye bhāṇḍa āgāra āyudha āgāre niviṣṭam abhavat madhu asurāṇām vināśāya surāṇām vijayāya ca dṛśyante vividha utpātāḥ ghorāḥ ghora nidarśanāḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ ghora utpātāḥ samutthitāḥ daitya indrasya vināśāya dṛśyante kāla nirmitāḥ medinyām kampamānāyām daitya indreṇa mahātmanā mahīdharāḥ nāga gaṇāḥ nipetuḥ amita ojasaḥ catur śīrṣāḥ pañca śīrṣāḥ sapta śīrṣāḥ ca pannagāḥ elāmukhaḥ kāliyaḥ ca mahāpadmaḥ ca vīryavān sahasra śīrṣā nāgaḥ vai hema tāla dhvajaḥ prabhuḥ śeṣaḥ anantaḥ mahābhāgaḥ duṣprakampyaḥ prakampitaḥ dīptāni antar jala sthāni pṛthivīdharaṇāni ca nāgāḥ tejaḥ dharāḥ ca api pātāla tala cāriṇaḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ daityaḥ tadā saṃspṛṣṭavān mahīm saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭaḥ krodhāt vārāhaḥ iva pūrvajaḥ nadī bhāgīrathī ca eva sarayūḥ kauśikī tathā yamunā tu atha kāverī kṛṣṇaveṇā ca nimnagā suveṇā ca mahābhāgā nadī godāvarī tathā carmaṇvatī ca sindhuḥ ca tathā nada nadīpatiḥ narmadā śubha toyā ca tathā vetravatī nadī gomatī go kula ākīrṇā tathā pūrva sarasvatī mahī kālamahī ca eva tamasā puṣpavāhinī suvarṇa prakaṭam ca eva suvarṇa ākara maṇḍitam mahānadam ca lauhityam śaila kānana śobhitam pattanam kośa karaṇam ṛṣi vīra jana ākaram māgadhāḥ ca mahāgrāmāḥ muṇḍāḥ śuṅgāḥ tathā eva ca suhmāḥ mallāḥ videhāḥ ca mālavāḥ kāśi kosalāḥ kailāsa śikhara ākāram yat kṛtam viśvakarmaṇā suvarṇa vedikaḥ śrīmān megha paṅkti niṣevitaḥ bhrājamānaḥ arka sadṛśaiḥ jātarūpa mayaiḥ drumaiḥ śālaiḥ tālaiḥ tamālaiḥ ca karṇikāraiḥ ca puṣpitaiḥ ayomukhaḥ ca vikhyātaḥ parvataḥ dhātu maṇḍitaḥ surāṣṭrāḥ ca sa bāhlīkāḥ śūra ābhīrāḥ tathā eva ca bhojāḥ pāṇḍyāḥ ca vaṅgāḥ ca kaliṅgāḥ tāmraliptakāḥ tathā eva auṇḍrāḥ ca pauṇḍrāḥ ca vāmacūḍāḥ sa keralāḥ kṣobhitāḥ tena daityena sa devāḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃghaḥ ca viprakīrṇam manoharam jātarūpa mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ apsaraḥ gaṇa nāditam giri puṣpitakaḥ ca eva lakṣmīvān priya darśanaḥ utthitaḥ sāgaram bhittvā viśrāmaḥ candra sūryayoḥ rarāja su mahā śṛṅgaiḥ gaganam vilikhan iva candra sūrya aṃśu saṃkāśaiḥ sāgara ambu samāvṛtaiḥ vidyutvān sarvatas śrīmān āyataḥ śata yojanam vidyutām yatra saṃpātāḥ nipātyante naga uttame ṛṣabhaḥ parvataḥ ca eva śrīmān vṛṣabha saṃjñitaḥ kuñjaraḥ parvataḥ śrīmān yatra agastya gṛham śubham viśālākṣaḥ ca durdharṣaḥ sarpāṇām ālayaḥ purī tathā bhogavatī ca api daitya indreṇa abhikampitā mahāsenaḥ giriḥ ca eva pāriyātraḥ ca parvataḥ cakravān ca giri śreṣṭhaḥ vārāhaḥ ca eva parvataḥ prāgjyautiṣa puram ca api jātarūpa mayam śubham yasmin vasati duṣṭa ātmā narakaḥ nāma dānavaḥ meghaḥ ca parvata śreṣṭhaḥ megha gambhīra niḥsvanaḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ tatra sahasrāṇi parvatānām dvijottamāḥ taruṇa āditya saṃkāśaḥ meruḥ tatra mahā giriḥ kampitam mānasam ca eva haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākulam triśṛṅga parvataḥ ca eva kumārī ca sarit varā tuṣāra caya saṃchannaḥ mandaraḥ ca api parvataḥ uśīrabinduḥ ca giriḥ candraprasthaḥ tathā adrirāj krauñcaḥ saptarṣi śailaḥ ca dhūmravarṇaḥ ca parvataḥ nadyaḥ sa sāgarāḥ sarvāḥ saḥ akampayata dānavaḥ kapilaḥ ca mahīputraḥ vyāghravān ca eva kampitaḥ khecarāḥ ca satī putrāḥ pātāla tala vāsinaḥ gaṇaḥ tathā paraḥ raudraḥ megha nāma aṅkuśa āyudhaḥ ūrdhva gaḥ bhīma vegaḥ ca sarvaḥ eva abhikampitāḥ gadī śūlī karālaḥ ca hiraṇyakaśipuḥ tadā jīmūta ghana saṃkāśaḥ jīmūta ghana niḥsvanaḥ jīmūta ghana nirghoṣaḥ jīmūtaḥ iva vegavān deva ariḥ ditijaḥ vīraḥ nṛsiṃham samupādravat samutpatya tatas tīkṣṇaiḥ mṛgendreṇa mahā nakhaiḥ mahī ca kālaḥ ca śaśī nabhaḥ ca grahāḥ ca sūryaḥ ca diśaḥ ca sarvāḥ nadyaḥ ca śailāḥ ca mahā arṇavāḥ ca gatāḥ prasādam diti putra nāśāt tatas pramuditāḥ devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ nāmabhiḥ divyaiḥ ādidevam sanātanam yat tvayā vihitam deva nārasiṃham idam vapuḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ bhavān kartā vikartā ca lokānām prabhavaḥ avyayaḥ parām ca siddhim ca param ca devam param ca mantram paramam haviḥ ca param ca dharmam paramam ca viśvam tvām āhuḥ agryam puruṣam purāṇam param śarīram paramam ca brahma param ca yogam paramām ca vāṇīm param rahasyam paramām gatim ca tvām āhuḥ agryam puruṣam purāṇam param parasya api param ca bhūtam tvām āhuḥ agryam puruṣam purāṇam param parasya api param mahat yat tvām āhuḥ agryam puruṣam purāṇam param parasya api param ca dāntam tvām āhuḥ agryam puruṣam purāṇam stutvā nārāyaṇam devam brahma lokam gataḥ prabhuḥ tatas nadatsu tūryeṣu nṛtyantīṣu apsaraḥsu ca kṣīrodasya uttaram kūlam jagāma hariḥ īśvaraḥ nārasiṃham vapuḥ devaḥ sthāpayitvā su dīptimat paurāṇam rūpam āsthāya prayayau garuḍadhvajaḥ aṣṭa cakreṇa yānena bhūta yutena bhāsvatā Purāṇa ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kathitam narasiṃhasya māhātmyam vistareṇa ca katham ca vaiṣṇavī sṛṣṭiḥ padma madhye abhavat purā sūtaḥ uvāca śrutvā ca narasiṃhasya māhātmyam ravinandanaḥ jala arṇava gatasya iha nābhau jātam janārdana puṣkare ca katham bhūtāḥ devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ purā etat ākhyāhi nikhilam yogam yoga vidām pate śṛṇvataḥ tasya me kīrtim na tṛptiḥ upajāyate kiyatā vā atha kālena hi uttiṣṭhati mahā yaśāḥ ke prajāpatayaḥ tāvat āsan pūrvam mahā mune katham nirmitavān ca eva citram lokam sanātanam katham ekārṇave śūnye naṣṭa sthāvara jaṅgame naṣṭa anila anale loke naṣṭa ākāśa mahī tale vibhuḥ mahābhūta patiḥ mahā tejāḥ mahā ākṛtiḥ āste sura vara śreṣṭhaḥ vidhim āsthāya yoga vid śṛṇuyām parayā bhaktyā brahman etat aśeṣataḥ vaktum arhasi dharmiṣṭha yaśaḥ nārāyaṇa ātmakam śraddhayā ca upaviṣṭānām bhagavan vaktum arhasi nārāyaṇasya yaśasaḥ śravaṇe yā tava spṛhā tat vaṃśya anvaya bhūtasya nyāyyam ravi kula ṛṣabha śṛṇuṣva ādi purāṇeṣu vedebhyaḥ ca yathā śrutam brāhmaṇānām ca vadatām śrutvā vai su mahātmanām yathā ca tapasā dṛṣṭvā bṛhaspati sama dyutiḥ parāśara sutaḥ śrīmān guruḥ dvaipāyanaḥ abravīt tat te aham kathayiṣyāmi yathāśakti yathāśruti yat vijñātum mayā śakyam ṛṣi mātreṇa sattamāḥ kaḥ samutsahate jñātum param nārāyaṇa ātmakam tat karma viśva vedānām tat rahasyam mahā ṛṣīṇām tam īśam sarva yajñānām tat tattvam sarva darśinām tat adhyātma vidām cintyam narakam ca vikarmiṇām tat bhūtam adhibhūtam ca tat param parama ṛṣīṇām yaḥ kartā kārakaḥ buddhiḥ manaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ eva ca praṇavaḥ puruṣaḥ śāstā ekaḥ ca iti vibhāvyate prāṇaḥ pañcavidhaḥ ca eva dhruvaḥ akṣaraḥ eva ca kālaḥ pākaḥ ca paktā ca draṣṭā svādhyāyaḥ eva ca saḥ asmān kārayate sarvān saḥ atyeti vyākulīkṛtān yajāmahe tam eva ādyam tam eva icchāma nirvṛtāḥ yāḥ kathāḥ ca eva vartante śrutayaḥ vā atha tad parāḥ viśvam viśvapatiḥ yaḥ ca sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ Purāṇa catvāri āhuḥ sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām tu kṛtam yugam tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā dviguṇā ravinandana svadharma niratāḥ santaḥ jāyante yatra mānavāḥ viprāḥ sthitāḥ dharma parāḥ rāja vṛttau sthitāḥ nṛpāḥ kṛṣyām abhiratāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ śuśrūṣavaḥ sthitāḥ etat kārtayugam vṛttam sarveṣām api pārthiva prāṇinām dharma saṅgānām api vai nīca janmanām trīṇi varṣa sahasrāṇi tretā yugam iha ucyate tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā dviguṇā parikīrtyate dvābhyām adharmaḥ pādābhyām tribhiḥ dharmaḥ vyavasthitaḥ tretāyām vikṛtim yānti varṇāḥ tu ete na saṃśayaḥ cāturvarṇyasya vaikṛtyāt yānti daurbalyam āśramāḥ dvāparasya tu yā ceṣṭā tām api śrotum arhasi dvāparam dve sahasre tu varṣāṇām ravinandana tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā dviguṇā yugam ucyate tatra ca artha parāḥ sarve prāṇinaḥ rajasā hatāḥ sarve naiṣkṛtikāḥ kṣudrāḥ jāyante ravinandana tathā varṣa sahasram tu varṣāṇām dve śate api saṃdhyayā saha saṃkhyātam krūram kali yugam smṛtam yatra adharmaḥ catuṣpādaḥ syāt dharmaḥ pāda vigrahaḥ kāminaḥ tapasā hīnāḥ jāyante tatra mānavāḥ nāstikāḥ brahma bhaktāḥ vā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ahaṃkāra gṛhītāḥ ca prakṣīṇa sneha bandhanāḥ viprāḥ śūdra samācārāḥ santi sarve kalau yuge āśramāṇām viparyāsaḥ kalau samparivartate varṇānām ca eva saṃdehaḥ yuga ante ravinandana vidyāt dvādaśasāhasrīm yuga ākhyām pūrva nirmitām śarīra nirvṛtim dṛṣṭvā loka saṃhāra buddhitaḥ devatānām ca sarvāsām brahma ādīnām mahīpate daityānām dānavānām ca yakṣa rākṣasa pakṣiṇām gandharvāṇām apsarasām bhujaṃgānām ca pārthiva parvatānām nadīnām ca paśūnām ca eva sattama tiryagyoni gatānām ca sattvānām kṛmiṇām tathā mahābhūta patiḥ pañca hṛtvā bhūtāni bhūta kṛt jagat saṃharaṇa arthāya kurute vaiśasam mahat bhūtvā sūryaḥ cakṣuṣī ca ādadānaḥ bhūtvā vāyuḥ prāṇinām prāṇa jālam Purāṇa bhūtvā nārāyaṇaḥ yogī sattva mūrtiḥ vibhāvasuḥ gabhastibhiḥ pradīptābhiḥ saṃśoṣayati sāgarān tatas pītvā arṇavān sarvān nadīḥ kūpān ca sarvaśas parvatānām ca salilam sarvam ādāya raśmibhiḥ bhittvā gabhastibhiḥ ca eva mahīm gatvā rasātalāt vāyuḥ ca balavān bhūtvā vidhunvānaḥ akhilam jagat prāṇa apāna samāna ādyān vāyūn ākarṣate hariḥ tatas deva gaṇāḥ sarve bhūtāni eva ca yāni tu gandhaḥ ghrāṇam śarīram ca pṛthivīm saṃśritāḥ guṇāḥ jihvā rasaḥ ca snehaḥ ca saṃśritāḥ salile guṇāḥ rūpam cakṣuḥ vipākaḥ ca jyotiḥ eva āśritāḥ guṇāḥ sparśaḥ prāṇaḥ ca ceṣṭā ca pavane saṃśritāḥ guṇāḥ śabdaḥ śrotram ca khāni eva gagane saṃśritāḥ guṇāḥ loka māyā bhagavatā muhūrtena vināśitā manaḥ buddhiḥ ca sarveṣām kṣetrajñaḥ ca iti yaḥ śrutaḥ tam vareṇyam parameṣṭhī hṛṣīkeśam upāśritaḥ vāyunā ākramyamāṇāsu druma śākhāsu ca āśritaḥ teṣām saṃgharṣaṇa udbhūtaḥ pāvakaḥ śatadhā jvalan adahat ca tadā sarvam vṛtaḥ saṃvartakaḥ analaḥ sa parvata drumān gulmān latā vallīḥ tṛṇāni ca vimānāni ca divyāni purāṇi vividhāni ca yāni ca āśrayaṇīyāni tāni sarvāṇi saḥ adahat bhasmīkṛtya tatas sarvān lokān lokaguruḥ hariḥ bhūyas nirvāpayāmāsa yuga antena ca karmaṇā sahasra vṛṣṭiḥ śatadhā bhūtvā kṛṣṇaḥ mahā balaḥ tatas kṣīra nikāyena svādunā parama ambhasā tena rodhena saṃchannā payasām varṣataḥ dharā sarva sattva vivarjitā naṣṭa arka pavana ākāśe sūkṣme jagati saṃvṛte saṃśoṣam ātmanā kṛtvā samudrān api dehinaḥ dagdhvā saṃplāvya ca tathā svapiti ekaḥ sanātanaḥ paurāṇam rūpam āsthāya svapiti amita vikramaḥ eka arṇava jala vyāpī yogī yogam upāśritaḥ anekāni sahasrāṇi yugāni eka arṇava ambhasi kaḥ ca eva puruṣaḥ nāma kiṃyogaḥ kaḥ ca yogavān asau kiyantam kālam ca ekārṇava vidhim prabhuḥ na draṣṭā na eva gamitā na jñātā na eva pārśvagaḥ nabhaḥ kṣitim pavanam apaḥ prakāśakam prajāpatim bhuvana dharam sura īśvaram pitāmaham śruti nilayam mahā munim praśāmya bhūyas śayanam hi arocayat Purāṇa evam ekārṇavībhūte śete loke mahā dyutiḥ pracchādya salilena urvīm haṃsaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ tadā virajaskam mahā bāhum akṣayam brahma yat viduḥ ātma rūpa prakāśena tamasā saṃvṛtaḥ prabhuḥ yāthātathyam param jñānam bhūtam tat brahmaṇā purā rahasi āraṇyaka uddiṣṭam yat ca aupaniṣadam smṛtam yaḥ ca anyaḥ puruṣa ākhyaḥ syāt saḥ eṣa puruṣottamaḥ ye ca yajña karāḥ viprāḥ ye ca ṛtvijaḥ iti smṛtāḥ asmāt eva purā bhūtāḥ yajñebhyaḥ śrūyatām tathā brahmāṇam prathamam vaktrāt udgātāram ca sāmagam hotāram api ca adhvaryum bāhubhyām asṛjat prabhuḥ brahmaṇaḥ brāhmaṇācchaṃsi prastotāram ca sarvaśas tau mitrāvaruṇau pṛṣṭhāt pratiprastāram eva ca udarāt pratihartāram potāram ca eva pārthiva acchāvākam atha ūrubhyām neṣṭāram ca eva pārthiva pāṇibhyām atha ca āgnīdhram subrahmaṇyam ca jānutaḥ grāvastutam tu pādābhyām unnetāram ca yājuṣam evam eva eṣa bhagavān ṣoḍaśa eva jagatpatiḥ pravaktṝn sarva yajñānām ṛtvijaḥ asṛjat uttamān tat eṣa vai veda mayaḥ puruṣaḥ yajña saṃjñitaḥ vedāḥ ca etad mayāḥ sarve sa aṅga upaniṣada kriyāḥ svapiti ekārṇave ca eva yat āścaryam abhūt purā śrūyatām tat yathā viprāḥ mārkaṇḍeya kutūhalam gīrṇaḥ bhagavataḥ tasya kukṣau eva mahā muniḥ aṭan tīrtha prasaṅgena pṛthivīm tīrtha gocarām āśramāṇi ca puṇyāni devatāyatanāni ca deśān rāṣṭrāṇi citrāṇi purāṇi vividhāni ca japa homa paraḥ śāntaḥ tapaḥ ghoram samāsthitaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ tatas tasya śanais vaktrāt viniḥsṛtaḥ sa niṣkrāman na ca ātmānam jānīte deva māyayā tasya utpannam bhayam tīvram saṃśayaḥ ca ātma jīvite deva darśana saṃhṛṣṭaḥ vismayam paramam gataḥ cintayan jala madhya sthaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ viśaṅkitaḥ vyaktam anyatamaḥ bhāvaḥ teṣām saṃbhāvitaḥ mama na hi īdṛśam jagat kleśam ayuktam satyam arhati naṣṭa candra arka pavane naṣṭa parvata bhū tale śarvaryām jāgratam iva bhāsantam svena tejasā devam draṣṭum iha āyātaḥ kaḥ bhavān iti vismayāt sampraviṣṭaḥ punar kukṣim mārkaṇḍeyaḥ ati vismayaḥ sa tathā eva yathāpūrvam yaḥ dharām aṭate purā puṇya tīrtha jala upetām vividhāni āśramāṇi ca kratubhiḥ yajamānāḥ ca samāpta vara dakṣiṇān apaśyat deva kukṣi sthān yājakān śataśas dvijān sat vṛttam āsthitāḥ sarve varṇāḥ brāhmaṇa pūrvakāḥ catvāraḥ ca āśramāḥ samyak yathā uddiṣṭāḥ mayā tava evam varṣa śatam sāgram mārkaṇḍeyasya dhīmataḥ carataḥ pṛthivīm sarvām na kukṣi antaḥ samīkṣitaḥ suptam nyagrodha śākhāyām bālam ekam niraikṣata tathā eva ekārṇava jale nīhāreṇa āvṛta ambare sa muniḥ vismaya āviṣṭaḥ kautūhala samanvitaḥ bālam āditya saṃkāśam na aśaknot abhivīkṣitum pūrva dṛṣṭam idam mene śaṅkitaḥ deva māyayā agādha salile tasmin mārkaṇḍeyaḥ sa vismayaḥ sa tasmai bhagavān āha svāgatam bāla yogavān mārkaṇḍeyaḥ muniḥ tu āha bālam tam śrama pīḍitaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca kaḥ mām nāmnā kīrtayati tapaḥ paribhavan mama na hi eṣa vaḥ samācāraḥ deveṣu api mama ucitaḥ mām brahmā api hi deveśaḥ dīrgha āyuḥ iti bhāṣate mārkaṇḍeya iti mām uktvā mṛtyum īkṣitum arhati sūtaḥ uvāca evam ābhāṣya tam krodhāt mārkaṇḍeyaḥ mahā muniḥ tathā eva bhagavān bhūyas babhāṣe madhusūdanaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca aham te janakaḥ vatsa hṛṣīkeśaḥ pitā guruḥ āyuṣpradātā paurāṇaḥ kim mām tvam na upasarpasi mām putra kāmaḥ prathamam pitā te aṅgirasaḥ muniḥ pūrvam ārādhayāmāsa tapaḥ tīvram samāśritaḥ tatas tvām ghora tapasā prāvṛṇot amita ojasam kaḥ samutsahate ca anyaḥ yaḥ na bhūta ātmaka ātmajaḥ draṣṭum ekārṇava gatam krīḍantam yoga vartmanā mūrdhni baddha añjali puṭaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ mahā tapāḥ nāma gotre tatas procya dīrgha āyuḥ loka pūjitaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca iccheyam tattvataḥ māyām imām jñātum tava anagha yat ekārṇava madhya sthaḥ śeṣe tvam bāla rūpavān kiṃsaṃjñaḥ ca eva bhagavān loke vijñāyase prabho tarkaye tvām mahātmānam kaḥ hi anyaḥ sthātum arhati śrī bhagavān uvāca aham nārāyaṇaḥ brahman sarva bhūta vināśanaḥ aham sahasra śīrṣa ākhyaḥ yaḥ padaiḥ abhisaṃjñitaḥ aham indra pade śakraḥ varṣāṇām parivatsaraḥ aham sarvāṇi sattvāni daivatāni akhilāni tu bhujaṃgānām aham śeṣaḥ tārkṣyaḥ vai sarva pakṣiṇām kṛtāntaḥ sarva bhūtānām viśveṣām kāla saṃjñitaḥ aham dharmaḥ tapaḥ ca aham sarva āśrama nivāsinām aham ca eva sarit divyā kṣīrodaḥ ca mahā arṇavaḥ aham ijyā kriyā ca aham aham vidyādhipaḥ smṛtaḥ aham jyotiḥ aham vāyuḥ aham bhūmiḥ aham nabhaḥ aham āpaḥ samudrāḥ ca nakṣatrāṇi diśaḥ daśa aham varṣam aham somaḥ parjanyaḥ aham aham raviḥ kṣīroda sāgare ca aham samudre vaḍavāmukhaḥ vahniḥ saṃvartakaḥ bhūtvā piban toya mayam haviḥ aham purāṇaḥ paramam tathā eva aham parāyaṇam yat kiṃcid paśyase vipra yat śṛṇoṣi ca kiṃcana viśvam sṛṣṭam mayā pūrvam sṛjyam ca adya api paśya mām yuge yuge ca srakṣyāmi mārkaṇḍeya akhilam jagat tat etat akhilam sarvam mārkaṇḍeya avadhāraya śuśrūṣuḥ mama dharmān ca kukṣau cara sukham mama mama brahmā śarīra sthaḥ devaiḥ ca ṛṣibhiḥ saha evamādi purāṇa īśaḥ vadan eva mahāmatiḥ vaktram āhṛtavān āśu mārkaṇḍeyam mahā munim tatas bhagavataḥ kukṣim praviṣṭaḥ muni sattamaḥ Purāṇa āpavaḥ sa vibhuḥ bhūtvā cārayāmāsa vai tapaḥ chādayitvā ātmanaḥ deham yādasām kula saṃbhavam mahatām pañcabhūtānām viśvaḥ viśvam acintayat īṣat saṃkṣobhayāmāsa saḥ arṇavam salila āśrayaḥ śabdam prati tadā udbhūtaḥ mārutaḥ chidra saṃbhavaḥ vivardhatā balavatā vegāt vikṣobhitaḥ arṇavaḥ kṛṣṇavartmā samabhavat prabhuḥ vaiśvānaraḥ mahān tatas saṃśoṣayāmāsa pāvakaḥ salilam bahu ātma teja udbhavāḥ puṇyāḥ āpaḥ amṛta rasa upamāḥ ākāśam chidra sambhūtam vāyuḥ ākāśa saṃbhavaḥ ābhyām saṃgharṣaṇa udbhūtam pāvakam vāyu saṃbhavam dṛṣṭvā prītaḥ mahādevaḥ mahā bhūta vibhāvanaḥ dṛṣṭvā bhūtāni bhagavān loka sṛṣṭi artham uttamam yat pṛthivyām dvijendrāṇām tapasā bhāvitātmanām jñānam vṛṣṭam tu viśva arthe yoginām yāti mukhya tām tam yogavantam vijñāya sampūrṇa aiśvaryam uttamam padmam nābhi udbhavam ca ekam samutpāditavān tadā sahasra parṇam virajam bhāskara ābham hiraṇmayam Purāṇa atha yogavatām śreṣṭham asṛjat bhūri tejasam sraṣṭāram sarva lokānām brahmāṇam sarvatomukham tat ca padmam purāṇa jñāḥ pṛthivī rūpam uttamam nārāyaṇa samudbhūtam pravadanti mahā ṛṣayaḥ yā padmā sā rasā devī pṛthivī paricakṣyate kailāsam muñjavantam ca tathā anyam gandhamādanam ete deva gaṇānām ca siddhānām ca mahātmanām āśrayāḥ puṇya śīlānām sarva kāma phala pradāḥ eteṣām antare deśaḥ jambūdvīpaḥ iti smṛtaḥ jambūdvīpasya saṃsthānam yajñiyāḥ yatra vai kriyāḥ divyāḥ tīrtha śata ādhārāḥ su ramyāḥ saritaḥ smṛtāḥ smṛtāni yāni padmasya kesarāṇi samantataḥ asaṃkhyeyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ te viśve vai dhātu parvatāḥ yāni padmasya parṇāni bhūrīṇi tu narādhipa te durgamāḥ śaila citāḥ mleccha deśāḥ vikalpitāḥ yāni adhobhāga parṇāni te nivāsāḥ tu bhāgaśas daityānām uragāṇām ca pataṅgānām ca pārthiva teṣām mahā arṇavaḥ yatra tat rasa iti abhisaṃjñitam mahāpātaka karmāṇaḥ majjante yatra mānavāḥ proktā atha dikṣu sarvāsu catvāraḥ salila ākarāḥ evam nārāyaṇasya arthe mahī puṣkara saṃbhavā prādurbhāvaḥ api ayam tasmāt nāmnā puṣkara saṃjñitaḥ etasmāt kāraṇāt tad jñaiḥ purāṇaiḥ parama ṛṣibhiḥ yājñikaiḥ veda dṛṣṭāntaiḥ yajñe padma vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ evam bhagavatā tena viśveṣām dhāraṇā vidhiḥ parvatānām nadīnām ca hradānām ca eva nirmitaḥ śanais svayaṃbhūḥ śayanam sṛjat tadā jagat mayam padma vidhim mahā arṇave Purāṇa divya rakta ambara dharau śveta dīpta ugra daṃṣṭriṇau mahā vivṛta tāmra akṣau pīna uraskau mahā bhujau nava megha pratīkāśau āditya sadṛśa ānanau vidyut ābhau gadā agrābhyām karābhyām ati bhīṣaṇau tau pādayoḥ tu vinyāsāt utkṣipantau iva arṇavam kampayantau iva harim śayānam madhusūdanam yoginām śreṣṭham āsādya dīptam dadṛśatuḥ tadā nārāyaṇa samājñātam sṛjantam akhilāḥ prajāḥ daivatāni ca viśvāni mānasān asurān ṛṣīn dīptau mumūrṣū saṃkruddhau roṣa vyākulita īkṣaṇau kaḥ tvam puṣkara madhya sthaḥ sita uṣṇīṣaḥ catur bhujaḥ ādhāya niyamam mohāt āste tvam vigata jvaraḥ āvābhyām param īśābhyām aśaktaḥ tvam iha arṇave kaḥ sraṣṭā kaḥ ca te goptā kena nāmnā vidhīyase madhu kaiṭabhau ūcatuḥ āvābhyām chādyate viśvam tamasā rajasā atha vai rajaḥ tamaḥ mayau āvām ṛṣīṇām avalaṅghitau āvābhyām uhyate lokaḥ duṣkarābhyām yuge yuge āvām arthaḥ ca kāmaḥ ca yajñaḥ svarga parigrahaḥ sukham yatra mudā yuktam yatra śrīḥ kīrtiḥ eva ca yeṣām yat kāṅkṣitam ca eva tat tat āvām vicintaya yatnāt yogavataḥ dṛṣṭyā yogaḥ pūrvam mayā arjitaḥ tam samādhāya guṇavat sattvam ca asmi samāśritaḥ rajasaḥ tamasaḥ ca eva yaḥ sraṣṭā viśva saṃbhavaḥ tatas bhūtāni jāyante sāttvikāni itarāṇi ca saḥ eva hi yuvām na aṃśe vaśī devaḥ haniṣyati bāhum nārāyaṇaḥ brahmā kṛtavān ātma māyayā kṛṣyamāṇau tatas tasya bāhunā bāhuśālinaḥ tatas tau āhatuḥ gatvā tadā devam sanātanam padmanābham hṛṣīkeśam praṇipatya sthitau ubhau jānīvaḥ tvām viśva yonim tvām ekam puruṣottamam tvam āvām pāhi hetu artham idam nau buddhi kāraṇam amogha darśanaḥ sa tvam yatas tvām vidvaḥ śāśvatam tatas tvām āgatau āvām abhitas prasamīkṣitum śrī bhagavān uvāca madhu kaiṭabhau ūcatuḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca bāḍham yuvām tu pravarau bhaviṣyat kāla saṃbhave varam pradāya atha mahā asurābhyām sanātanaḥ viśva varaḥ surottamaḥ Purāṇa ūrdhvabāhuḥ mahā tejāḥ tapaḥ ghoram samāśritaḥ babhāse sarva dharma sthaḥ sahasrāṃśuḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ atha anyat rūpam āsthāya śaṃbhuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ avyayaḥ ājagāma mahā tejāḥ yoga ācāryaḥ mahā yaśāḥ sāṃkhya ācāryaḥ hi matimān kapilaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ varaḥ parāvara viśeṣa jñau pūjitau ca mahā ṛṣibhiḥ brahma ātma dṛḍha bandhaḥ ca viśālaḥ jagat āsthitaḥ grāmaṇīḥ sarva bhūtānām brahmā trailokya pūjitaḥ trīn imān kṛtavān lokān yathā iyam brahmaṇaḥ śrutiḥ putram ca śaṃbhave ca ekam samutpāditavān ṛṣiḥ saḥ utpanna mātraḥ brahmāṇam uktavān mānasaḥ sutaḥ kim kurmaḥ tava sāhāyyam bravītu bhagavān ṛṣiḥ śuśrūṣuḥ asmi yuvayoḥ kim karomi kṛtāñjaliḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca yat satyam akṣaram brahma hi aṣṭādaśavidham tu tat saṃkalpayitvā manasā tam eva ca mahāmanāḥ tatas saḥ atha abravīt vākyam kim karomi pitāmaha pitāmaha samājñātaḥ brahmāṇam samupasthitaḥ brahma abhyāsam tu kṛtavān bhuvaḥ ca pṛthivīm gataḥ prāptaḥ ca paramam sthānam sa tayoḥ pārśvam āgataḥ mokṣa pravṛtti kuśalam bhūrbhuvam nāmataḥ vibhum evam putrāḥ trayaḥ api ete uktāḥ śaṃbhoḥ mahātmanaḥ tān gṛhītvā sutān tasya prayātaḥ sva arjitām gatim nārāyaṇaḥ ca bhagavān kapilaḥ ca yati īśvaraḥ tatas ghoratamam bhūyas saṃśritaḥ paramam vratam śarīra ardhāt tatas bhāryām samutpāditavān śubhām sadṛśīm ātmanaḥ devīm samarthām loka sarjane tatas jagāda tripadām gāyatrīm veda pūjitām sṛjan prajānām patayaḥ sāgarān ca asṛjat vibhuḥ aparān ca eva caturaḥ vedān gāyatri saṃbhavān ātmanaḥ sadṛśān putrān asṛjat vai pitāmahaḥ viśve prajānām patayaḥ yebhyaḥ lokāḥ viniḥsṛtāḥ viśveśam prathamam tāvat mahā tāpasam ātmajam sarva mantra hitam puṇyam nāmnā dharmam sa sṛṣṭavān vasiṣṭham gautamam ca eva bhṛgum aṅgirasam manum atha eva adbhutam iti ete jñeyāḥ paitāmaha ṛṣayaḥ trayodaśa guṇam dharmam ālabhanta mahā ṛṣayaḥ aditiḥ ditiḥ danuḥ kālā anāyuḥ siṃhikā muniḥ dakṣasya apatyam etāḥ vai kanyāḥ dvādaśa pārthiva marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ putraḥ tapasā nirmitaḥ kila tasmai kanyāḥ dvādaśa anyāḥ dakṣaḥ tāḥ pradadau tadā nakṣatrāṇi ca somāya tadā vai dattavān ṛṣiḥ rohiṇī ādīni sarvāṇi puṇyāni ravinandana lakṣmīḥ marutvatī sādhyā viśveśā ca matā śubhā devī sarasvatī ca eva brahmaṇā nirmitāḥ purā etāḥ pañca variṣṭhāḥ vai suraśreṣṭhāya pārthiva dattā bhadrāya dharmāya brahmaṇā dṛṣṭa karmaṇā yā tu rūpavatī patnī brahmaṇaḥ kāmarūpiṇī surabhiḥ sā hitā bhūtvā brahmāṇam samupasthitā jajñire ca sutāḥ tasyām vipulāḥ dhūma saṃnibhāḥ nakta saṃdhyā abhra saṃkāśāḥ prādahan tigma tejasaḥ rodanāt ravaṇāt ca eva rudrāḥ iti tatas smṛtāḥ nirṛtiḥ ca eva śaṃbhuḥ vai tṛtīyaḥ ca aparājitaḥ mṛgavyādhaḥ kapardī ca dahanaḥ atha īśvaraḥ ca vai ahirbudhnyaḥ ca bhagavān kapālī ca api piṅgalaḥ senānīḥ ca mahātejāḥ rudrāḥ tu ekādaśa smṛtāḥ tasyām eva surabhyām ca gāvaḥ yajña īśvarāḥ ca vai prakṛṣṭāḥ ca tathā māyāḥ surabhyāḥ paśavaḥ akṣarāḥ ajāḥ ca eva tu haṃsāḥ ca tathā eva amṛtam uttamam oṣadhyaḥ pravarāyāḥ ca samutthitāḥ dharmāt lakṣmīḥ tathā kāmam sādhyā sādhyān vyajāyata bhavam ca prabhavam ca eva hi īśam ca asuḥ aham tathā aruṇam ca aruṇim ca eva viśvāvasu bala dhruvau haviṣyam ca vitānam ca vidhāna śamitau api vatsaram ca eva bhūtim ca sarva asura niṣūdanam suparvāṇam bṛhat kāntiḥ sādhyāḥ loka namaskṛtāḥ vāsava anugatā devī janayāmāsa vai surān viśvāvasum tṛtīyam ca caturtham somam īśvaram saptamam ca tathā vāyum aṣṭamam nirṛtim vasum viśve devāḥ ca viśvāyām dharmāt jātāḥ iti śrutiḥ dakṣaḥ ca eva mahābāhuḥ puṣkara svanaḥ eva ca viśrāntaka vapurbālaḥ viṣkambhaḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ viśvān devān deva mātā viśveśā janayat sutān amaram śaravṛṣṭim ca sukarṣam ca mahā bhujam virājam ca eva vācam ca viśvāvasu matim tathā aśvamitram citraraśmim tathā niṣadhanam nṛpa hūyantam vāḍavam ca eva cāritram mandapannagam bṛhantam vai bṛhadrūpam tathā vai pūtanā anugam marutvatī purā jajñe etān vai marutām gaṇān aditiḥ kaśyapāt jajñe ādityān dvādaśa eva hi indraḥ viṣṇuḥ bhagaḥ tvaṣṭā varuṇaḥ hi aryamā raviḥ pūṣā mitraḥ ca dhanadaḥ dhātā parjanyaḥ eva ca iti ete dvādaśa ādityāḥ variṣṭhāḥ tridivaukasaḥ tapaḥ śreṣṭhau guṇa śreṣṭhau tridivasya api saṃmatau danuḥ tu dānavān jajñe ditiḥ daityān vyajāyata kālā tu vai kālakeyān asurān surasā tu vai anāyuṣāyāḥ tanayāḥ vyādhayaḥ su mahā balāḥ siṃhikā graha mātā vai gandharva jananī muniḥ tāmrā tu apsarasām mātā puṇyānām bhārata udbhava krodhāyāḥ sarva bhūtāni piśācāḥ ca eva pārthiva jajñe yakṣa gaṇān ca eva rākṣasān ca viśām pate catuṣpadāni sattvāni tathā gāvaḥ tu saurabhāḥ suparṇān pakṣiṇaḥ ca eva vinatā ca vyajāyata mahīdharān sarva nāgān devī kadrūḥ vyajāyata evam vṛddhim samagaman viśve lokāḥ paraṃtapa tadā vai pauṣkaraḥ rājan prādurbhāvaḥ mahātmanaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ pauṣkaraḥ te mayā dvaipāyana īritaḥ purāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ ca eva mayā viṣṇuḥ hariḥ prabhuḥ yaḥ ca idam agryam śṛṇuyāt purāṇam sadā naraḥ parvasu gauraveṇa cakṣuṣā manasā vācā karmaṇā ca caturvidham prasādayati yaḥ kṛṣṇam tam kṛṣṇaḥ anuprasīdati kṣīṇa āyuḥ labhate ca āyuḥ putra kāmaḥ sutam tathā yajñāḥ vedāḥ tathā kāmāḥ tapāṃsi vividhāni ca prāpnoti vividham puṇyam viṣṇu bhaktaḥ dhanāni ca sarvam vihāya yaḥ imam paṭhet pauṣkarakam hareḥ prādurbhāvam nṛpa śreṣṭha na tasya hi aśubham bhavet eṣa pauṣkarakaḥ nāma prādurbhāvaḥ mahātmanaḥ kīrtitaḥ te mahābhāga vyāsa śruti nidarśanāt Purāṇa viṣṇu tvam śṛṇu viṣṇoḥ ca hari tvam ca kṛte yuge vaikuṇṭha tvam ca deveṣu kṛṣṇa tvam mānuṣeṣu ca īśvarasya hi tasya eṣā karmaṇām gahanā gatiḥ saṃprati atītān bhavyān ca śṛṇu rājan yathātatham eṣa nārāyaṇaḥ bhūtvā hariḥ āsīt sanātanaḥ brahmā vāyuḥ ca somaḥ ca dharmaḥ śakraḥ bṛhaspatiḥ eṣa viṣṇuḥ iti khyātaḥ indrasya avarajaḥ vibhuḥ vadha artham sura śatrūṇām daitya dānava rakṣasām pradhāna ātmā purā hi eṣa brahmāṇam asṛjat prabhuḥ saḥ asṛjat pūrvapuruṣaḥ purākalpe prajāpatīn asṛjat mānavān tatra brahma vaṃśān anuttamān etat āścarya bhūtasya viṣṇoḥ karma anukīrtanam kīrtanīyasya lokeṣu kīrtyamānam nibodha me āsīt trailokya vikhyātaḥ saṅgrāmaḥ tārakā mayaḥ yatra te dānavāḥ ghorāḥ sarve saṅgrāma durjayāḥ ghnanti deva gaṇān sarvān sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasān te vadhyamānāḥ vimukhāḥ kṣīṇa praharaṇāḥ raṇe trātāram manasā jagmuḥ devam nārāyaṇam prabhum etasmin antare meghāḥ nirvāṇa aṅgāra varcasaḥ caṇḍāḥ vidyut gaṇa upetāḥ ghora nirhrāda kāriṇaḥ anyonya vega abhihatāḥ pravavuḥ saha mārutāḥ vajra vega anala anilaiḥ arūpavanti rūpāṇi tasmin utpāta lakṣaṇe jātam ca niṣprabham sarvam na prājñāyata kiṃcana viveśa rūpiṇī kālī kāla megha avaguṇṭhitā dyauḥ na bhāti abhibhūta arkā ghoreṇa tamasā āvṛtā tān ghana oghān sa timirān dorbhyām ākṣipya sa prabhuḥ vapuḥ saṃdarśayāmāsa divyam kṛṣṇa vapuḥ hariḥ balāhaka añjana nibham balāhaka tanūruham tejasā vapuṣā ca eva kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇam iva acalam dīpta pīta ambara dharam tapta kāñcana bhūṣaṇam dhūma andhakāra vapuṣam yugānta agnim iva utthitam catur dviguṇa pīna aṃsam kirīṭa channa mūrdhajam nandaka ānandita karam śara āśīviṣa dhāriṇam viṣṇu śailam kṣamā mūlam śrīvṛkṣam śārṅga śṛṅgiṇam vidyā ahaṃkāra sāra āḍhyam mahābhūta prarohaṇam sāgara ākāra nirhrādam rasātala mahā āśrayam mṛgendra pāśaiḥ vitatam pakṣa jantu niṣevitam śīla artha cāru gandha āḍhyam sarva loka mahā drumam vimāna vihaga vyātam toyada āḍambara ākulam jantu matsya gaṇa ākīrṇam śaila śaṅkha kulaiḥ yutam vīravṛkṣa latā gulmam bhujaga utkṛṣṭa śaivalam dvādaśa arka mahā dvīpam rudra ekādaśa pattanam daitya rakṣaḥ gaṇa grāham yakṣa uraga jhaṣa ākulam pitāmaha mahā vīryam sarva strī ratna śobhitam śrī kīrti kānti lakṣmībhiḥ nadībhiḥ upaśobhitam tam tu yoga mahā pāram nārāyaṇa mahā arṇavam anugraha karam devam praśānti karaṇam śubham te kṛtāñjalayaḥ sarve devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ jayaśabdam puraskṛtya śaraṇyam śaraṇam gatāḥ sa teṣām tām giram śrutvā viṣṇuḥ daivata daivatam manaḥ cakre vināśāya dānavānām mahā mṛdhe ākāśe tu sthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ uttamam vapuḥ āsthitaḥ uvāca devatāḥ sarvāḥ sapratijñam idam vacaḥ śāntim vrajata bhadram vaḥ mā bhaiṣṭa marutām gaṇāḥ jitāḥ me dānavāḥ sarve trailokyam parigṛhyatām te tasya satya saṃdhasya viṣṇoḥ vākyena toṣitāḥ devāḥ prītim samājagmuḥ prāśya amṛtam iva uttamam tatas tamaḥ saṃhṛtam tat vineśuḥ ca balāhakāḥ pravavuḥ ca śivāḥ vātāḥ praśāntāḥ ca diśaḥ daśa śuddha prabhāṇi jyotīṃṣi somaḥ cakruḥ pradakṣiṇām na vigraham grahāḥ cakruḥ praśāntāḥ ca api sindhavaḥ virajaskāḥ abhavan mārgāḥ nāka varga ādayaḥ trayaḥ yathārtham ūhuḥ saritaḥ na api cukṣubhire arṇavāḥ āsan śubhāni indriyāṇi narāṇām antarātmasu mahā ṛṣayaḥ vīta śokāḥ vedān uccais adhīyata yajñeṣu ca haviḥ pākam śivam āpa ca pāvakaḥ pravṛtta dharmāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ lokāḥ mudita mānasāḥ Purāṇa tatas abhayam viṣṇu vacaḥ śrutvā daityāḥ ca dānavāḥ kiṅkiṇī jāla nirghoṣam dvīpi carma pariṣkṛtam ruciram ratna jālaiḥ ca hema jālaiḥ ca śobhitam īhāmṛga gaṇa ākīrṇam pakṣi paṅkti virājitam divya astra tūṇīra dharam payodhara vināditam gadā parigha sampūrṇam mūrtimantam iva arṇavam hema keyūra valayam svarṇa maṇḍala kūbaram yuktam ṛkṣa sahasreṇa samṛddha ambuda nāditam dīptam ākāśa gam divyam ratham para ratha arujam adhyatiṣṭhat raṇa ākāṅkṣī merum dīptaḥ iva aṃśumān śaila ākāram asaṃbādham nīlāñjana caya upamam kārṣṇāyasa mayam divyam loha īṣā ābaddha kūbaram loha jālena mahatā sa gavākṣeṇa daṃśitam āyasaiḥ parighaiḥ pūrṇam kṣepaṇīyaiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ prāsaiḥ pāśaiḥ ca vitataiḥ a saṃyuktaiḥ ca kaṇṭakaiḥ śobhitam trāsa yānaiḥ ca tomaraiḥ ca paraśvadhaiḥ pramukhe tasya sainyasya dīpta śṛṅgaḥ iva acalaḥ syandanam vāhayāmāsa sapatna anīka mardanaḥ kharaḥ tu vikṣaran darpāt netrābhyām roṣa jam jalam sphurat danta uṣṭha nayanaḥ saṅgrāmam saḥ abhyakāṅkṣata tvaṣṭā tu aṣṭa gajam ghoram yānam āsthāya dānavaḥ vyūhitum dānava vyūham paricakrāma vīryavān vipracitti sutaḥ śvetaḥ śveta kuṇḍala bhūṣaṇaḥ śveta śaila pratīkāśaḥ yuddhāya abhimukhe sthitaḥ ariṣṭaḥ bali putraḥ ca variṣṭhaḥ adri śilā āyudhaḥ kiśoraḥ tu ati saṃharṣāt kiśoraḥ iti coditaḥ sa balāḥ dānavāḥ ca eva saṃnahyante yathākramam lambaḥ tu nava megha ābhaḥ pralamba ambara bhūṣaṇaḥ daitya vyūha gataḥ bhāti sa nīhāraḥ iva aṃśumān svarbhānuḥ āsya yodhī tu daśana uṣṭha īkṣaṇa āyudhaḥ hasan tiṣṭhati daityānām pramukhe sa mahā grahaḥ siṃha vyāghra gatāḥ ca anye varāha ṛkṣeṣu ca apare kecid khara uṣṭra yātāraḥ kecid śvāpada vāhanāḥ pattinaḥ tu apare daityāḥ bhīṣaṇāḥ vikṛta ānanāḥ eka pāda ardha pādāḥ ca nanṛtuḥ yuddha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ āsphoṭayantaḥ bahavaḥ kṣveḍantaḥ ca tathā pare hṛṣṭa śārdūla nirghoṣāḥ neduḥ dānava puṃgavāḥ te gadā parighaiḥ ugraiḥ śilā musala pāṇayaḥ pāśaiḥ prāsaiḥ ca parighaiḥ tomara aṅkuśa paṭṭiśaiḥ cikrīḍuḥ te śataghnībhiḥ śatadhāraiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ gaṇḍaśailaiḥ ca śailaiḥ ca parighaiḥ ca uttama āyasaiḥ Purāṇa surāṇām api sainyasya vistāram vaiṣṇavam śṛṇu sa balāḥ sa anugāḥ ca eva saṃnahyanta yathākramam grāmaṇīḥ sarva devānām āruroha sura dvipam dīptimadbhiḥ sadasyaiḥ ca brahmarṣibhiḥ abhiṣṭutaḥ yam ārūḍhaḥ sa bhagavān paryeti sakalam jagat svarge śakra anuyāteṣu deva tūrya ninādiṣu sundaryaḥ parinṛtyanti śataśas apsarasām gaṇāḥ ketunā nāga rājena rājamānaḥ yathā raviḥ tasthau sura gaṇa anīke daityān nādena bhīṣayan kālapāśān samāvidhyan hayaiḥ śaśi kara upamaiḥ vāyu īritaiḥ jala ākāraiḥ kurvan līlāḥ sahasraśas pāṇḍura uddhūta vasanaḥ pravāla rucira aṅgadaḥ maṇi śyāma uttama vapuḥ hari bhāra arpitaḥ varaḥ varuṇaḥ pāśa dhṛk madhye deva anīkasya tasthivān yakṣa rākṣasa sainyena guhyakānām gaṇaiḥ api yuktaḥ ca śaṅkha padmābhyām nidhīnām adhipaḥ prabhuḥ rājarāja īśvaraḥ śrīmān gadā pāṇiḥ adṛśyata sa rāja rājaḥ śuśubhe yuddha arthī naravāhanaḥ ukṣāṇam āsthitaḥ saṃkhye sākṣāt iva śivaḥ svayam pūrvapakṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ pitṛrājaḥ tu dakṣiṇaḥ varuṇaḥ paścimam pakṣam uttaram naravāhanaḥ caturṣu yuktāḥ catvāraḥ lokapālāḥ mahā balāḥ sūryaḥ sapta aśva yuktena rathena amita gāminā śriyā jājvalyamānena dīpyamānaiḥ ca raśmibhiḥ cacāra madhye lokānām dvādaśa ātmā dineśvaraḥ somaḥ śveta haye bhāti syandane śīta raśmivān himavat toya pūrṇābhiḥ bhābhiḥ āhlādayan jagat tam ṛkṣa pūga anugatam śiśirāṃśum dvijeśvaram śaśa chāyā aṅkita tanum naiśasya tamasaḥ kṣayam jyotiṣām īśvaram vyomni rasānām rasa dam prabhum oṣadhīnām sahasrāṇām nidhānam amṛtasya ca dadṛśuḥ dānavāḥ somam hima praharaṇam sthitam yaḥ prāṇaḥ sarva bhūtānām pañcadhā bhidyate nṛṣu sapta dhātu gataḥ lokān trīn dadhāra cacāra ca yam vadanti uttamam bhūtam yam vadanti aśarīriṇam yam āhuḥ ākāśa gamam śīghra gam śabda yoginam sa vāyuḥ sarva bhūta āyuḥ udbhūtaḥ svena tejasā śara bhūtāḥ divi indrāṇām ceruḥ vyātta ānanāḥ divi parvataiḥ ca śilā śṛṅgaiḥ śataśas ca eva pādapaiḥ upatasthuḥ sura gaṇāḥ prahartum dānavam balam yaḥ sa devaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ padmanābhaḥ trivikramaḥ yugānta kṛṣṇavartma ābhaḥ viśvasya jagataḥ prabhuḥ bhūmi āpaḥ vyoma bhūta ātmā śyāmaḥ śānti karaḥ ari hā ari ghnam amara ādīnām cakram gṛhya gadā dharaḥ savyena ālambya mahatīm sarva asura vināśinīm kareṇa kālīm vapuṣā śatru kāla pradām gadām dadhāra āyudha jātāni śārṅga ādīni mahā balaḥ pavana adhika saṃpātam gagana kṣobhaṇam khagam deva asura vimardeṣu bahuśas dṛṣṭa vikramam mahā indreṇa amṛtasya arthe vajreṇa kṛta lakṣaṇam śikhinam balinam ca eva tapta kuṇḍala bhūṣaṇam sphīta kroḍa avalambena śītāṃśu sama tejasā pakṣābhyām cāru patrābhyām āvṛtya divi līlayā yuga ante sa indracāpābhyām toyadābhyām iva ambaram nīla lohita pītābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam aruṇāvarajam śrīmān āruhya samare vibhuḥ suvarṇa varṇa vapuṣā suparṇam khecara uttamam tam anvayuḥ deva gaṇāḥ munayaḥ ca samāhitāḥ gīrbhiḥ parama mantrābhiḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca janārdanam tat vaiśravaṇa saṃśliṣṭam vaivasvata puraḥsaram pavana āviddha nirghoṣam saṃpradīpta hutāśanam viṣṇoḥ jiṣṇoḥ ca bhrājiṣṇoḥ tejasā tamasā āvṛtam svasti astu dānava anīke uśanāḥ vākyam ādade Purāṇa tābhyām balābhyām saṃjajñe tumulaḥ vigrahaḥ tadā surāṇām asurāṇām ca paraspara jaya eṣiṇām dānavāḥ daivataiḥ sārdham nānā praharaṇa udyatāḥ kṣipyamāṇaiḥ ca musalaiḥ saṃpatadbhiḥ ca sāyakaiḥ cāpaiḥ visphāryamāṇaiḥ ca pātyamānaiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ balibhiḥ dānavaiḥ jitakāśibhiḥ viṣaṇṇa vadanāḥ devāḥ jagmuḥ ārtim parām mṛdhe veṣṭitāḥ śara jālaiḥ ca niryatnāḥ ca asuraiḥ kṛtāḥ praviṣṭāḥ dānavīm māyām na śekuḥ te viceṣṭitum astam gatam iva ābhāti niṣprāṇa sadṛśa ākṛti balam surāṇām asuraiḥ niṣprayatna āyudham kṛtam daitya cāpa cyutān ghorān chittvā vajreṇa tān śarān te anyonyam na avabudhyanta devānām vāhanāni ca ghoreṇa tamasā āviṣṭāḥ puruhūtasya tejasā māyā pāśaiḥ vimuktāḥ tu yatnavantaḥ sura uttamāḥ vapūṃṣi daitya siṃhānām tamaḥ bhūtāni apātayan apadhvastāḥ visaṃjñāḥ ca tamasā nīla varcasā petuḥ te dānava gaṇāḥ chinna pakṣāḥ iva adrayaḥ tadā asṛjat mahā māyām mayaḥ tām tāmasīm dahan yugānta udyota jananīm sṛṣṭā āmaurveṇa vahninā sā dadāha tatas sarvān māyā maya vikalpitā daityāḥ ca āditya vapuṣaḥ sadyas uttasthuḥ āhave māyā maurvīm samāsādya dahyamānāḥ divaukasaḥ bhejire candra viṣayam śītāṃśu salila pradam te dahyamānāḥ hi aurveṇa vahninā naṣṭa cetasaḥ śaśaṃsuḥ vajriṇam devāḥ saṃtaptāḥ śaraṇa eṣiṇaḥ saṃtate māyayā sainye hanyamāne ca dānavaiḥ purā brahmarṣi jaḥ śakra tapaḥ tepe su dāruṇam ūrvaḥ sa pūrva tejasvī sadṛśaḥ brahmaṇaḥ guṇaiḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ ca eva dānavaḥ dānava īśvaraḥ ṛṣim vijñāpayāmāsuḥ purā parama tejasam ṛṣi vaṃśeṣu bhagavan chinna mūlam idam padam kaumāram vratam āsthāya kleśam eva anuvartase bahūni vipra gotrāṇi munīnām bhāvitātmanām eka dehāni tiṣṭhanti viviktāni vinā prajāḥ bhavān tu tapasā śreṣṭhaḥ prajāpāta sama dyutiḥ tatra vartasva vaṃśāya vardhaya ātmānam ātmanā jagarhe tān ṛṣi gaṇān vacanam ca idam abravīt yathā ayam vihitaḥ dharaḥ munīnām śāśvataḥ purā ārṣam vai sevataḥ karma vanya mūla phala āśinaḥ janānām vṛttayaḥ tisraḥ ye gṛha āśrama vāsinaḥ asmākam tu varam vṛttiḥ vana āśrama nivāsinām abbhakṣāḥ vāyubhakṣāḥ ca dantolūkhalinaḥ tathā aśmakuṭṭāḥ hi aśanakāḥ pañca ātapa sahāḥ ca ye brahyacaryāt brāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇa tvam vidhīyate ye sthitāḥ brahmacarye tu brāhmaṇāḥ divi saṃsthitāḥ nā asti yogam vinā siddhiḥ na vā siddhim vinā yaśaḥ na asti loke yaśaḥ mūlam brahmacaryāt param tapaḥ yaḥ nigṛhya indriya grāmam bhūta grāmam ca pañcakam kva dārāḥ kva ca saṃyogaḥ kva ca bhāva viparyayaḥ nanu iyam brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā manasā mānasī prajā yadi asti tapasaḥ vīryam yuṣmākam vidita ātmanām sṛjadhvam mānasān putrān prājāpatyena karmaṇā manasā nirmitā yoniḥ ādhātavyā tapasvibhiḥ na dāra yogaḥ bījam vā vratam uktam tapasvinām vapuḥ dīpta antarātmānam etat kṛtvā manaḥ mayam dāra yogam vinā srakṣye putram ātma tanūruham evam ātmānam ātmā me dvitīyam janayiṣyati ūrvaḥ tu tapasā āviṣṭaḥ niveśya ūrum hutāśane tasya ūrum sahasā bhittvā jvālā mālī hi anindhanaḥ jagataḥ dahana ākāṅkṣī putraḥ agniḥ samapadyata didhakṣan iva lokān trīn jajñe parama kopanaḥ utpanna mātraḥ ca uvāca pitaram kṣīṇayā girā tridiva ārohibhiḥ jvālaiḥ jṛmbhamāṇaḥ diśaḥ daśa uvāca vāryatām putraḥ jagataḥ ca dayām kuru tathyam etat vacaḥ putra śṛṇu tvam vadatām vara ūrvaḥ uvāca matim etām dadāti iha parama anugrahāya vai prabhāta kāle samprāpte kāṅkṣitavye samāgame kutra ca asya nivāsaḥ syāt bhojanam vā kimātmakam yatra aham āsa niyatam piban vāri mayam haviḥ tatas yuga ante bhūtānām eṣa ca aham ca putraka sahitau vicariṣyāvaḥ niṣputrāṇām ṛṇa apahaḥ eṣaḥ agniḥ antakāle tu salila āśī mayā kṛtaḥ dahanaḥ sarva bhūtānām sa deva asura rakṣasām evam astu iti tam saḥ agniḥ saṃvṛta jvāla maṇḍalaḥ aurvasya agneḥ prabhām jñātvā svām svām gatim upāśritāḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ dṛṣṭvā tadā tat mahat adbhutam uccais praṇata sarva aṅgaḥ vākyam etat uvāca ha tapasā te muni śreṣṭha parituṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ tat mām paśya samāpannam tava eva ārādhane ratam yadi sīdet muni śreṣṭha tava eva syāt parājayaḥ tām eva māyām gṛhṇīṣva mama putreṇa nirmitām nirindhanām agni mayīm durdharṣām pāvakaiḥ api eṣā te svasya vaṃśasya vaśagā ari vinigrahe saṃrakṣati ātma pakṣam ca vipakṣam ca pradhakṣyati jagāma tridivam hṛṣṭaḥ kṛtārthaḥ dānava īśvaraḥ eṣā durviṣahā māyā devaiḥ api durāsadā aurveṇa nirmitā pūrvam pāvakena ūrva sūnunā tasmin tu vyutthite daitye nirvīryā eṣā na saṃśayaḥ śāpaḥ hi asyāḥ purā dattaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ yena eva tejasā dīyatām me sakhā śakra toya yoniḥ niśākaraḥ tena aham saha saṃgamya yādobhiḥ ca samāvṛtaḥ māyām etām haniṣyāmi tvad prasādāt na saṃśayaḥ Purāṇa evam astu iti saṃhṛṣṭaḥ śakraḥ tridaśa vardhanaḥ saṃdideśa agratas somam yuddhāya śiśirāyudham asurāṇām vināśāya jaya artham ca divaukasām tvam mattaḥ prativīryaḥ ca jyotiṣām ca īśvara īśvaraḥ kṣaya vṛddhī tava vyakte sāgarasya iva maṇḍale loka chāyā mayam lakṣma tava aṅkaḥ śaśa saṃnibhaḥ tvam āditya pathāt ūrdhvam jyotiṣām ca upari sthitaḥ śveta bhānuḥ hima tanuḥ jyotiṣām adhipaḥ śaśī adhikṛt kāla yoga ātmā iṣṭaḥ yajña rasaḥ avyayaḥ oṣadhīśaḥ kriyāyoniḥ haraśekhara bhāj tathā śītāṃśuḥ amṛta ādhāraḥ capalaḥ śveta vāhanaḥ tvam kāntiḥ kānti vapuṣām tvam somaḥ soma pāyinām saumyaḥ tvam sarva bhūtānām timira ghnaḥ tvam ṛkṣa rāj śamaya tvā asurīm māyām yayā dahyāma saṃyuge eṣa varṣāmi śiśiram daitya māyā apakarṣaṇam etān mad śīta nirdagdhān paśya tvam hima veṣṭitān vimāyān vimadān ca eva daitya siṃhān mahā āhave iti uktvā tāraka adhīśaḥ sa jaleśaḥ śiva udakaiḥ plāvayāmāsa sainyāni surāṇām śānti vṛddhaye teṣām himakara utsṛṣṭāḥ sa pāśāḥ hima vṛṣṭayaḥ veṣṭayanti sma tān ghorān daityān megha gaṇāḥ iva
